🏅 Beginner's Guide
===================

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904)

[What is TickTick?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#what-is-ticktick%3F)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TickTick is a simple and easy-to-use time management tool. It includes modules for Tasks, Calendar, Eisenhower Matrix, Pomodoro, and Habit Tracker. You can use it to manage your work and life, achieve your goals in less time, and free yourself from the clutter of to-do lists.

Getting Started Video

iOS

Android

### [Todo List, Save Brainpower](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#todo-list%2C-save-brainpower)

Write down things in your mind, so you can have a clear understanding of the tasks you need to complete each day.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904)

### [Schedule Management, Clear at a Glance](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#schedule-management%2C-clear-at-a-glance)

You can visually view the schedules of each month and day, and no longer be confused about "what's next".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904)

### [Eisenhower Matrix, Boost Efficiency](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#eisenhower-matrix%2C-boost-efficiency)

Eisenhower Matrix can help you divide tasks into two levels of importance and urgency, helping you be more efficient.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904)

### [Efficient Focus, Rescue Procrastination](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#efficient-focus%2C-rescue-procrastination)

Start a Pomodoro timer, focusing for 25 minutes at a time to help you concentrate and get things done.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904)

### [Develop Habits, Improve Yourself](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#develop-habits%2C-improve-yourself)

The Habit Gallery has over 60 habits to choose from. Select the habits you want and set small goals for yourself!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904)

[How can I use it?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#how-can-i-use-it%3F)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Convenient and Fast Recording of Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#convenient-and-fast-recording-of-tasks)

Meet your quick recording needs anytime, anywhere:

*   Suddenly have an idea in your mind? Record it all at once using voice recording.
*   Can't handle a work email at the moment? Forward it to TickTick to make sure you don't forget.

You can quickly add tasks in many ways.

👉 [How to quickly add tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782436621254656)

### [Never Miss a Reminder Again](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#never-miss-a-reminder-again)

You can set multiple reminders for important tasks, such as your mother's birthday. Set a reminder three days in advance and another one on the day itself to make sure you don't miss it.

👉 [Effective Reminder feature](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)

### [Use Repeat Feature to Save Brain Capacity](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#use-repeat-feature-to-save-brain-capacity)

We have many tasks that need to be done regularly, such as:

*   Weekly meetings
*   Credit card payments
*   Friend's birthday

This is where the Repeat feature comes in handy. TickTick provides many time options for recurring tasks.👉 [Powerful recurring tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

[Follow TickTick](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904#follow-ticktick)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to get more application updates and time management methods, you can follow us on social media.

*   Twitter: @TickTick
*   Instagram: @TickTickApp
*   Facebook: @TickTickApp

📝 Desktop Sticky Notes
=======================

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

When we were in school, we used to organize the key points of each chapter on sticky notes and paste them at the beginning of the chapter for easy review.

When we started working, we would write our daily to-do list on sticky notes and stick them on our computer screens to remind ourselves constantly.

From student to the workplace, sticky notes have always been with us.

Our new feature "Desktop Sticky Notes" is just like the traditional sticky notes, it can be used to quickly record your fragmented information or pin important tasks on your desktop for easy follow-up and processing.

We believe that in the workplace, Desktop Sticky Notes can help you quickly record your thoughts and ideas as your preferred feature

See how to use it 👇

[Open Sticky Notes](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136#open-sticky-notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We provide two ways to open sticky notes.

### [Method 1: Open Sticky Notes on Task](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136#method-1%3A-open-sticky-notes-on-task)

You can right-click on the task and select "Open as Sticky Note", or in the task details page, click on the bottom right corner "..." - "Open as Sticky Note".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

### [Method 2: Open Sticky Notes with Hotkeys](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136#method-2%3A-open-sticky-notes-with-hotkeys)

If you want to be able to directly open the Sticky Notes feature, you just need to set a shortcut key for "New Sticky Note" to quickly add it.

**Step 1: Set Hotkeys**

Click on your profile picture - "Settings" - "Hotkeys" - "Global Actions" - "Add Sticky Note".

You can set shortcut keys according to your usage habits.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

**Step 2: Use Hotkeys to Open Sticky Notes**

After setting it up successfully, you can quickly use the shortcut keys to call up the Sticky Notes feature anytime and anywhere, such as on the desktop or in other scenarios.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

How to open Sticky Notes in bulk?

On the task list page, press the "Shift" key and click on the task range that needs to be opened in bulk. Then select "Open Sticky Notes" on the right side, and the selected tasks can be opened in bulk at once.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

How to close Sticky Notes?

You can click the close button in the upper right corner of the Sticky Note, or use the shortcut to close it.

Windows

macOS

PC: Ctrl+W

Mac: ⌘+W

[Common Operations and Tips](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136#common-operations-and-tips)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Sticky Note Settings](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136#sticky-note-settings)

You can set your preferences in the note settings, including Default Color, Font Size, Default Grid Spacing, and Restore Default Size.

Please open "Settings" - "Functions" - "Sticky Note".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

How to change the Sticky Note Color?

For opened notes, you can quickly switch their color.

Move the mouse to the top of the sticky note, click the clothes-shaped button, and select your favorite color, or you can also use color shortcut keys to switch.

Windows

macOS

Shortcut key to switch color: Ctrl+Shift+C

Shortcut key to switch color: ⇧+⌘+C

### [Pin Sticky Notes](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136#pin-sticky-notes)

When we are in a video conference or searching for information, the note stays at the forefront of the page, making it easy for us to quickly record key points.

Move the mouse to the top of the note, click the "Pin" button in the upper right corner of the note to pin it. Or use the shortcut key F12 to pin the sticky note.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

How to make newly created notes default to pinned?

Usage: Open "Settings" - "Functions" - "Sticky Note" - Enable "Pin by Default".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

### [One-click Arrangement](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136#one-click-arrangement)

If you have opened multiple notes at once, you can use the one-click arrangement function to organize them.

Steps:

1.  Click the "..." button in the lower right corner of the note - "Arrange by".
    
2.  Use the one-click arrangement shortcut key.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

One-click Arrangement shortcuts

macOS

Windows

Arrange by Top, ⌥ + ⌘+↑

Arrange by Left, ⌥ + ⌘+←

Arrange by Right, ⌥ + ⌘+→

Arrange by Top, Alt+↑

Arrange by Left, Alt+←

Arrange by Right, Alt+→

### [Single-line Sticky Note](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136#single-line-sticky-note)

When you open all the tasks of the day on sticky notes and pin them to the desktop, it takes up a lot of space. At this time, you can double-click the top of the note to turn it into a single line and freely drag it to adjust its position.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

When you need to complete a task, double-click to view the task details.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

How do I create a Sticky Note directly?

You can use a shortcut key to quickly open a Sticky Note. Set the "New Sticky Note" shortcut key in "Settings" - "Hotkeys" - "Global Action".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

How do I sync sticky notes on my phone?

Currently, the Sticky Note function is only available on the computer and cannot be opened on the mobile app.

How to disable the display of sticky notes in the Windows Status Bar?

Currently, Windows users can customize whether sticky notes are displayed in the status bar window.

To use this feature: "Settings" - "Features" - "Sticky Note" - "Not Show in the Taskbar". After enabling "Not Show in the Taskbar," you can view all opened sticky notes by pressing the "Win + Tab" shortcut.

# ⏳ Timeline View

![](data:image/svg+xml,%3csvg%20xmlns=%27http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%27%20version=%271.1%27%20width=%27210%27%20height=%2719%27/%3e)![](https://help.ticktick.com/res/article/sidebar-brand-tick.png?w=640&q=75)

⏳ Timeline View
===============

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

Timeline View is a simple visualization chart that displays all tasks in a project in the order they are scheduled. When you enable the Timeline View in a list, tasks will be displayed on a horizontal timeline.

Using the Timeline View, you can intuitively see when each task is due, where it fits in the project timeline, and quickly understand each person's progress to adjust work plans accordingly. You can also plan and schedule work and life over a longer period of time.

Now, let's see how to use it👇

[Enable Timeline View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760#enable-timeline-view)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Desktop

Mobile

Click on any "Regular List", "Folder", or "Filter", and find "..." in the upper right corner - " View" - "Timeline View" to enable it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

Click on any "List", "Folder", or "Filter", find the "..." in the upper right corner, select "View", and then select "Timeline View" to enable it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

Why can't I find "Timeline View"?

Only regular lists support switching views. Smart lists such as "Today", "Tomorrow", and "Next 7 Days" do not currently support Timeline View.

[Common Operations and Tips](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760#common-operations-and-tips)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Creating and Modifying Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760#creating-and-modifying-tasks)

Desktop

Mobile

**Create Tasks**

Adding tasks in the timeline view is very simple. You can click on a blank area to directly add a task, and the task will automatically be assigned a date based on the date you clicked on.

For example, a task added on April 2nd in the image below will automatically be set to April 2nd.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Arrange Tasks**

The Timeline View can only display tasks with assigned dates. Tasks without assigned dates will be displayed in the "Arrange Tasks" section on the right.

You can drag tasks directly into the timeline and set the date and time.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Modify Task Duration**

In the Timeline View, the length of a task represents its duration.

If you want to adjust the duration of a task, simply move your mouse to the edge of the task and drag it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Modify Task Time**

The position of a task represents its start and end time.

When you need to adjust the task time, simply click and hold the task, and drag it to the corresponding position.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

After dragging, the task will automatically correspond to the time based on where you release it.

**Create Task**

In the Timeline View, you can directly add a task by long-pressing on a blank area.

The task will automatically include the time based on the date you click.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Modify Task Duration**

The length of a task represents its duration. If you want to adjust the duration of a task, simply long press the task and drag its edge.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Modify Task Time**

The position of a task represents its time. When you need to adjust the time of a task, simply hold the task and drag it to the corresponding position.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

### [View Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760#view-tasks)

Desktop

Mobile

**Scroll to View**

Hold down the left or right mouse button and slide to move the timeline. You can view tasks for several weeks or months on the timeline.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Switch Display Ratio**

When the task time span is large, you can adjust the display ratio by clicking "Day", "Week", or " Month" in the upper right corner of the view.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Scroll to View**

Swipe left or right on the screen to move the timeline. You can view tasks for several weeks or months on the timeline.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Switch Display Ratio**

When the task time span is large, you can adjust the display ratio by clicking on "Day", "Week", or "Month" in the upper right corner of the view.

You can also pinch and zoom the time span with two fingers, or swipe outward with two fingers to shrink the time span.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

[Recommended Use Cases](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760#recommended-use-cases)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Organize Personal Work**

Set "👩🏻‍💻 Work" as a folder, and then divide routine work into several lists by category.

Assign monthly and daily tasks to different list sections to give you a clear understanding of your daily and monthly work and achieve true clarity!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Managing Complex Projects**

First, create a project list, then create a section for each team that needs to be involved in this project, and then open the timeline view to quickly understand the progress of each team's work.

For better team collaboration, you can also share this task list with the leaders of each team and assign corresponding tasks directly to them.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

**Creating Life Plans**

We can also use the timeline view to create monthly plans, review plans, wedding plans, renovation plans, and more.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

[FAQs](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760#faqs)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

Can the Timeline View on mobile devices support landscape mode?

Yes, simply rotate your phone to landscape mode.

How can I change the color of task blocks in the view?

In the Timeline View, click on "..." in the upper right corner and select "View Options" to set the color of task blocks.

Two-Step Verification

🌮️ Widgets
===========

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

TickTick has prepared a variety of stylish and practical widgets that not only enhance your phone's aesthetics but also help you improve efficiency!

Let's take a look at various task, calendar, focus, and habit widgets together!👇

[Widgets](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752#widgets)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

iOS

Android

macOS

Windows

**Lock Screen Widget**

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

How to add "Lock Screen Widget"

> iOS system needs to be upgraded to iOS 16, and TickTick needs to be updated to version 6360 or above.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

1.  When in lock screen mode, long press the screen to enter the settings mode, and click "Customize".
2.  Click "Add Widget" in the middle of the screen and find "TickTick".
3.  Select the desired widget type and tap or drag to add it.

**Widgets**

TickTick has prepared exclusive widgets for various features, which can be added to the mobile screen to easily improve efficiency.

**1\. Tasks**

We provide 3 types of widgets: "Tasks", "Task Completion Statistics", and "Add Task".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   "Tasks": You can view and access the task list to understand daily task arrangements.
*   "Task Completions": You can view the number of tasks completed each day in the past 30 days.
*   "Add Task": You can quickly open the app to add tasks.

**2\. Calendar**

We offer three types of widgets: "Today's Calendar," "Daily View," and "Monthly Calendar View."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   "Today's Calendar": You can view the "Monthly Calendar" and "Today's Tasks," and click on tasks to quickly access the "Today" smart list.
    
*   "Daily View": You can see your upcoming task schedule in real-time, quickly locate your current task, and efficiently focus on completing it.
    
*   "Monthly Calendar View": All events for the month are displayed at a glance, making it easy to see when you are busy and when you are free.
    

**3\. Eisenhower Matrix**

You can view your tasks in the Eisenhower Matrix and focus more energy on Important and Urgent matters.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

**4\. Habits**

We provide three widgets: "Today Habits," "Weekly Habits," and "Habit Heat Map."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   "Today Habits": You can easily see the habits you need to develop each day and cultivate good habits more purposefully.
*   "Weekly Habits": You can check the progress of the habits you need to check in for the week, making it easier to track your completion.
*   "Habit Heat Map": You can easily track the completion status of each day of the month and the progress of the entire month, helping you develop good habits.

**5\. Pomodoro Focus**

We provide two widgets: "Today Focus" and "Focus Distribution."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   "Today Focus": You can view your daily focus time, manage your time, and improve efficiency.
*   "Focus Distribution": You can quickly view the duration of focus time for each day of the week, helping you better allocate time and review your week's schedule.

**6\. Countdown**

We offer a "Countdown" widget that lets you pin important dates to your home screen.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/b2790f6adf6ba5caef793ed41c21b6b4.png)

**Control Center Controls**

The 'Control Center Component Library' has been newly introduced in iOS 18. TickTick offers 8 controls within this feature: Add Task, Today’s Tasks, Pomodoro, Stopwatch, Open Calendar, Open Matrix, Open Focus, and Open Habit.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/cf946a35a0e94e74b9c99ea41e4d4cc2.png)

> With these controls, you can quickly activate Focus Mode or jump directly to specific pages.

How to add control？

Swipe down to open the Control Center, click the "+" icon in the top corner to enter edit mode, then scroll to the bottom and tap "Add Control." Find "TickTick" from the list, and you can add TickTick controls.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

How to adjust control size？

Simply drag the bottom-right corner of the control to resize it.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/6650bb1fb1d45c528c0ab09a62d2e9d1.gif)

**Apple Watch Widgets**

You can now add task and habit widgets to your Apple Watch face for easy tracking and management.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

How to Add Apple Watch Widgets:

1.  Open the Watch app on your iPhone,go to “My Watch" settings.
2.  Under "Complications," select the area where you want to add the widget. 3.Find and choose the "TickTick" widget.

Both task and habit widgets on the watch face and Smart Stack support one-tap completion for quick task management!

**1\. Tasks**

We provide two widgets: "Tasks" and "Task Completions".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   **"Tasks"**: You can view and access the task list to understand daily task arrangements.
*   **"Task Completions"**: You can view the number of tasks completed each day in the last 30 days.

**2\. Calendar**

We provide three widgets: "Timeline", "Week", and "Month".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   "Daily View": You can see your recent task schedule in real time, quickly locate your current task, and efficiently focus on completing it. P.S. You can switch between "Day" and "3-Day" views as desired.
    
*   "Weekly View": You can view and access your tasks for the week, and proceed with your weekly plan in an orderly manner.
    
*   "Monthly View": All your activities for the month are presented instantly, making it easy to glance and know when you are busy or free.
    

**3\. Eisenhower Matrix**

*   You can view your tasks in the Eisenhower Matrix and focus more energy on Important and Urgent matters.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

**4\. Habits**

We offer three widgets: "Today Habits," "Weekly Habits," and "Habit Heat Map."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   Today Habits: You can easily view the habits to develop each day and cultivate good habits with more purpose.
*   Weekly Habits: You can check the progress of the habits to complete this week and easily track their completion.
*   Habit Heat Map: You can easily track the completion status of each day in the current month and the progress of the whole month, which helps you develop good habits.

**5\. Pomodoro**

We offer three widgets: "Pomodoro," "Today Focus," and "Focus Distribution."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   Pomodoro: You can start focusing on the screen and concentrate on what needs to be done at the moment.
*   Today Focus: You can view your daily focus time, manage your time, and improve efficiency.
*   Focus Distribution: You can quickly check the duration of your focus time each day within the week, which can help you better review and allocate your time for the week.

We offer five different widgets: "Tasks," "Eisenhower Matrix," "Today Habits," "Daily View," and "Monthly Calendar View."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   Daily View: You can view "Monthly Calendar" and "Today's Tasks".
*   Eisenhower Matrix: You can view your tasks in the Eisenhower Matrix and focus more energy on important and urgent matters.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   Monthly Calendar View: All the events of the month are instantly displayed, so you can easily scan to know when you are busy and when you are free.
*   Tasks: You can view and access your task list to understand your daily task arrangements.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   Today Habits: You can see your recent task arrangements in real-time, quickly locate yourcurrent task, and efficiently focus on completing it.

We provide six different widgets: Tasks, Calendar, Eisenhower Matrix, Habits, Countdowns, and Pomodoro.

*   Tasks: You can view and access your task list to understand your daily task arrangements.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   Calendar: You can easily view your schedule in the calendar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   Eisenhower Matrix: You can view your tasks in the Eisenhower Matrix and focus more energy on Important and Urgent matters.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   Pomodoro Focus: You can start focusing on what needs to be done on your desktop.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

*   Habits: View your habits and complete check-ins directly from the widget to track your daily progress.
    
*   Countdowns: See the remaining days until important dates and keep track of upcoming anniversaries.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

[How to add widgets?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752#how-to-add-widgets%3F)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iOS

Android

macOS

Windows

**Add Lock Screen Widgets**

> iOS system needs to be upgraded to iOS 16, and TickTick needs to be updated to version 6.3.60 or above.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

1.  Under lock screen mode, long press the screen to enter the setting mode and click "Customize".
2.  Click "Add Widgets" in the middle of the screen and find "TickTick".
3.  Select the desired widget type, click or drag to add it.

> If you cannot find TickTick in the lock screen widget list, you can try the following two methods: 1. If you have just upgraded the app, please reopen the app and then add it again. 2. If you still cannot find it, restart your phone and then add it (or switch the language in "Settings" - "General" - "Language and Region" to achieve a quick restart).

**Widgets**

To add the TickTick widget on iOS 15 or later, long press the screen and tap the "+" in the top left corner, search for TickTick, and then select the widget you need.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

As each Android phone brand has a different way of "adding widgets," you can find the corresponding method below according to your phone brand.

**Google Pixel**

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

1.  Long press the blank space on the screen and tap "Widget".
2.  Find "TickTick" and select the widget you want.
3.  Add the widget.

**Samsung**

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

1.  Long press on a blank space on the screen or pinch the screen with two fingers to enter the desktop editing mode, then click on "Widget" at the bottom.
    
2.  Search for "TickTick" and select the desired widget.
    
3.  Click "Add" to add it.
    

Click the time in the top right corner of your desktop, slide to the bottom and click "Edit widget", search for TickTick and select the widget you need.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

Add a desktop widget by right-clicking the TickTick icon in the taskbar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

Why doesn't the iOS widget support completing tasks by clicking?

After iOS 13, due to limitations in the iOS system, it is not possible to complete tasks with one click.

How to edit widgets?

Long press the widget to configure the "Theme", "View", "Auto Dark Mode", and more.

How to place TickTick widgets on the desktop on Mac?

As of macOS 14.0, it is now possible to place TickTick widgets on the desktop with interactive support. To do this, ensure that your system is updated to macOS 14.0 and, while editing the widget, simply drag and drop it onto the desktop.

Why doesn't Android have a Daily View?

You can long press the widget, select " Edit Widget", and enter "Widget Settings" to set it up.

Are there any Eisenhower Matrix widgets?

We already support Eisenhower Matrix widgets. You can swipe left to find them.

💻 Cross-Platform Support

🕐 Smart Recognition
====================

TickTick provides Smart Recognition to help you create tasks quickly, set reminders and sort tasks easily.

[Turn on Smart Recognition](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080#turn-on-smart-recognition)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Go to 'Settings', tap on 'General', find 'Smart Recognition' and switch it on.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

Click on "Avatar", select "Settings", find "Smart Recognition" and turn it on.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

[Date recognition](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080#date-recognition)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Automatically recognise the date and time information in tasks and set reminders when creating tasks via Quick Add, voice input etc.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

You can also customise whether the date is removed from the task text or not.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

### [Date and time](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080#date-and-time)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

When you enter an ambiguous date in the list, the TickTick will be uniformly recognised as the most recent valid date and time. For example: the current actual time is 4pm, when you enter "remind me at 9pm" it will be recognised as 9pm today)

### [Repeat](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080#repeat)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

### [Early reminder](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080#early-reminder)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

### [Postponed reminder](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080#postponed-reminder)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

📔 Notes and Summary
====================

[Notes](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#notes)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

The Note feature is, minimalistic, lightweight, and user-friendly. You can use it to collect information anytime, anywhere, save inspiration and reminders, and deeply integrate with your to-do list and schedule. You can also combine "Templates" and "Summary" to intelligently generate weekly reports, efficiently review, and save a lot of time without realizing it.

### What are the applicable scenarios for note-taking?

Here are a few common application scenarios for your reference:

*   📝 "Subject Materials" - set up a separate list to store materials for a particular course.
*   📝 "Daily Summary" - can be mixed with to-do tasks to record observations and insights of the day.
*   📝 "Work Review" - combined with powerful task summary, track progress and gains and losses in work.

### [Create a Note List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#create-a-note-list)

Mobile

Desktop

Click "Add" - "List" in the sidebar - click "More" - select "Note" in the "List Type" column to create a note list.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

Click the "Add List" option in the sidebar, and then select "Note List" in the "List Type" column to successfully add a note list.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

### [Add Notes](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#add-notes)

Mobile

Desktop

In the "Note List", click the add button in the lower right corner to directly add notes.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

Then you can freely write in the note interface. You can use the style menu above the keyboard to set styles such as bold and highlight for the content.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

On this basis, you can also add dates, reminders, tags, and templates to the notes, making it as convenient as managing tasks.

In the "Note List", click the "input box" to edit the note name and press the "Enter" key to directly add the note.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

### [Managing Notes with Kanban View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#managing-notes-with-kanban-view)

**Note Classification**

Mobile

Desktop

To better manage your notes by category, you can click the "..." button in the upper right corner, select "View", and switch to "Kanban View" to classify and group the notes by category.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

To better manage your notes by category, you can click on the top right corner of the list "..." - View" - "Kanban View", and Set up groups by category.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

**Custom Sorting**

Mobile

Desktop

You can freely adjust the order of both groups and notes in the list to better classify and manage your notes.

To adjust the sorting of sections, simply click on the "..." button in the top right corner of the list and select "Manage Section". Then, long press on the "≡" icon on the right side of the section and drag it to customize the sorting of the sections.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

And to change the note sorting, just long press and drag the notes to the corresponding position.

Sections and tasks can be freely dragged and dropped to define their sorting.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

### [Efficient Note-Taking with Templates](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#efficient-note-taking-with-templates)

Want to take notes more efficiently? Don't miss out on the treasure trove of "Templates".

You can save a series of commonly used processes as templates, making them standardized and fixed, such as reading notes, meeting minutes, weekly work summaries, etc. When you need to use them again, you don't need to manually enter them, just call them up with one click.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

Mobile

Desktop

Go to the note details page and click "Use a Template". We have prepared three preset templates for you: simply select one to automatically add it to your notes.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

Click on the "⌄" icon on the right side of the input box and select "Add from Template". Select any template and it will be automatically added to your notes.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

> You can also manage existing note templates in "Settings" - "Template" - "Note Template".

You can also continuously optimize according to your own needs and customize new templates.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

### [FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#faq)

What is the relationship between notes and tasks?

Tasks and notes are parallel relationships. In addition to creating task lists (as you are familiar with), you can also create dedicated note lists. The main differences are as follows:

*   ✅ **"Task":** Can be checked off when completed, used for time management, goal breakdown, project management, etc.
    
*   📃 **"Note":** Does not have a concept of completion, used for taking notes, reflecting and summarizing, storing knowledge, etc.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

How to convert a task into a note?

Mobile

Desktop

Go to the task details page, click the "..." icon in the upper right corner, and select "Convert to Note" to convert the current task into a note.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

Go to the task details page, click the "..." icon in the lower right corner, and select "Convert to Note" to convert the current task into a note.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

> Tasks converted to notes do not automatically go to the notes list, they remain in the original list and tasks with subtasks cannot be converted to notes.

[Summary](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#summary)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

Still struggling with daily and weekly reports? Use the "Summary" feature to make your work easier and more efficient, in combination with the note-taking function.The "Summary" of TickTick can help you understand and summarize the completion status of tasks over a period of time, and generate editable text that you can directly add to note pages or copy to other platforms.

### [Display Summary](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#display-summary)

Mobile

Desktop

Click the "+" icon in the note list to create a new note, enter the note title and click on the note description area below, then click the "Summary Preview" icon in the image.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

Click on the avatar in the upper left corner of the page, enter "Settings" - "Functions" - "Smart Lists" - "Summary", and change the summary status to "Show". After that, the "Summary" will appear at the top of the left sidebar.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/471cfdad03cf845230b8a683d94216f7.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ef7160837cfad8ecf9b61d4c16a910d3.png)

### [Insert Summary](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#insert-summary)

Click on the note description area, select the summary icon in the middle, and enter the task summary preview page. Click Insert to add.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

> Note: We support displaying focus data and completion status for multi-level tasks in the summary, and have added various sorting rules. Please note that only "Notes" on mobile devices support adding summaries.

### [Set Content and Format](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#set-content-and-format)

You can use our provided functions to quickly set the content and format to insert into the summary.

Mobile

Desktop

*   Time Range: You can choose to insert tasks within which time range;

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

*   Filter: Filter by list, tag, and assignee;

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

*   Sort: Set the sorting method for tasks;

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

*   Items to Show: Or set to display more information such as "Completion date" and "Progress";

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

Finally, click "Insert" to insert the summary content into the note.

You can filter tasks by **Date, Lists**, or **Status**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/6ee220f5ab58f9c567f17b4e9a6676d8.png)

Under **More**, you can also filter by **Priority**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/b00356aa6cc871df983526eca7c2e58c.png)

In **Display Options**, you can:

*   Choose how to Grouping (e.g., by completion status or list).

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5fb8d419387a32086f7099d1ae6ab6b6.png)

*   Customize what information to Fields (e.g., status, progress, tag.).

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/fa309ae21d5788be3f2248960a44e8d3.png)

**Save as Template**

Once you’ve configured your filters, you can save them as a template for quick access next time. Tap the **“+”** button below the template section to create a new one.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/580235e5f9d945dfdd8f9b2f4f3e359d.png)

### [Exporting Summary](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304#exporting-summary)

Mobile

Desktop

If you need to export a summary, you can click on the "..." in the upper right corner of the note and select "Share" to export the summary in text or image format.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

Open "Summary" in the left sidebar, after confirming the filtering conditions, click "Save As" to choose the preferred export style.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/acd3e30d07a2014d4e9e36c47c16d069.png)

⌨️ Desktop Shortcuts
====================

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776)

Use keyboard shortcuts and command menus to perform in-app operations without a mouse, increasing efficiency.

[Command Menu](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776#command-menu)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use ⌘+K or Ctrl+K to open the "Command Menu," enter a name, and easily navigate to various functional modules within the app.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776)

> Mac application does not currently support this feature.

[Keyboard Shortcuts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776#keyboard-shortcuts)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use a single key or combination of keys on the keyboard to complete an operation, saving time and freeing up the mouse.

You can enter "?" to conveniently view the shortcut key list.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

### [How to Modify Shortcuts?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776#how-to-modify-shortcuts%3F)

*   You can modify them in the shortcut interface in the Settings.
*   You can modify them in the shortcut interface in the sidebar.
*   You can modify them by opening the shortcut interface in the "Command Menu" - "Help" - "Show Shortcuts".

> Shortcuts displayed in gray cannot be modified.

✅ Task
======

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782436621254656)

In daily life, we often forget important information and feel overwhelmed. Is there a simple and intuitive method to help us manage our lives?

Hand it over to "TickTick" 👇

*   Create tasks one by one for things you want or need to do, reducing the pressure on your brain to remember. 👉 [Add tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)
    
*   If you're afraid of forgetting important dates, set reminders for them so you won't miss them. 👉 [Add reminders to tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)
    
*   For tasks that are fixed in time, such as weekly reports or rent payments, set them as recurring tasks to solve them all at once. 👉 [Set recurring tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)
    
*   In the process of constantly completing tasks, we can accumulate confidence in our own abilities and enjoy the pleasure of continuous improvement. Live with intention and achieve more ❤️.
    

🚀 What's New

Add Tasks

![](data:image/svg+xml,%3csvg%20xmlns=%27http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%27%20version=%271.1%27%20width=%27210%27%20height=%2719%27/%3e)![](https://help.ticktick.com/res/article/sidebar-brand-tick.png?w=640&q=75)

🎯 Eisenhower Matrix
====================

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782071033135104)

Have you ever encountered this situation?

Every day is very busy, and you feel like there is not enough time, but looking back, you find that you are doing things that are not that important? Or maybe you have long-term goals, but you have been procrastinating without making progress?

At this time, using our "Eisenhower Matrix" function may help you focus more on important and urgent work:

Eisenhower Matrix is a popular and effective time management method: based on the two dimensions of importance and urgency, all tasks are placed in the four matrixs, and then processed according to the principles of each matrix. 👉 [How to use Eisenhower Matrix](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864)

We have prepared the commonly used rules for the Eisenhower Matrix for you, and you can also customize the rules according to your own needs. From now on, all tasks will be automatically classified into the four matrixs based on the rules you set. 👉 [How to edit the rules for Eisenhower Matrix](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

💡 Want to go deeper? Check out our article: [Master Task Prioritization with the Eisenhower Matrix](https://ticktick.com/resources/article/7310113943366664192/eisenhower-matrix)

FAQ - Calendar

How to Use Eisenhower Matrix

🍅 Pomodoro
===========

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782025193586688)

The Pomodoro Technique is a simple and effective time management method, which was proposed by an Italian, Francesco Cirillo, in 1992.

> The reason why it is named "Pomodoro" is simply because the timer he used during university was shaped like a tomato.

The principle of the Pomodoro Technique is to divide time into several "Pomodoro timers", with each focused on for 25 minutes, followed by a 5-minute break. Completing 4 Pomodoro timers allows you to take a longer break.

Some people may ask, that's it? Will it really be effective? The answer is yes, because:

1.  The brain cannot process multiple things at the same time.
2.  The brain's sustained attention time is limited, and it is difficult for us to maintain high concentration for more than half an hour.

The core of the Pomodoro Technique is to create a sense of ritual that guides you to quickly enter a state of concentration and maintain focus during this time until the Pomodoro timer ends. Due to its short duration, it is easy for you to stick with it, and the sense of achievement from completing a Pomodoro session will give you positive feedback, which in turn motivates you to persevere and achieve more difficult goals.

[👉 How to start Focus?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

[👉 How to maintain Focus?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

💡 Want to go deeper? Check out our article: [The Pomodoro Technique: What, Why, and How](https://ticktick.com/resources/article/7310136858346782720/pomodoro-technique)

How to Edit the Rules for Eisenhower Matrix

How to Start Focus?

⏰ Habit Tracker
===============

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781896457814016)

We want to develop some habits because they can bring about change and help us grow into better versions of ourselves.

However, developing habits is not an easy task:

*   We always find it difficult to start a habit due to procrastination or fear of difficulty.
*   We also find it difficult to stick to a habit because we often fall into a period of fatigue.

According to the book _Mini Habit_, in order to make this process simple and easy to operate, we can set it up to be super simple, so simple that you can't find any excuse not to do it:

*   If you want to develop the habit of "reading," then try setting it as "reading 2 pages a day."
*   If you want to develop the habit of "exercising," then try "doing 2 push-ups a day."
*   If you want to develop the habit of "memorizing vocabulary," then try "memorizing 1 page of vocabulary a day."

We also provide flexible check-in methods and data reviews to help you develop habits better.

👉 [Start sticking to a habit](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296)

👉 [Better achieve habits](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

👉 [Review habit completion status](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320)

💡 Want to go deeper? Check out our article: [Master Habit Formation for Better Mental Health](https://ticktick.com/resources/article/7310117703971241984/habit-stick)

Focus Statistics

Start a New Habit

💎 Design Principles
====================

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054327235582361600)

How to create an app loved by millions of users worldwide? This is not a simple question.

### [Only Classic Design Can Transcend Time](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054327235582361600#only-classic-design-can-transcend-time)

Those familiar with efficiency apps may notice that our app is different from others, with a major difference being the presentation of task details.

Many apps put a lot of functional buttons on the task details page, which looks rich. But in our opinion, this is not good design, because these functions are not necessary for users.

So we boldly subtracted and only left the most essential functions, leaving more space for users to write. Because we believe that only simple design can approach classics, transcend time, and withstand the test of time.

In addition to simplicity, we also strive to meet users' intuition in many designs.

In real life, we can pick up an object and place it in different positions. In our app, you can also adjust the position of tasks by long-pressing and dragging, whether in the task list, calendar, or Eisenhower Matrix.

All of these operations are so natural that you don't even realize they are our design.

### [Befriend Users Without Disturbing Them](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054327235582361600#befriend-users-without-disturbing-them)

In our view, when users use our app, they are to some extent having a conversation with us. We hope that our relationship with users is not that of customers or traffic, but more like friends.

Because when users record their things in our app, it is a kind of trust in us. So we hope that in the eyes of users, we are a kind, honest, and trustworthy image.

This is why we don't have "splash ads," even though it can bring us considerable revenue. We also maintain the rare "restraint" in this industry, without unremovable red dots and dazzling marketing activities.

In the interaction with users, users will also inadvertently feel our intentions. Here's a small example.

"Do you think 12:30 AM is midnight or noon?"

When asked this question, many people are confused, but in fact, in the 12-hour format, 12:30 AM is actually early morning. So when users choose 12:30 AM, we will have a small prompt to avoid them selecting the wrong time.

And there are actually many designs like this in our app.

### [Help Users Manage Everything in Life](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054327235582361600#help-users-manage-everything-in-life)

We now have nearly 20 million users worldwide, and the earliest users of our product have been with us for 9 years.

From the initial Task and Reminder features to the later Calendar function, Pomodoro, Habit Tracker, and Eisenhower Matrix.

We are very grateful to these users. It is because of their support that we can continuously improve and refine our app. At the same time, it also allows us to more deeply understand that "what users need is not just task management, but everything in their lives."

Of course, at the same time, a new issue has been placed in front of us:

How to balance powerful features and ease of use while meeting the needs of more users?

Our answer is to respect the user's power of choice.

In our app, users can choose which features they need and which ones they don't, based on their preferences. Users can also adjust the order of features and even hide less frequently used ones behind a "More" button.

### [Final Thoughts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054327235582361600#final-thoughts)

Finally, thank you so much for reading, and we hope our app can help you lead a mindful life and achieve more.

🔍 FAQ
======

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

[🔥 Hot Topics](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672#%F0%9F%94%A5-hot-topics)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How to back up data?

You can log in to the web version to back up your data.

*   Log in to your account - Click on the "Avatar" in the upper left corner - "Settings", then click on "Backup & Restore" in the left sidebar - "Generate Backup" to save your data backup on the desktop.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

How to merge account data?

If you want to merge the data of two accounts, you can first back up the data of one account, and then import the backed up data into another account.

1.  Back up data: Log in to the Web version, click on Avatar - "Settings" - "Account" - "Backup & Restore" - "Generate Backup" to save the backup data.
2.  Import Backup: Log in to the account that needs to import data on the Web end, click on the Avatar - "Settings", click on "Backup & Restore" - "Import Backup" to complete the merge.

How to add pictures or attachments to tasks?

TickTick supports adding pictures and attachments to tasks. After the attachment is uploaded successfully, it will be automatically synchronized to various platforms. The size limit for each picture or attachment uploaded by a regular user is 10 MB, and for a premium member it is 20 MB.

> Premium members can upload up to 99 attachments or pictures per day, while regular users are limited to 1 upload per day.

Mobile

Desktop

Click on the task - upper right corner "..." - "Attachment" to add pictures or attachments.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

*   Option 1: Click on the task, then click on the "···" icon on the bottom right corner and select "Upload Attachment" to add an attachment.
*   Option 2: Use the copy and paste shortcut keys (Ctrl + C / Ctrl + V) to directly add an image to the task details page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

How to connect TickTick with your smartwatch?

iOS

WearOS

Download and install TickTick on your phone. It will sync and display on your smartwatch.

Download TickTick from Google Play on both your phone and smartwatch, then log in to your TickTick account on your phone. You will be able to use TickTick directly on your smartwatch.

> Versions below WearOS 2.5 are not supported.

How to view Habit and Focus records in the calendar?

Mobile

Desktop

In the calendar view, click on "..." in the upper right corner and select "View Options" to enable "Show Habit" and "Show Focus Records" to view the records in the calendar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

In the calendar view, click "View Options" on the right side, and enable "Show Habit" and "Show Focus Records" to view records in the calendar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

Does TickTick offer Educational Discounts?

We always believe that education can bring positive changes to individuals and the world, and we hope to help more students and educators manage their studies, lives, challenges, and goals. Therefore, we have introduced an educational discount: students and educators can enjoy a 25% discount on TickTick Premium. You can register with an educational email, or switch your current account to your educational email and then apply. For specific steps and details, please click [Educational Discount](https://ticktick.com/education)
 to view.

What if I am not reminded when an task is due??

Android

iOS

Since Android security services and third-party security applications may affect the alerting feature of Tick List, please check first according to the following steps:

1.  Has TickTick been granted notification permission? Please make sure that TickTick has been granted notification permission, otherwise TickTick will not alert you properly.
2.  Does the phone system come with security service? If so, please allow TickTick to auto-start itself and keep it running in the background while in standby.
3.  Is there a third-party security application installed? If so, please make sure that TickTick is whitelisted and memory accelerated in each security app. You can also click "Settings" - "Sounds & Notifications" - "Reminders not working?" in the app. to see more solutions on that page.

Please first confirm whether the notifications for TickTick has been allowed in the system settings. The specific steps are: Tap "Settings" in the phone system - "Notifications" - "TickTick" to view the notification status.

How to set the start day of the week?

Go to "Settings" - "Date & Time" - "Week Start on", where you can select "Sunday", "Monday", or "Saturday", as the start of the week.

How is the Achievement Score calculated?

The Achievement Score is related to your daily use of TickTick, such as creating tasks, completing tasks, focusing, and habit tracking. Adding and completing tasks will increase the achievement scores; As the achievement scores increase, your level in TickTick will also be boosted up.

The achievement level can also be exchanged for exclusive themes👇

Need an invoice for your TickTick Premium purchase? No problem!

For the purchase made via TickTick web, we have prioritized our invoice issuing mechanism and make it automatic. Now, you can easily download your invoices by following the steps:

*   **Web (PayPal)**

1.  Click the **personal profile** at the top left and select **Settings**.
2.  Click on the **Premium Account** tab.
3.  In the **Latest Order** section, click the **More** button, and you will go to the receipt history page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

4.  Update and confirm your billing information first in the **Billing Info** section before invoicing.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

1.  Find the exact invoice you require, and click **invoice**.
2.  **Download** or **print** the invoice PDF.

*   **App Store & Google Play**

 are only available via the web app.

If you subscribed to a TickTick Premium via Google Play or App Store. Please follow the instructions below to get an invoice.

(App Store)

  (Google)

> Refunded orders do not support invoice issuance.

How can I change my payment method or platform?

If you only need to update your payment card, you can do so directly on your payment platform (for example, Google Play or Apple App Store).

If your subscription is billed through Stripe, please contact us and we’ll help you update your card information.

If you wish to **switch payment platforms** (e.g., from Stripe to Google), please note that this is **not supported**. You’ll need to cancel your current subscription and re-subscribe using your preferred platform.

However, please be aware that canceling may result in a **higher renewal price** if the plan price has increased, so we recommend keeping your current subscription unless necessary.

How do I buy and use a TickTick gift card?

Time is the most valuable gift of all. Buy a gift card for someone else or for yourself, enjoy a year of premium, and live each day to the fullest.

You can purchase gift cards on our website 👉 [Gift Cards - TickTick](https://ticktick.com/card)

*   How do I redeem a gift card for a membership?

The redemption code in the gift card email can be redeemed for a premium. You can redeem it through the following ways:

1.  Email: Copy the redemption code - Click "Redeem in TickTick" - "Redeem" page - Enter the redemption code.
    
2.  Android: Go to "Settings" page - "Upgrade to Premium Account" - "Redeem" at the bottom of the page - Enter the redemption code.
    
3.  Web: Click "Avatar" - "Settings" - "Premium" - "Redeem" - enter the redemption code.
    

Once the redemption is activated successfully, the membership benefits will take effect immediately.

How to cancel auto-renewal or subscription on iOS?

Due to official restrictions on the Apple platform, developers are not authorized to cancel subscriptions, and users need to make changes themselves. If you need to cancel a subscription, you can follow these steps:

1.  Go to App Store and click on the Apple ID avatar;
2.  Click on "Subscriptions" on the "Account" page;
3.  In "Subscriptions", click on the subscription you want to manage, and click "Cancel Subscription".

How to purchase premium for the entire team?

Purchase gift cards for team members and use the redemption code to redeem premium membership.

You can purchase gift cards on TickTick official website [Gift Cards - TickTick](https://ticktick.com/card)
. Select the quantity you want to purchase, "Send the card(s) to me/Group Buying" - then receive the redemption code in the email.

What are the different levels of task management?

TickTick has a clear hierarchy for tasks: "Folder" - "List" - "Section" - "Task" - "Subtask," which can help you efficiently manage your tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

*   Folder: Folders are commonly used to manage lists. If you have a large number of similar lists, such as meetings, reports, and business trips, you can create a "Work" folder to organize them.
*   List: Lists can be used to categorize and organize tasks. You can create common lists based on your personal life and work schedule and put similar tasks in the same list. In addition, regular lists can be shared and collaborated on with others.
*   Task: Tasks are the basic level for schedule management.
*   Subtask: Subtasks are a level lower than tasks, and tasks can be split into several subtasks to achieve them one by one.

Can I bulk edit or delete tasks?

TickTick supports batch editing of tasks, which allows you to modify the date, priority, list, tags, or complete, merge, delete, and share all tasks in batches.

If you have a lot of tasks that need the same operation, you can use batch editing to complete them.

Mobile

Desktop

Click the "···" button in the upper right corner of the task list "Select". Then select the tasks you want to edit and modify them in batches.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

On the task list page, hold down the "Ctrl" or "Shift" key (for macOS, the "Command" key), select multiple tasks with the mouse, and then right-click to batch edit them.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

How to add images or attachments to tasks?

TickTick supports adding images and attachments to tasks. After the attachment is uploaded successfully, it will be automatically synchronized to all platforms. The size limit for each image or attachment is 10 MB for regular users and 20 MB for premium members.

> Premium members can upload up to 99 attachments or images per day, while regular users are limited to one upload per day. Up to 20 attachments can be uploaded per task.

Mobile

Desktop

Click on the image icon in the lower left corner of the task to add an image; click "..." - "Attachment" in the upper right corner to add an image or other attachment.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

*   Option 1: Click on the task - click on the "···" button on the bottom right - "Upload Attachment" to add attachments;
*   Option 2: Copy and paste (Ctrl + C / Ctrl + V) to directly add images to the task details page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

What should I do if I am not reminded when a task is due?

iOS

Android

If you are an iOS user, please check your system settings first to make sure that you have allowed the TickTick reminder notification.

Click "Settings" - "Notifications" - "TickTick" in your phone system and check the notification status.

As Android system security service and third-party security applications may affect the reminder function of TickTick.

If you are an Android user, please check the following steps first:

1.  Has TickTick already got the notification permission? Please make sure that TickTick has been granted notification permission, otherwise If not, you will not be alerted properly.
2.  Does the phone system have its own security service? If so, please allow TickTick to start itself and keep it running in the background.
3.  Do you have a third-party security application installed? If so, please make sure that TickTick is added to the startup whitelist and memory acceleration whitelist in every security software. You can also click "Settings" - "Sounds & Notifications" - "Reminders not working? to see more solutions on that page.

> If the above method still doesn't solve the issue, please click "Settings" - "Feedback" in TickTick. Submit your feedback to us, and we will deal with it as soon as possible.

How to adjust the timeline in the calendar view?

In the TickTick calendar view, the timeline covers the entire day, but the "00:00-07:00" and "21:00-00:00" time periods are hidden by default.

Mobile

Desktop

*   Expand time period: Click on the two time periods to expand the hidden time periods.
*   Adjust time period: With all time periods expanded, you can adjust the hidden time periods by dragging the timeline bar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

*   Expand time period: Click on the two time periods to expand the hidden time periods.
*   Adjust time period: With all time periods expanded, you can adjust the hidden time periods by dragging the timeline bar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

Why can't I check off a recurring task in the calendar view?

Currently, in TickTick, you cannot modify future recurring tasks until the current recurrence is completed. Therefore, you need to handle the previous recurring tasks. Here's how you can do it:

1.  If the task is already completed, you can check it off by clicking on the recurring task in the previous period.
2.  If the task is not completed, you can swipe right on the recurring task in the "List" or "Month" view of the calendar, and then click "Skip this Recurrence" in the date popup.

What calendars does TickTick support subscribing to?

TickTick supports calendars such as Google, Outlook, iCloud, and more.

To learn more, you can read this article 👉[Subscribing to Third-Party Calendars in TickTick](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781614550253568)

[🤝 Collaborate](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672#%F0%9F%A4%9D-collaborate)

How to share a list with others?

TickTick not only helps you manage your personal affairs, but also allows you to collaborate and share with others. Share the list with other members, and all members can view, edit, add and delete tasks in the list.

Mobile

Desktop

To enter the task list page of a certain list, click on "···" in the upper right corner and select "Share" to invite new members.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

There are three ways to invite new members:

*   Contact invitation: Enter the email or name of the contact and press enter to send an invitation. If the email address has not registered with Dida365, they can activate sharing by clicking on the link in the email. You can also select one or more contacts from the recently invited and team members list to invite.
*   Link invitation: Click to create a sharing link that can be copied and sent to others. If other members confirm joining the list, you will receive a notification to approve the request. After you confirm, the member can then share the list.

> Both invitation methods can set permissions for the invitee, with permissions divided into three levels: commentable, read-only, and editable.

On the list page, click the "..." button in the upper right corner and select "Share" to invite new members.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

There are two ways to invite new members:

*   Contact invitation: Enter the contact's email or name and press Enter to send an invitation. If the email has not registered for TickTick, they can activate the sharing by clicking on the link in the email. You can also select one or more contacts from the recently invited and team members displayed.
*   Shared Link Invitation: Click to create a shared link, which can be copied and sent to others. If other members confirm joining the list, you will receive a notification requesting to join. After you confirm your agreement, the member can share this list.

> Users who join the shared list can edit the content of the list. The list sharer's username can be seen in the list editing interface or the sharing interface.

Do all members of the shared list need to be premium members?

No. Both premium and free users can share and join shared lists, but premium users can add up to 29 members to each shared list, while free users can only add one shared member to their shared lists.

How can I assign tasks to others?

Any member of the shared list can assign tasks to the executor. The member will receive a notification reminder in the "Notifications".

Mobile

Desktop

You can enter the task details page and click the "Assign" icon in the upper right corner to assign tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

You can enter the task details page and click on the "Assign" icon in the upper right corner to assign tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

What should I do if I don't want to receive reminders for tasks assigned to others in the shared list?

You can turn on "Do not disturb". If there are no tasks assigned to you in the shared list, you will not receive reminders.

Mobile

Desktop

Swipe left on the shared list in the left sidebar, click "Edit" to enter the list editing page, and enable "Notifications" - "Do not disturb".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

In the right-click menu of the list on the left sidebar, click "Edit" to enter the list editing interface, and you can enable "Don't disturb".

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d6c745506943c7c692aaac368df78b5f.png)

How to comment on tasks?

Mobile

Desktop

Go to the task details page - click on the "..." in the upper right corner - "More" - "Comment".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)

Enter the task details page - click the "Comment" icon in the lower right corner to comment on the task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055792921664028672)
