🚀 What's New
=============

[More Flexible Countdown ✨ (March 9)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#more-flexible-countdown-%E2%9C%A8-(march-9))

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To make it easier to record and manage important dates, this update brings several improvements to the Countdown feature.

### [New Day Calculation Mode](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#new-day-calculation-mode)

When creating an anniversary, you can now choose whether the selected date should be counted as Day 1, making the day calculation more flexible for different scenarios.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> How to set it up: Add a countdown → Select **Anniversary** → Choose a date → Under **Day Calculation Mode**, select **Standard** or **Standard +1 Day**.

### [Custom Repeat Option](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#custom-repeat-option)

Countdowns now support more flexible recurrence rules, such as the Xth weekday of a specific month each year or the Xth day of each month. This makes it easier to set reminders for a wider range of occasions.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> How to set it up: Open a countdown → Click the **…** in the top-right corner → Select **Edit** → Click **Repeat** → Choose **Custom**.

### [Notes for Countdown](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#notes-for-countdown)

You can now add notes to each countdown to record reminders, memories, or anything special about that day.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> How to set it up: Open the countdown details page → Click the **note icon** in the bottom-left corner → Add your note.

### [Other Updates](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#other-updates)

*   Habit Widgets for PC

Habit widgets are now available on PC. View your habits and complete check-ins directly from your desktop without opening the app.

*   Option to Show Item Icons in Calendar

You can now choose whether to display item icons in the Calendar. Click the **…** in the top-right corner of Calendar → **View Options** → **Style** → Toggle **Show Item Icons**.

*   Custom Dark Theme for iOS & Desktop

Custom dark theme colors are now available on iOS and Desktop. Go to **Settings** → **Appearance** → **Theme**, select **Dark**, and choose your preferred accent color.

[Version 8.0 — A Major Update to Tasks & Calendar 🚀 (Jan 8)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#version-8.0-%E2%80%94-a-major-update-to-tasks-%26-calendar-%F0%9F%9A%80-(jan-8))

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Suggested Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#suggested-tasks)

The Today list now includes a new **Suggested Tasks** feature. It helps you review unfinished tasks and decide what to focus on today. Tasks are suggested based on factors such as creation time, rescheduling history, and upcoming due dates, making it easier to identify priorities and quickly add them to Today.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> How to use: Today → Top-right Suggested Tasks

[View detailed instructions](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616)

### [List Backgrounds](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#list-backgrounds)

You can now set a personalized background for each list. By using different visual styles, it’s easier to distinguish between work, life, and personal lists at a glance, especially when switching between different contexts.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> Mobile only

> How to use: List → More → Background

[View detailed instructions](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608#list-background)

### [Yearly View + Heatmap](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#yearly-view-%2B-heatmap)

A new **Yearly View** is now available, giving you a year-at-a-glance overview to support long-term planning and important task scheduling.

You can also enable the **heatmap** to visualize task density across the year and quickly review busy and lighter periods.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> How to use: Calendar → View Options → Style → Enable Heatmap

### [Flexible Month View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#flexible-month-view)

The Month View now supports pinch-to-zoom gestures. You can zoom in to show fewer weeks and check more tasks directly within each date, reducing collapsed items and improving task browsing across specific time ranges.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> Mobile only

### [Calendar View Options](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#calendar-view-options)

**Enhanced Color Options**

Color settings for tasks are now more centralized. After choosing to display colors by List or Tag, you can directly assign colors to the corresponding lists or tags.

Habit and Countdown now also support custom colors. You can choose a unified color or set individual colors to better distinguish different types of content and improve overall clarity.

[View detailed instructions](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#color)

**New Modern Style**

A new Modern calendar style is now available, offering a cleaner and more streamlined look with improved readability.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> How to use: Calendar → View Options → Style → Modern

### [Desktop Interface Improvements](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#desktop-interface-improvements)

A new **Card Style** layout is now available on desktop. The card-based interface makes information structure clearer and browsing more intuitive.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> How to use: Settings → Appearance → Theme → Interface Style → Card

We’ve also refined various desktop UI details to improve consistency across spacing, colors, and visual hierarchy, resulting in a more cohesive and polished experience.

[Interface Refresh 🆕 Now More Translucent (Oct 30)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#interface-refresh-%F0%9F%86%95-now-more-translucent-(oct-30))

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Adapted for iOS 26 Liquid Glass](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#adapted-for-ios-26-liquid-glass)

TickTick now supports the Liquid Glass design on iOS 26, bringing a more translucent, natural, and visually upgraded interface.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

### [Custom Dark Theme for Android](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#custom-dark-theme-for-android)

You can now freely choose your preferred accent color in Dark Mode.

> Go to **Settings** > **Appearance** > **Theme**, tap **Dark**, and set your color.

### [Optimized Pomodoro Experience](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#optimized-pomodoro-experience)

After a focus session ends, if you continue working, you can add the extra time to your focus record for more complete tracking. If you finish early but forget to stop the timer, you can manually adjust the duration on the Focus Completion page to keep your records accurate.

👉 [Click to learn how to use it](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#edit-or-add-focus-duration-after-a-session)

[Adapted for iOS 26 ✨ Optimized Constant Reminder ⏰ (Sep 15th)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#adapted-for-ios-26-%E2%9C%A8-optimized-constant-reminder-%E2%8F%B0-(sep-15th))

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On iOS 26, the upgraded Constant Reminder works like a system alarm, ringing on time even in Focus, Do Not Disturb, or Sleep mode—so important tasks are never missed.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> After upgrading to iOS 26, enable Constant Reminder when setting a reminder and grant system alarm permission.

[🍅 Focus Records More Flexible, Operation Experience Upgraded! ✨ (Jul 31st)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#%F0%9F%8D%85-focus-records-more-flexible%2C-operation-experience-upgraded!-%E2%9C%A8-(jul-31st))

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Optimized Focus Record Experience](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#optimized-focus-record-experience)

Deleting focus records is no longer limited to 30 days—you can now freely add or delete records anytime. At the same time, Batch Edit and Delete All are supported, helping you quickly manage your focus data.

Want to review specific records? You can now filter focus records by Date, Duration, or Linked Status to easily find what you need.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

### [🛠️ Operation Details Optimized](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#%F0%9F%9B%A0%EF%B8%8F-operation-details-optimized)

*   **Alt Key Features on Desktop**

In the calendar, hold Alt (Option on Mac) to display the completion checkbox—check tasks off without opening them. In the task list, hold Alt/Option to view the full time of each task, so you won’t miss any part of its schedule.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

*   **Unlink from Parent Task**

Sometimes a task is linked to a parent task, but later you may want to remove the link. Click the × next to the linked parent task, or hover over the main task and select Unlink.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

*   **Improved Link Editing Experience**

Hover over a link to bring up a quick menu, where you can quickly edit or copy the link.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

[🚀 Countdown Experience Upgraded (Jun 30th)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#%F0%9F%9A%80-countdown-experience-upgraded-(jun-30th))

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Customize Counting Mode](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#customize-counting-mode)

Want to know how many days until your anniversary—or how many days have passed? Now, for past dates with repetition (like a yearly anniversary), you can tap the Counting Mode button to choose how it's displayed:

*   Countdown: Shows “XX days until XX”
*   Count Up: Shows “It’s been XX days since XX”

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

### [Show Age for Birthdays](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#show-age-for-birthdays)

When adding or editing a birthday, you can enable the Show Age toggle to see the person’s exact age directly on the card—no need for mental math. The key info is right there at a glance.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

### [Switch Between Days, Weeks & Years](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#switch-between-days%2C-weeks-%26-years)

Mobile

Desktop

On the countdown details page, tap the day count in the center to switch between days, weeks, months, or years. This helps you better visualize the passage of time using different units.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

On desktop, just click the number on the countdown card to switch units.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

### [Enable Show Group](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#enable-show-group)

Tap the “…” in the top right of the Countdown homepage and turn on Show Group. Your important dates will be automatically organized by type, making everything easier to browse.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

[🎉 Countdown | Never Miss an Important Day! (May 12th)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#%F0%9F%8E%89-countdown-%7C-never-miss-an-important-day!-(may-12th))

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A life-changing exam, a long-awaited vacation, a meaningful anniversary — some days inspire us, some keep us hopeful, and others deserve to be remembered.

Now introducing a brand-new feature in TickTick: Countdown, designed to help you mark meaningful moments, count down with anticipation, and celebrate what truly matters.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

*   **Countdowns**: Exams, project deadlines, ID expirations... Stay on track with clear countdowns for what matters most.
    
*   **Anniversaries**: Birthdays, relationship milestones, or any day worth remembering... Set custom recurring reminders to celebrate every year.
    
*   **Rich Styles**: Choose from rich styles or upload your own image to create a page that feels personal and meaningful.
    
*   **Synced View**: Your countdowns can show in Smart Lists and the Calendar, so important days always stay visible.
    

How to enable the Countdown feature?

📱 On mobile: Go to **Settings** > **Tab Bar**, find **Countdown**, and tap the plus icon to enable it.

💻 On desktop: Click your avatar, go to **Settings** > **Features**, and enable **Countdown**.

Once enabled, just tap the + button on the Countdown page to add your very first countdown.

👉 Learn more: [Countdown](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7321455627362893824)

[Comprehensive Upgrade! 📅 More Complete Calendar, Stronger Security (Mar 25th)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#comprehensive-upgrade!-%F0%9F%93%85-more-complete-calendar%2C-stronger-security-(mar-25th))

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Apple Health Data Integration](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#apple-health-data-integration)

Now, your workouts and mindfulness records can be displayed alongside your tasks and events in the calendar! View your tasks, schedules, and health data at a glance, and easily manage your daily status!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> Available on iOS 16 and later.

How to enable?

*   Method 1: Go to Calendar → Tap the **...** in the top right corner → Select **View Options** → Go to **Apple Health Data**.
    
*   Method 2: Go to **Settings** → Click **Import & Integration** → Select **Apple Health Data**.
    

### [Batch Operations in Desktop Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#batch-operations-in-desktop-calendar)

When unexpected events occur, and you need to adjust multiple tasks quickly, here’s how you can modify multiple tasks at once: Hold down **Ctrl** (Windows) or **Command** (Mac) while clicking to select or dragging to select multiple tasks. You can right-click to complete or delete tasks in bulk, and drag to adjust task times.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

> Day, Week, and Multi-Day views: Support click and drag selection. Month and Multi-Week views: Support click selection only.

Additionally, we've introduced the **Postpone** feature. Select multiple tasks from your task list or calendar view, then click the Postpone button to delay them in bulk, making schedule adjustments more convenient.

> Available on: Windows & Web (macOS version under development).

### [Two-Step Verification Support](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#two-step-verification-support)

TickTick now supports Two-Step Verification, adding an extra layer of security to your account during login!

How to enable?

Go to **Settings** → **Account & Security** → **Two-Step Verification**, and enable it with just one tap for extra protection.

Note for Mac & PC users: Please enable it via the web version first.

👉 Learn more: [Two-Step Verification](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7307588296744370176)

[🔗 Major Update: Seamless Task Management (Feb 28th)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#%F0%9F%94%97-major-update%3A-seamless-task-management-(feb-28th))

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Notion Integration](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#notion-integration)

If you manage projects in Notion and rely on TickTick for task management, the new **Notion Integration** feature is here to connect the two seamlessly.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

*   Seamless Sync: Sync Notion databases to TickTick, view tasks on the calendar, and set reminders effortlessly.
    
*   Automatic Updates: Edit tasks in TickTick and sync them back to Notion in real-time to keep plans up-to-date.
    

How to add the integration?

Mobile

Desktop

Go to **Settings > Import & Integration > Notion** to get started.

Click your profile picture, go to **Settings**, find **Integrations & Import > Notion**, then click **Add Integration**.

For more detailed instructions, please refer to: [Integrate Notion](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

### [Other Updates](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#other-updates-1)

1.  **Optimized Voice Task Adding Experience**

New visual design for a smoother task-adding experience. Simply long-tap the "+" button in the task or calendar module to use.

Improved long voice input experience: While speaking, drag the "+" button to the left to switch to recording mode. Release the button to continue input without holding it, making it easier to use.

> Available for iOS 17 or newer.
> 
> Some Android devices do not support recording mode.

2.  **Link Parent Task Optimization**

How can you quickly organize and categorize multiple tasks? Now, after selecting multiple tasks, you can tap the "..." menu or Right-click on the task to quickly **Link Parent Task**.

[Enhanced Reminders Update! ⏰ (Jan 15th)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#enhanced-reminders-update!-%E2%8F%B0-(jan-15th))

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Added End-Time Reminder](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#added-end-time-reminder)

Set 'At the end' reminders for tasks with duration to stay on top of deadlines.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

### [Added Persian Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#added-persian-calendar)

Enable the Persian Calendar in "Settings" > "Date & Time" > "Additional Calendar" to easily manage schedules and events based on the Persian calendar.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080)

### [Default Duration Added Custom Option](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#default-duration-added-custom-option)

Now, under "Task Default" > "Default Duration," you can select "Custom" to better suit your needs.

### [Added the option to "Archive together with other members."](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082552170989486080#added-the-option-to-%22archive-together-with-other-members.%22)

When a project ends, members with editing permissions can select "Archive together with other members" to reduce repetitive actions and keep team progress aligned.

> Note: macOS doesn't support archive sync yet.

> To experience these features, update your mobile app to version 7.4.70 or above and desktop app to version 6.1.40 or above.

⏳ Countdown
===========

In the fast-paced rhythm of life, there are always special days you don't want to forget—or rush through. TickTick's Countdown feature helps you thoughtfully record each important moment.

🎂 **Anniversaries** — Celebrate the moments that matter: falling in love, getting married, birthdays, the day you brought your pet home... Each year, these dates mark a time to cherish. TickTick will remind you right on time, so you can fully embrace these special occasions.

⏳ **Countdowns** — Count down to every moment you’re looking forward to: a trip, an exam, a performance, a goal achieved... Watching the days tick down fuels your motivation and builds a sense of joyful anticipation. TickTick helps you plan each step, making preparation smoother and more intentional.

📌 Perfect for:

*   Those who don't want to miss important dates
    
*   Those who love to plan ahead and prepare surprises
    
*   Those who need countdowns to stay motivated toward goals
    
*   Those who want to add more meaning and celebration to everyday life
    

These days may not always be the most urgent, but they are often the most heartwarming. Anniversaries help you honor the past; countdowns help you look forward to the future. One reminds you to treasure love, the other keeps you moving toward your dreams.

Start adding your important days now!

👉 [Add Countdowns](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408)

👉 [Customize Your Countdowns](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534550377070592)

👉 [Manage Your Countdowns](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534343065206784)

Habit Review

Add Countdowns

🤝 Collaboration
================

Whether you are collaborating with colleagues to complete a work project or planning a weekend trip with family and friends, you can use a shared list for synchronization and discussion. All operations below require the use of a "shared list".

**"What are the applicable scenarios for collaboration?"**

Here are a few common application scenarios for your reference:

*   "Work project" - tasks in the shared list can be assigned to respective responsible persons, allowing for tracking of the list or task progress and gaining real-time insights into the level of completion.
*   "Camping plan" - after deciding on a camping location, instead of immediately setting off, a camping plan list needs to be created and shared with your friends, assigning each person their respective tasks to ensure worry-free camping.

👉 [How to Share a List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520)

👉 [How Teams Can Collaborate](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

Manage Your Countdowns

How to Share a List

🔑 Account and Security
=======================

The users of TickTick can be divided into two types:

*   Regular users: Anyone can create a TickTick account for free.
*   Premium members: After upgrading to a premium, you can unlock a ton of practical member features.👉 [Premium features](https://ticktick.com/about/upgrade)
    

From registration, start your journey with TickTick, create tasks, establish lists... make your life more organized.👉 [Registration and Login](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781436309110784)

Afraid of losing data? Want to use data from multiple apps in one application? We also offer you the choice to merge multiple apps into one.👉 [Data Backup and Migration](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781405648748544)

=========================

You can also integrate events and tasks from other apps together for unified planning.

In addition, we also provide multiple ways to link your TickTick account. Check them out!

💻 Cross-Platform Support
=========================

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780388337090560)

Currently, TickTick supports downloading and use on all platforms. Whether it's a phone, computer, or smartwatch, TickTick supports almost all devices and operating systems.

*   Sitting in the office, whether you are using the Windows or Mac system, you can download TickTick to use;
*   On the way to work, you can take out your phone to see if there is anything to do;
*   Going out for exercise, inconvenient to use a phone? No problem, you can receive reminders on your watch;
*   Lying in bed, you can use a pad to review the day's events;
*   Traveling outside, unable to use your own computer, you can open the web version to use, which is equally convenient and fast.

You can click here to download and use the corresponding version → [Download TickTick](https://ticktick.com/about/download)

[🕐 Smart Recognition](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

[🔜 Shortcuts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

🖱️ Desktop Interaction Tips
============================

You can boost your efficiency in TickTick by using modifier key actions—just hold down keys like Ctrl, Alt, or Shift while performing mouse actions. This makes everyday task management smoother and faster.

[✅ Task](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#%E2%9C%85-task)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Select multiple tasks for batch editing](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#select-multiple-tasks-for-batch-editing)

When you need to modify multiple tasks at once, there's no need to click each one individually. You can:

*   Hold down **Ctrl** and click to select multiple individual tasks.
    
*   Hold down **Shift** and click the first and last task in a range to select all tasks in between.
    
*   Use **Shift** + **↑** / **↓** to select multiple tasks via keyboard.
    
*   **Click and drag your mouse** to box-select multiple tasks.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)

Once selected, a batch editing toolbar will appear on the right side, allowing you to quickly update the tasks' due date, priority, list, tags, and more. You can also use keyboard shortcuts to perform bulk actions — like **Ctrl** + **0** to set all selected tasks to today.

> For more keyboard shortcuts, go to the bottom-left corner of the desktop app and click **?** → **Shortcuts**.

### [Quickly switch between tasks or lists](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#quickly-switch-between-tasks-or-lists)

Need to browse through tasks or lists quickly? Simply press the **↑** or **↓** arrow keys to move between them smoothly—no mouse required.

### [Organize tasks by dragging](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#organize-tasks-by-dragging)

To move a task from one list to another, hover over it and drag the hamburger icon on the left to the destination list in the sidebar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)

The same applies to Smart Lists and tags:

*   Drag a task onto a Smart List to auto-assign the corresponding due date.
    
*   Drag a task onto a tag to apply it instantly—no need to open the task or switch views.
    

> You can also do this with multiple selected tasks at once.

### [Create subtasks by dragging](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#create-subtasks-by-dragging)

Want to build task hierarchies? Just drag a task below and slightly to the right of another. This will automatically turn it into a subtask.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)

To remove the subtask relationship, drag it out of the indented position.

### [Immersive writing](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#immersive-writing)

Need to focus on editing a task? Press **Ctrl + Alt + 0** (Mac: **Command + Shift + 0**) to enter immersive writing mode and enjoy full-screen editing.

### [Insert task links quickly](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#insert-task-links-quickly)

To link another task within a note or a task description, just type **\[\[** and a dropdown will appear, allowing you to quickly find and insert the related task — no need to copy and paste.\
\
![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)\
\
### [Style paragraphs with the command menu](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#style-paragraphs-with-the-command-menu)\
\
In the task detail area, type **/** to open the command menu. Then use the ↑ / ↓ keys and Enter to quickly apply text formatting — like headings, bullet lists, and more. You can format as you type, without interrupting your writing flow.\
\
![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)\
\
### [Efficient text selection](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#efficient-text-selection)\
\
When editing task details, use **Shift** + **←** / **→** to select characters precisely, or **Ctrl** + **Shift** + **←** / **→** to select by word. These shortcuts help you edit content more efficiently.\
\
[📅 Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#%F0%9F%93%85-calendar)\
\
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\
\
### [Duplicate tasks quickly](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#duplicate-tasks-quickly)\
\
Sometimes a task isn't recurring but needs to happen multiple times. Hold down **Ctrl** (or **Option** on Mac), then drag the task to a new time slot to create a copy—just like duplicating a file.\
\
![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)\
\
> If you're using the web version on a Mac, hold Command and drag to copy a task.\
\
### [Select and manage multiple tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#select-and-manage-multiple-tasks)\
\
Need to update several tasks at once? Hold down **Ctrl** and click to multi-select tasks in the calendar. Or drag a box across the timeline in day, week, or multi-day view to select multiple tasks for batch moving, editing, deleting, and more.\
\
![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)\
\
> Available on Windows and web platforms; currently not supported on Mac.\
\
### [Show checkboxes for tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#show-checkboxes-for-tasks)\
\
To quickly mark tasks as complete in the calendar, hold down **Alt** (Windows) or **Option** (Mac). This reveals checkboxes without having to open the task details.\
\
![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)\
\
### [Switch dates efficiently](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#switch-dates-efficiently)\
\
Use the arrow keys **↑** / **↓** / **←** / **→** to scroll through calendar dates—navigate to previous or next day, week, or month without using your mouse.\
\
### [Scroll through dates in Day / Week view](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#scroll-through-dates-in-day-%2F-week-view)\
\
In Day, Week, or Multi-Day view, hold down **Shift** and scroll your mouse wheel to move horizontally across dates — like flipping through a planner.\
\
### [Zoom the timeline](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#zoom-the-timeline)\
\
Want to see more or fewer time blocks on the calendar? Hold **Ctrl** (or **Command** on Mac) and scroll your mouse wheel to zoom the timeline in Day, Week, and Multi-day views.\
\
### [Adjust font size](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#adjust-font-size)\
\
Use **Ctrl +** / **Ctrl -** (or **Command +** / **Command -**) to increase or decrease interface font size. Press **Ctrl** + **0** (or **Command** + **0**) to reset to default. Perfect for matching your screen resolution and personal preference.\
\
[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288#faq)\
\
------------------------------------------------------------------\
\
I can't find the shortcuts mentioned in the article. Are the shortcuts different on Mac and Windows?\
\
Yes, keyboard shortcuts differ between operating systems. Common key mappings are:\
\
*   Ctrl key on Windows = Command (⌘) key on Mac\
    \
*   Alt key on Windows = Option (⌥) key on Mac\
    \
\
Just replace the Windows key mentioned with the matching Mac key depending on your system.\
\
Once you get familiar with these modifier key actions and quick techniques, you'll find managing tasks and scheduling with TickTick smoother than ever.\
\
⌨️ Desktop Shortcuts\
\

\

🔜 Shortcuts
============

**"Shortcuts”** is a powerful automation tool introduced by the iOS system, allowing users to create and implement personalized functionalities by simply arranging and combining various actions. It can be understood as a simplified programming tool, enabling users to create and customize a series of action sequences to execute common tasks more efficiently.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/74823292e1c5f36dc5495c8268c43a76.gif)

[How to Add a Shortcut](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200#how-to-add-a-shortcut)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By setting up a "View Today" shortcut, you can skip the complex process of opening "TickTick - Lists - Today" and simply tap the shortcut to view the content directly in a pop-up.

How do I set up Shortcut？

iOS

macOS

Open the **"Shortcuts" app** on your phone. If you can't find it, search for it in the App Store and download it.

After opening the app, tap the **"+" in the top right corner - "Add Action" - then search for "TickTick."** You can add the actions you need based on your preferences.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/bd92f3d17e5307388706ddd04290a072.png)

Upgrade your computer to version 4.0.21 or above, then find "Shortcuts" in system Settings and add your preferred actions. You can add frequently used actions to the menu bar in the "Shortcuts" app.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

This way, you can quickly access them from the **Menu bar** at the top of your Mac.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

Whether you want to start a Focus Timer or add a task, you can do it directly from the Menu bar! ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200) 

Next, let's explore some practical ways to combine TickTick with Shortcuts 👇👇👇

### [💫 Voice-to-Text for Inspiration](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200#%F0%9F%92%AB-voice-to-text-for-inspiration)

If you often have quick ideas, try creating tasks using voice-to-text! When inspiration strikes, just open the shortcut to convert your voice into text, and save it instantly to a specified TickTick list.

**Setup Instructions:**

Open the **Shortcuts app**, tap the **"New Shortcut**" button (or the "+" in the top-right corner), search for "**Dictate Text**" in the search bar, then add **"TickTick" - "Add Content to Task"**. For the **"Title"** field, select the variable **"Dictate Text"**, and for the **"List"** field, choose the relevant task list where you want to add the task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

### [💻 Custom Workflows](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200#%F0%9F%92%BB-custom-workflows)

Beyond basic actions, you can use Shortcuts to create your own workflows. For example, set up a “Start Working” shortcut that automatically puts your phone in Do Not Disturb mode when you begin focusing. When it’s time to work, just tap the shortcut to seamlessly enter work mode.

**Setup Instructions:**

Open the **Shortcuts app**, tap the **"New Shortcut"** button (or the "+" in the top-right corner), search for **"TickTick" - "Focus"**. Then, in the search bar, type **"Set Focus"** to complete the setup.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

[Shortcut Automations](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200#shortcut-automations)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Shortcuts aren’t limited to the actions above. You can set different triggers in Shortcuts - Automation, allowing your iPhone to run specific actions automatically under certain conditions!

Didn’t quite get it? No worries, check out these examples:

### [⏰ Intelligent Alarm Clock](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200#%E2%8F%B0-intelligent-alarm-clock)

1.  Open the Shortcuts app and go to the Automation page. Tap on the **“New Automation”** button (or the “+” in the top-right corner), then **select “Alarm”**. Set the trigger to **“Goes Off” → “Existing” → “Run Immediately”.** ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)
    
2.  Tap on **"New Blank Automation"** → In the search bar, type **"Weather" → Select "Get Current Weather"**.Next, select the **"TickTick" app → Choose "Smart List" → Select "Today".** ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)
    
3.  Select **"Text"** and input your custom message, using variables like Date, Weather, and To-Do List. Then choose **"Speak Text"** and **click Done to complete the setup.** ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)
    

### [🍅 Start Focusing](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200#%F0%9F%8D%85-start-focusing)

Want to easily track your fragmented time?

For example, you might spend over 20 minutes studying with a learning app during your commute. but you often forget to start the focus timer and end up losing your focus tracking. Now, by setting up an automation shortcut to start focusing, you can easily record your time.

**How to set it up:**

Open the Shortcuts app and go to the **Automation page**. Tap on the **“New Automation”** button (or the “+” in the top-right corner), **select "App,"** then set it to trigger when the **"Duolingo" App** is opened. Choose the **"Start Focus"** action in TickTick, select your preferred focus mode and duration, then tap **"Done"** to complete the set up. ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

When you open the learning app, TickTick’s focus mode will automatically start, tracking your study time without any extra effort.

### [✉️ Etract SMS](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200#%E2%9C%89%EF%B8%8F-etract-sms)

Always forget to pick up your parcel from the self-pickup station?

Try this tip to automatically add parcel reminders to your TickTick tasks! When you receive a delivery SMS, the task will be automatically added to TickTick, so you never miss the pickup time again!

**How to set it up:**

1.  Open the Shortcuts app and go to the **Automation page**. Tap the **"New Automation**" button (or the "+" in the top right corner), choose **"Messages,"** and select **“Messages Contains"** under message criteria. ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)
    
2.  In the input box, enter the keyword for the message, such as the name of your delivery station (e.g., "Amazon Locker"), then choose **"Run Immediately."** Proceed to the next page and tap **“New Blank Automation."** ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)
    
3.  In the input box below, search for **"Get Text from Input"** and select **"Input"** **\-“Shortcut Input”.** ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)
    
4.  Search for **"TickTick"** in the input box, then select **"Add Task."** Tap on **"Title" to choose "Text,"** select the list you want the task to be added to, and click **"Done"** to finish creating the automation. ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)
    

Now, whenever you receive a message containing "Amazon Locker," it will automatically be added as a task in your TickTick list.

You can also set up similar automation for other tasks, such as "Phone bill," "Utility payments," or "Bank card," to extract relevant information from messages.

# How to Use Eisenhower Matrix

![](<Base64-Image-Removed>)

Ctrl K

Welcome

[🏅 Beginner's Guide](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7054286604315131904)

[✅ Task](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782436621254656)

[🎯 Eisenhower Matrix](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782071033135104)

[How to Edit the Rules for Eisenhower Matrix](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

[🍅 Pomodoro](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782025193586688)

[⏳ Timeline View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

[⌨️ Desktop Shortcuts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776)

[🖱️ Desktop Interaction Tips](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)

[📔 Notes and Summary](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

[🔜 Shortcuts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

How to Use Eisenhower Matrix
============================

[Understanding the Eisenhower Matrix](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864#understanding-the-eisenhower-matrix)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In 1954, former US President Eisenhower mentioned the concepts of "Not Urgent & Important" and "Urgent & Unimportant" in a university speech, quoting a school principal's statement.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864)

After that, Stephen Covey introduced the Eisenhower Matrix in _The 7 Habits of Highly Effective People_. It separates tasks into four matrixs based on the two dimensions of **"importance" and "urgency"**. Then, tasks are placed into each matrix and completed according to the principles of each matrix.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864)

[Using the Eisenhower Matrix in TickTick](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864#using-the-eisenhower-matrix-in-ticktick)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Enable the Eisenhower Matrix](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864#enable-the-eisenhower-matrix)

You can enable the Eisenhower Matrix feature on both mobile and desktop to categorize your tasks based on urgency and importance.

Mobile

Desktop

Go to **Settings > Tab Bar**, then enable **Eisenhower Matrix**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/bfa241182e78e6d9bcc0e30a6b306146.png)

Click your avatar > **Settings > Features**, then enable **Eisenhower Matrix**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/eebc9e65c2f1f3215628366c511c7859.png)

We will automatically place tasks in the corresponding quadrant based on the priority you set for the task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864)

After enabling Eisenhower Matrix, you can keep your original usage habits. For example, tasks created in lists such as "Today" and "Work" will automatically appear in the Eisenhower Matrix without any extra steps.

### [Adding Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864#adding-tasks)

Of course, you can also create tasks directly in Eisenhower Matrix. Drag the plus sign to any matrix to add a task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864)

We will automatically add attributes to your tasks according to the rules of the corresponding matrix. For example, tasks created in the "Urgent & Important" matrix will be automatically set to today and high priority. Of course, you can also see this task in the "Inbox" and "Today" lists.

### [Editing Matrix Rules](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864#editing-matrix-rules)

Some time management experts may ask when they see this:

*   I already use priority to practice the Eisenhower Matrix, can it be compatible now?
*   I want to see "work" tasks in the Eisenhower Matrix, but not "life" tasks, is this possible?

Of course, these requirements can be perfectly realized!

Just enter the matrix editing interface, and you can customize the rules of each matrix according to your needs.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864)

How to Editing Matrix Rules？

On the Eisenhower Matrix page, click the ••• icon in the top right corner and select **Edit** to enter the quadrant rule editor.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/66405b21c87e28517b677845bd30449b.png)

In the editor, you can define rules for each quadrant using **List, Tag, Date, Priority, or Task.** Tasks will be automatically sorted into the appropriate quadrant based on these rules.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/0be399244cc0cb3abd7e385e194ab509.png)

How to Editing Matrix on Desktop?

Hover over any quadrant, click the **•••** icon in the top right corner, and select **Edit** to open the quadrant rule editor.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e68dd7a5ac456600efe30f58e729ae28.png)

### [Actions in the Quadrant Matrix](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864#actions-in-the-quadrant-matrix)

After opening a Quadrant Matrix, tap the ••• icon in the top right corner to access options like: **Edit Matrix**, **View Details**, **Show Completed**, **Show Check Items**, **Sort**, **Share**, **Print**, and **Select**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/2c69de9febdafcb2cf2037fefb528daf.png)

How to Use Actions in the Quadrant Matrix on Desktop?

Currently, only the **Sort** feature is available in the Quadrant Matrix on desktop. To sort tasks, hover over the matrix, click the **•••** icon in the top right corner, and select **Sort** from the menu.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/adb3d5e3707a1bb1db90912bfa30b48a.png)

👉 [How to edit rules for Eisenhower Matrix?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

[How to Manage Our Life with the Eisenhower Matrix](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864#how-to-manage-our-life-with-the-eisenhower-matrix)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now, we have already seen the Eisenhower Matrix in TickTick, so how should we use it?

In fact, the Eisenhower Matrix has already given us the answer.

1.  Urgent & Important tasks - do them immediately.
2.  Not Urgent &Important tasks - focus on them, plan and arrange.
3.  Urgent & Unimportant tasks - do them when you have low energy or delegate them to others.
4.  Not Urgent & Unimportant tasks - try not to do them as much as possible.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864)

Many people may have encountered such a situation: they know a task is very important, but they think there is still plenty of time, so they put it off. As a result, when the deadline approaches, they realize that they don't have enough time and become very anxious. They stay up late and work overtime to complete the task hastily. Not only is the quality not high, but their body also becomes very tired.

**This may be the problem caused by insufficient focus and failure to plan and arrange properly for "Not Urgent &Important" tasks.**

There are many people who encounter a different situation: they are busy from morning till night every day, with work, study, and life constantly knocking on their door. But when it comes time to summarize, they find that there seems to be no result.

**This may be because they have spent too much time and energy on "Urgent & Unimportant" tasks.**

The Eisenhower Matrix actually provides us with a new perspective, helping us decide how to respond to tasks based on the Urgent & Important dimensions.

When we have energy and relatively free time, we can look at the "Not Urgent &Important" tasks and see if there are any that can be arranged and planned. And when we are not in a good state, we can handle the "Urgent & Unimportant" tasks or delegate them to others.

**And when we find that a task needs to be moved to a different matrix, we can easily adjust it by dragging and dropping.**

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782055577124864#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

How to enable the Eisenhower Matrix?

Enable Eisenhower Matrix in "Settings" >"Tab Bar".

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/eebc9e65c2f1f3215628366c511c7859.png)

Year View: See Your Productivity at a Glance
============================================

**Year View** gives you a high-level overview of everything you completed over the past year. With the heatmap display, you can quickly spot:

*   Which months were your most productive
*   When your pace slowed down

so you can better understand your time patterns and how you’ve grown over time.

[How to Switch to Year View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7399726920725692416#how-to-switch-to-year-view)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

1.  Tap the **View icon** in the top-right corner.
2.  Select **Year**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/2346c9bc48c024fdb33386f2d3c77fe5.png)

Quick Tip:

Long-press the **Calendar** icon at the bottom to jump directly to Year View.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/87ba867973a385ad0056e86f6644fc5d.png)

1.  Click the **View switch** button in the top-right corner.
2.  Select **Year**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/fe2cde41beaaf48ca405bff62dbcd314.png)

Quick Tip:

Press Y or 4 on your keyboard to quickly switch to Year View.

[Navigating in Year View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7399726920725692416#navigating-in-year-view)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In Year View, you can tap or click different areas to drill down into more detailed views.

Mobile

Desktop

Tap a month to open that month in **Month View**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/716c905edd8c61815552885b96f3320e.png)

A Back button will appear in the top-left corner so you can return to Year View.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/71b012fe52abc00d69cb09c29b0061e0.png)

Click a month name to open that month in Month View.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c7bacdc755bcd366e3b609db80079772.png)

Click a date to open Week View.

[Heatmap View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7399726920725692416#heatmap-view)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Year View supports a **heatmap** display that shows how often you complete tasks throughout the year. This gives you a quick, visual sense of how active you are over time.

By default, the heatmap is **turned off**. You can turn it on in Display Settings.

Mobile

Desktop

Go to: ⋯ (More) → View Options → Style → Heatmap → Show.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ddb6831586f8d4b77ea302d1486cceeb.png)

Go to: ⋯ (More) → View Options → Style → Heatmap → Show.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/439cb9ccda2a3bf7664fb9485f85e00d.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/622e926d84075bd2cfa47824b697b984.png)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7399726920725692416#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

Why can’t I see any tasks in Year View?

If you don’t see tasks in Year View, please check:

*   If you have a lot of tasks, data may take a moment to load.
    
*   Year View only displays tasks with a **date** set. Tasks without a date or time will not appear — please add a date to those tasks first.
    

Can I view data from previous years?

Yes. You can switch between years in Year View to review your past task history and long-term trends.

How to Edit the Rules for Eisenhower Matrix
===========================================

In the Eisenhower Matrix, each matrix corresponds to a set of rules. Tasks will be displayed in the corresponding matrix based on the rules you set.

To make it easier for you to get started, we have provided two commonly used sets of rule combinations by default:

*   Rule combination 1: Matrix → Priority
*   Rule combination 2: "Important" corresponds to "Priority", while "Urgent" corresponds to the "Time" dimension.

Of course, you can set the quadrant rules that suit your usage habits to help you better manage your tasks.

[Rule Combination 1: Matrix→ Priority](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728#rule-combination-1%3A-matrix%E2%86%92-priority)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

Under this rule: 4 priorities correspond to 4 matrixs.

As long as you set the priority in the task, the task will be displayed in the corresponding matrix.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

When you view tasks in the Eisenhower Matrix and drag to adjust their matrix, the priority of the tasks will also change accordingly.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

This rule is very simple and suitable for new users who are just getting started.

[Rule Combination 2: Matrix → Time + Priority](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728#rule-combination-2%3A-matrix-%E2%86%92-time-%2B-priority)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

Under this rule: Priority represents "importance" and Time represents "urgency".

For example:

*   When you set a task to "today" and "high priority", this task will automatically appear in the "Urgent & Important" matrix.
*   When you set a task to "1 month later" and "low priority", this task will automatically appear in the "Not Urgent & Unimportant" matrix.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

At this point, when you are in the Eisenhower Matrix, dragging tasks to adjust their matrix, the task's time and priority will also correspondingly change.

As time passes, tasks that were originally not urgent become urgent due to approaching deadlines. And these tasks will also automatically be adjusted to the urgent matrix according to the rules you set.

[Customize Matrix Rules](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728#customize-matrix-rules)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to the default rules we provide, you can also edit matrix rules according to your own needs.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

We provide 4 dimensions:

*   List/Tag: You can choose which list/tag tasks to display in the matrix. For example, you can choose to only view the "work" list and then select "work" in the list.
*   Time: You can modify the urgent time range to "Today ~ Tomorrow, Overdue" and change the non-urgent time range to "Day after tomorrow ~ 7 days later". This way, tasks that are due far in the future will no longer be displayed, allowing for greater focus on current tasks.
*   Priority: You can set each matrix to display tasks with a certain priority.

Instead of hesitating, it's better to choose a set of rules that currently suits you best and startusing them. As you use them, you will gradually master the essentials. When you become a time management master, we believe you will have created an efficient and unique Eisenhower Matrix.

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

How can I adjust the order of the Eisenhower Matrix?

Mobile

Desktop

Click the the three dots icon in the upper right corner, select "Edit", then select the matrix that needs to be reordered, and drag it to adjust its position.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

You may just drag and drop to change the order.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

How can I add the Eisenhower Matrix desktop widget?

Android

iOS

Windows

macOS

Select "Eisenhower Matrix" in the widget page.

Long press the screen, click on the "＋" in the upper left corner, search for TickTick, select "Eisenhower Matrix", and click "Add".

Right-click on the TickTick icon in the taskbar, then select "Add Eisenhower Matrix Widget".

Click on the time area in the upper right corner of the screen, click "Edit Widget", search for TickTick, select "Eisenhower Matrix", and click "Add".

How to customize the names of the matrixs?

Mobile

Desktop

Select the matrix for which title you want to change, click on the "..." in the upper right corner, and select "Edit Matrix" to modify the name according to your personal needs.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/615a4bd5cae0df4dd27c69e63e41269b.png)

Select the matrix for which title you want to change, click on the "..." in the upper right corner, and modify the name.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

How to hide completed tasks?

On the Eisenhower Matrix page, click on the "..." in the upper right corner and select "Hide Completed".

How to adjust the task order in the Eisenhower Matrix?

Select the matrix for which order you want to change, click on the "..." in the upper right corner, and select "Sort" to choose the sorting method.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782040439881728)

Start a New Habit
=================

[Enable the Habit Tracker Module](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296#enable-the-habit-tracker-module)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can enable the **Habit Tracker** feature on both mobile and desktop to start building and managing your habits.

Mobile

Desktop

Enable the "Habit" function in "Settings" - "Tab Bar".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296)

Click on the avatar - "Settings" - "Functions" - enable "Habit".

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3153c928b2e036f3151c9c0d1d8cb0eb.png)

[How to add a habit?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296#how-to-add-a-habit%3F)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Adding from the Habit Gallery](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296#adding-from-the-habit-gallery)

There are over 60+ habits available in the TickTick Habit Gallery, covering four major categories: life, health, exercise, and mentality. You can search for new skills you want to learn in the categories and add them to your habit page with just one click.

Mobile

Desktop

Find "Habit" in the bottom bar and click on the "+" sign to enter the Habit Gallery.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296)

Find "Habit" in the left sidebar, open the habit list page, click on the "+" sign in the upper right corner, select a habit icon, and choose the habit you need from the "Habit Gallery".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296)

How to Manage Your Habits?

Mobile

Desktop

Tap a habit to open the detail page. Tap the ••• icon in the top right corner to Edit, Start Focus, Share, Archive, or Delete the habit.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296)

Click a habit to open the detail page. Click the ••• icon in the top right corner to Edit, Start Focus, Archive, or Delete the habit.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/fcdf93b9d8b701a74c080bb47d02047d.png)

### [Custom Habits](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296#custom-habits)

If the habit you want is not in the habit gallery, you can also customize your own habit! Click "Create a new habit" in the habit gallery, you can fill in the habit name, select an icon, and write some encouraging words according to the situation. Then click "Next" to further edit the habit.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296)

[Edit Your Habits](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296#edit-your-habits)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Keep Up with the Frequency](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296#keep-up-with-the-frequency)

When cultivating habits, we cannot achieve them overnight. For example, with fitness, we do not need to make it a daily requirement. You can set it to be completed three times a week.

You can set different check-in frequencies for different habits, such as fitness, where I only need to complete it three times a week.

You can set it in the Habit editing page - Frequency.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296)

### [Setting a Simple Goal](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296#setting-a-simple-goal)

When establishing a habit in the early stages, we are actually establishing an "uninterrupted" habit. At this time, in order to make it simple and easy to operate, we might as well make it super simple, so simple that you cannot find any excuse not to do it.

*   If you want to develop the habit of memorizing vocabulary, try setting a goal of 5 words per day.
*   If you want to develop the habit of reading, consider setting a goal of reading 2 pages a day.

When establishing a habit, you can choose "Reach a certain amount" in the "Goal".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296)

[Real-time Tracking of Habit Progress](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296#real-time-tracking-of-habit-progress)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use the Habit Heat Map widget to pin your habits to your desktop for real-time tracking and viewing.

Place it together with Today's Habits to conveniently check the persistence of your habits during this period.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781878401335296)

Habit Review
============

[Statistics for Habit Detail Page](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320#statistics-for-habit-detail-page)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the habit detail page statistics, we provide a "Monthly Check-in Table" and "Check-in Data". You can check your own check-in status at any time.

Mobile

Desktop

You can see the overall check-in data of the habit by scrolling up on the individual habit page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320)

Clicking on an individual habit will allow you to view the overall check-in data on the right side.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320)

### [Yearly Heat Map for Habits](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320#yearly-heat-map-for-habits)

Click "More" in the check-in data to enter the yearly heat map page for that habit, making it easy for you to review your completion status for the year.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320)

[Reviewing Habit Check-In Status](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320#reviewing-habit-check-in-status)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the statistics icon on the habit page to view the check-in status for all habits.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320)

### [Weekly and Monthly Views](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320#weekly-and-monthly-views)

You can quickly view the habit check-in statistics for this week, and premium members can directly view their habit check-in progress for the entire month.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320)

How to view Weekly and Monthly Views on a Computer?

Currently, only mobile app is supported.

### [Habit Record](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320#habit-record)

In the record, you can better view the completion status of your habits every day. Clicking on ">" will also show you the specific timeline of completion. If you have recorded your habit check-ins, they will also be displayed in the timeline.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781785312952320)

Better Achieve Habits
=====================

[Habit Tracking Methods - Easily Adaptable to Every Scenario](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696#habit-tracking-methods---easily-adaptable-to-every-scenario)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To adapt to different habit tracking scenarios, TickTick has specifically built-in three different recording methods to make it as convenient as possible for everyone to record every achievement.

### [Automatic Recording](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696#automatic-recording)

If the completion amount of a habit is relatively fixed, we recommend that you set up automatic recording. For example, drinking water - in most cases, you can check off a habit after finishing one cup. The completion amount is always fixed at one cup.

Each time you slide the screen, it will automatically record that you have completed one cup.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

### [Manual Recording](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696#manual-recording)

If the completion amount of a habit is not fixed, we recommend that you set up manual recording. For example, studying vocabulary - you may feel better in the morning and study three pages, but feel tired at night and only study one page. The amount you complete each time is not fixed.

You can manually enter the completion amount each time you check off the habit.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

### [Complete All](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696#complete-all)

Of course, we also have habits that can be completed in one go. For example, the habit of going to bed early can be completed in one day without keeping a record of completion.

By swiping to check, this habit can be completed directly.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

How to set up a Goal?

On the check-in interface, click on the "..." in the upper right corner, then click "Edit", "Goal", and choose the check-in method under "When Checking".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

[Habit Reminder - Always On Point](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696#habit-reminder---always-on-point)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can set reminders for habits based on the time it takes you to complete them. For example, for drinking water, reminders can be set at different times throughout the day: 9:00, 12:00, 18:00, and 21:00. At the designated times, you will automatically be reminded to drink water.

In addition, if you set a time reminder for an individual habit, it will appear in the corresponding timeline of the calendar, which helps you better view your schedule.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

How to Hide Habit Check-ins from the Calendar？

On the calendar page, click the ••• icon in the top right corner, go to View Options, and turn off Show Habits to hide habit check-in records.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

It's also possible to record your daily mood and log, making it easier to review your habit completion.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

How do I turn off Habit Logs?

In the "Edit Habit" section at the bottom, you can turn off Habit Logs.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

To display habits in your Smart Lists, go to the habit page, tap the **management icon** in the top right corner, and select **Show in “Today” , “Next 7 Days”.**

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

[Reviewing Habits - Achievements and Efforts at a Glance](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696#reviewing-habits---achievements-and-efforts-at-a-glance)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the habit statistics section, we provide "Check-in Overview" and "Monthly Check-in Table." You can always check your progress, even if you didn't learn enough words to fill five pages that day, you can still record your efforts and accomplishments for completing three pages.

Mobile

Desktop

Tap a habit to enter the check-in page. Swipe up to view your check-in history for the current month.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

Click a habit to view its check-in history for the current month on the right side.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/1b7b2e23cb4e58676aad87f40db81ac2.png)

How to Log Missed Check-ins?

**On Mobile / Desktop:** Tap any date in the monthly check-in calendar to log a missed check-in.

How to Change the Checked-in Style?

In the habit detail page, click the ••• icon in the top right corner, then select **Checked-in Style** to switch between a **Checkmark** or **Habit icon**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c0de87b5f4396e07f39a1204105eb165.png)

> This feature is currently only available on desktop.

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

How do I archive a habit that I no longer need to stick to?

If you no longer need to stick to a habit, you can click on the "..." in the upper right corner of the habit details page and select "Archive".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

How do I set up habit sections?

On the habit editing page, habits are grouped by time periods such as "morning/afternoon/evening/other" to classify and modularize them for display. You can easily manage and view them by simply long-pressing and dragging them.

How to display habits in the calendar?

You can enable "Show Habit" in "View Options", so that habits can be displayed in the calendar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

What’s the Difference Between Delete and Archive?

*   **Delete**: The habit will be permanently removed along with all its check-in records. This action cannot be undone.
*   **Archive**: The habit will be hidden from your main view but not deleted. You can restore it anytime from the **Archived** section.

How to Restore an Archived Habit？

Mobile

Desktop

In the habit page, tap the management icon in the top right corner to enter the Archived section. Tap the habit to open its detail page, then tap the ••• icon and select Restore.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781805944733696)

Click the Habit button in the sidebar to open the habit page, then click Archived. Right-click the habit you want to restore and select Pick up habit.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d50567eca7aa10ee5a6c3272b1545ff1.png) ![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e425c88b3e7ced60547da7a6d9c58205.png)
