Week View - Easy Planning of Weekly Schedule
============================================

The "Week View" provided by TickTick can help you achieve your goals effectively and arrange your plans in an orderly manner, while effectively helping you to complete one task after another.

[Introduction to Week View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#introduction-to-week-view)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

The mobile version's Week View offers both a timeline layout and a grid layout.

1.  The timeline layout Week View consists of the "All-day Task Bar" and "Vertical Timeline," which allows you to clearly view your current tasks and make horizontal comparisons of each day.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d738438fc2fd672d976ca1401bb20ce4.png)

*   All-day Task Bar: Tasks that are "unassigned time" for the day, all-day tasks, and cross-day tasks will be displayed here.
*   Vertical Timeline: Tasks with set times will be displayed directly on the timeline.

> In addition, we also provide "Daily View" and "3-Day View" on mobile devices to help you focus on short-term tasks.

2.  The grid layout Week View is made up of an 8-block design, clearly displaying your weekly task schedule.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/0d52d1cd44fa63eccd6050d2a7b8c138.png)

How to switch Week View layouts?

After selecting the week view in the calendar, tap the layout switch button at the top to toggle between the timeline layout and the grid layout.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e636dfb49876fd556c0fe038bc5e9bfc.png)

The Week View consists of the "All-day Task Bar" and "Vertical Timeline," which allows you to clearly view your current tasks and make horizontal comparisons of each day.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/7c0d34c97ac72a0cefdf57ad02c0520b.png)

*   All-day Task Bar: Tasks that are "unassigned time" for the day, all-day tasks, and cross-day tasks will be displayed here.
*   Vertical Timeline: Tasks with set times will be displayed directly on the timeline.

> In addition, we also provide "Daily View" and "3-Day View" on mobile devices to help you focus on short-term tasks.

[Add Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#add-tasks)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With a variety of tasks, some may take all day, some have specific time periods, and some may even take several days. Don't worry, you can easily set them up in TickTick.

### [Add All-Day Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#add-all-day-tasks)

Mobile

Desktop

You can click the "+" button in the lower right corner to add or long-press the "All-Day Tasks" bar to add all-day tasks.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/816444f7a8b2dc711c0f282c76f8cb00.png)

In the grid layout, you can also drag the "+" button to a specific date box to add a task for that day.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/450253dc7b9eafadebd3814f2b8efc19.png)

Click on the blank space next to the date to add.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e86178eea264031fa03e84f2f5796578.png)

### [Add Duration Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#add-duration-tasks)

Mobile

Desktop

In the timeline layout, you can add a time-blocked task by following these steps:

*   Long press on the "Timeline" to add a task with a default duration of "one hour."
*   You can also add tasks for any duration by long pressing and dragging.
*   After long pressing on the task block, release it and drag the two small dots on the edge of the block to adjust the task duration.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3e1cfea834b47397a238f3478f5b266b.png)

In the grid layout, you can add a time-blocked task by following these steps:

*   Tap on a specific date to enter the Day View.
*   Long-press and drag on the timeline to add a task for any time period.
*   Then, tap the "Back" button in the top left or swipe from the side of the screen to return to the Week View.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/551aeb5c8492fce8e49cec2e706edf75.png)

*   Click on the "Timeline" to add a default time point task.
    
    ![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/12137cc819023a49352d5af133ec8b89.png)
    
*   You can add tasks of any duration by long-pressing and dragging.
    
*   Place the mouse on the edge of the task block and drag to adjust the task duration when the up and down arrow icons appear.
    

### [Add Tasks that Span Multiple Days](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#add-tasks-that-span-multiple-days)

Mobile

Desktop

When using the timeline layout, Click the "+" button in the lower right corner, click "Duration", and turn on the " All Day" button. Then select the start and end dates.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/52893c0b4a7b3b3b2813e597d2389afe.png)

In the grid layout, you can add multi-day tasks by long-pressing a date box and dragging to select multiple days.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/8d2d0e78df2d27a6e8dc1f6c3aa50266.png)

Long-press and drag on the date grid to select multiple dates and add tasks that span multiple days.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/8f01e747b4d3218db34dc380abf7ed83.png)

[Task Management](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#task-management)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Easily Adjust Task Time](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#easily-adjust-task-time)

Need to adjust the time for a scheduled task due to unforeseen circumstances? Simply use your finger to drag and drop the task block to the desired time in the calendar view.

In the grid layout Week View, you can also press and hold a task, then drag it to the edge of the screen to move it to the next week, or drag the task onto the small calendar to directly change the date.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3b2fb611338c8504ba0884990c8ef95e.png)

### [Schedule Tasks Without a Set Date](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#schedule-tasks-without-a-set-date)

Open the task management panel to view all tasks without a set date and schedule them at a convenient time.

Mobile

Desktop

To access this feature, swipe left on the right edge of the screen or click on the "..." button in the top right corner of the calendar view and select "Arrange Tasks." Drag and drop the task into the calendar to schedule it.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3ab4f433b66fbaa02ead1d3614b78710.png)

Click on the "..." in the top right corner of the calendar - "Arrange tasks", and drag the task into the calendar.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e3cc86fa22bcebc251fe9d98c6507bb3.png)

[View Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#view-tasks)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Easily Swipe to View Past and Future Schedules](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#easily-swipe-to-view-past-and-future-schedules)

Mobile

Desktop

TickTick also supports "any sliding", quickly switch one week by fast sliding, and freely control the range of displaying 7 days by slow dragging.

*   Easily adjust unfinished tasks for the next week.
*   Double-click the month at the top of the page to quickly jump back to this week.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e1ed79ef29f7e6cbf4ca5a28c67e9c22.png)

We also support the following functions in the Timeline View:

*   The "Timeline View" supports zooming with two fingers. If a task's name is not clear or cannot be displayed due to the width limit of the task block, zoom in with two fingers; if you want to view more hours at once, zoom out with two fingers.
    
*   The "Timeline View" supports hiding time periods.
    

> Click on the hidden time period to expand it, and click on any part of the expanded hidden time period to hide it. After expanding the hidden time period, long press and drag the button up or down to adjust it.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5d5e42dbb971fc0aee88d834f4950fdf.png)

When viewing the **Week View** on mobile, if you prefer a more spacious layout, try switching to the **3-Day View**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/4e7997b866c731e91c73d88f8a196afd.png)

It still uses a timeline format, but shows only three days at a time—making task names and time blocks easier to read. This view is great for planning your next few days in detail, such as scheduling key tasks or organizing your time more precisely.

*   You can swipe left or right with two fingers on your trackpad to navigate forward or backward through the displayed weeks. Alternatively, click the left/right arrow buttons at the top-right corner, or use the keyboard arrow keys (left/right/up/down) to switch the visible time range.
    
*   Click the "Today" button in the upper right corner of the interface to quickly return to today.
    

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5d5e42dbb971fc0aee88d834f4950fdf.png)

The timeline within the view also supports the following features:

*   Drag the bottom edge of the All-day Task area to adjust its height. Increasing this height allows you to see more all-day tasks without overlap.
    
*   You can zoom in or out on the timeline inside the view: use pinch gestures on your trackpad (pinch to zoom out, spread to zoom in), or hold the Ctrl key while scrolling your mouse wheel.
    
*   The timeline supports hiding time ranges: click a hidden time segment to expand it, then click anywhere inside the expanded section to collapse it again. You can also drag the edges of the hidden time area to adjust which hours are shown or hidden.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056)

Looking for a more flexible way to view your schedule over a specific time period? Try **Multi-Day View**.

Whether you’re planning your work for the next 10 days or organizing a 3–5 day trip, Multi-Day View helps you see and manage your schedule more clearly.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/afe4f085d1da33f1e834d2a5153f9d5a.png)

You can also use **Multi-Week Vie**w to review your tasks over 2 or 3 weeks at a time.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e3ed7ae1a6c1c429ddfd7daa047fec64.png)

> Note: Multi-Day View and Multi-Week View are available on desktop only.

### [Viewing Habits and Focus Records](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#viewing-habits-and-focus-records)

Every week there are things that need to be consistently done, such as various habits like exercise, reading. You can use 👉 [Habit](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781896457814016)
 to easily establish a habit, check-in ✅, and feel fullfilled at the end of the week.

How to view habits and focus records in the week view?

Mobile

Desktop

Click the "···" button in the upper right corner of the calendar interface > "View Options" to open "Show Habit" and "Show Focus Records".

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/8f4d747a98ebc1c52d52d6aba2dd0aca.png)

Click on the "..." in the upper right corner of the calendar - "View Options" - enable "Show Habit" and "Show Focus Records".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056)

[Easy Review](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056#easy-review)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Many users are busy throughout the week and when it comes time to write their weekly report, they feel at a loss for words. Even though they have done a lot, they don't know what to write. With the help of the "Week View", you can easily complete a review of your work for the week.

When you open the Week View, everything you have done this week is clear at a glance, and completed tasks will appear lighter in color.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/23402696cbaf315137ba4c0f842af6e0.png)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782149730861056)

To check the "Completed tasks" and "Undone tasks" for this week, use 👉[Summary](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)
 to easily export the weekly task completion and efficiently write your weekly report without difficulty ✌️.

Month View - Monthly Review and Reflection
==========================================

Summary and review is an important tool for self-growth. By reviewing and summarizing our work, life, and learning on a monthly basis, our growth trajectory becomes clearer and more defined 🌲.

The "Month View" feature of TickTick provides a comprehensive overview of the entire month:

*   When you need to review what you have done in a month, just take a look at the Month View.
*   When you need to plan something, check the Month View first and schedule your time accordingly.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e7ce1481313ec90e9aaa5c0e2f76c25c.png)

[Add Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782128335716352#add-tasks)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to the regular method of adding tasks, you can also create a task with a long duration directly in the Month View. Go to the Month View, long press on the starting date cell, drag it left/down to the end date, and release the mouse to create the task.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/9e8347a1ee0ca367057d066ea05af18d.png)

[Review Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782128335716352#review-tasks)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Compare the monthly goals that were set at the beginning and review the completion of tasks for this month.

With too many lists and tasks, how can we review them in an organized way? It's simple, just filter the list. You can filter the list according to different aspects of life, such as work, life, and study.

Mobile

Desktop

Click the "..." in the upper right corner, then go to "Filter View Range" to filter.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782128335716352)

Click on the icon in the top left corner of the calendar view, and then select the list to be displayed.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/fb48494b2217ef30d63a4e9508d099d5.png)

**How can you view only the tasks that have been missed and not completed when they are mixed with completed tasks?**

Mobile

Desktop

Click on the "···" in the upper right corner and select "View Options", then turn off "Show Completed".

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/8ba44def06530024fea4cd93f70d0b1b.png)

Click on the "..." in the top right corner of the calendar view, then select "View Options" and disable "Show Completed".

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5f3c369f2d710d6598bffc3cbf3d32e6.png)

**Looking back on last month and ahead to next month, we support quickly switching between months.**

Mobile

Desktop

*   Swipe left or right on the calendar view to switch between months.
*   Swipe up and down to switch months.
*   Double-clicking on the month displayed at the top of the view supports quick navigation back to the current month.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/a82d9c88c1edcb0dba0f139a9faf9bea.png)

**Want a more flexible view of your upcoming plans? Use the pinch gesture in Month View to adjust how many weeks are shown.**

Spread out with two fingers to zoom in and show fewer weeks with more task details; pinch in to zoom out and return to a full-month view.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/fa851a8734b5e5f007e36286ce6bb163.png)

When zoomed into Multi-week View, tap the upper-right **Reset to Default** icon to quickly switch back to the full Month View.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/9906329d39101239788167f86758cba2.png)

Swipe up and down with two fingers on the computer touchpad, or switch using the left and right arrows in the calendar view.

> Click "Today" to quickly jump back to this month.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/059b895faec2f35e4053388a7582d1b6.png)

[Summarize this Month](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782128335716352#summarize-this-month)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Analyzing and summarizing the reasons is a crucial step in reviewing:

*   Find gold from experience: clarify your achievements
*   Learn lessons from failure: understand your shortcomings

Summarizing can extract methods and rules from them, which not only helps to solve problems in specific cases but also solves a certain type of problem. Recording insights is the key to this retrospective, save them as "notes" here 👉 [Notes](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

1.  Create a "Review" list and add a note called "October Review".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782128335716352)

2.  Double-click the note to open it in a separate window.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782128335716352)

3.  Switch to the calendar view for October to review tasks for the month and easily conduct the view ✌️.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782128335716352)

Week View - Easy Planning of Weekly Schedule

Year View: See Your Productivity at a Glance

List View - View Tasks by Day
=============================

No matter what your goals are, as long as they are what you want to achieve, the journey to reach them starts with a small step.

The "List View" calendar provided by TickTick combines the calendar and task list, which can help you better focus on "daily tasks" and efficiently complete them ✅.

In the "List View," tasks are presented in the form of "to-do items", making it easier to view.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/8410b8bca0d59fceb66cd8ac20818083.png)

[Show Timeline](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782110086299648#show-timeline)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The List Calendar View now supports displaying a timeline, chronicling your day's schedule along a timeline.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/a51f3d749ef1b3d4930b2a71c72d028c.png)

How to use: List Calendar View > Show Timeline.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/363d7e98fa363802bdb06ef6e2eeca1a.png)

Calendar View Options
=====================

[Color](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#color)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

Using a single color in the calendar can feel monotonous and makes it harder to distinguish between tasks, habits, and countdowns. With Color settings, you can assign different display colors to each type—making everything easier to spot at a glance.

Mobile

Desktop

Tap the upper-right **…** → **View Options** → **Color** to manage how tasks, habits, and countdowns are displayed and customize their colors.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312)

Click the upper-right **…** → **View Options** → **Color** to manage how tasks, habits, and countdowns are displayed and customize their colors.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312)

### [Task Color](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#task-color)

Tasks can be colored by **List, Tag, or Priority**. When selecting By List or By Tag, you can directly customize colors for each list/tag below. By Priority uses fixed priority colors.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312)

### [Habits & Countdowns Color](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#habits-%26-countdowns-color)

Habits and countdowns support two color options:

1.  **Fixed Color**: All habits/countdowns share one color (customizable).
    
2.  **Individual Colors**: Assign a unique color to each habit or countdown.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312)

Both options allow free color selection below.

[Filter List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#filter-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With too many lists and tasks displayed in the calendar, how can you find the task you want to see? Filter the list.

Mobile

Desktop

Click "..." in the upper right corner of the calendar view, select "Filter View Range" to filter the displayed lists.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/73cf7bc5aea9ce04b889973ed9da174e.png)

Click on the icon in the top left corner of the calendar view to filter the displayed list.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312)

[Style](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#style)

----------------------------------------------------------------------

Want your calendar's interface style to better match your personal taste? Tap the **...** in the top-right corner of the calendar > **View Options**, then find **Style** and choose your preferred **Modern** or **Classic** style.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312)

Additionally, you can also control whether item icons are displayed in the Calendar. In Style, toggle **Show Item Icons** to choose whether icons for tasks, subscribed calendars, habits, countdowns, and other items are shown.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312)

On Desktop, even when item icons are hidden, you can hold the **Alt** key (or **Option** on Mac) to temporarily display them. This helps you quickly distinguish different item types and complete tasks with a single click.

[Additional Time Zone](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#additional-time-zone)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Need to coordinate schedules across multiple time zones for work, travel, or other activities? Enable the "Additional Time Zone" feature to make time comparisons more intuitive!

Mobile

Desktop

Tap the "..." in the top-right corner of the calendar > "View Options," then find and enable "Additional Time Zone." Once enabled, the timeline in the calendar view will display multiple time zones.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/9499518ac65ea0557484ff27a720917d.png)

Tap "Add Time Zone" to freely choose and add the time zones you need, and set the icon and label for each. Long press and drag to reorder the time zones you've added.

Click the "..." in the top-right corner of the calendar > "View Options," then find and enable "Additional Time Zone." After enabling, the timeline in the calendar view will show multiple time zones.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e9a9b896911b65c76d2a06ac0d0a4519.png)

Click "Time Zone Settings" under "Additional Time Zone" to freely choose and add the time zones you need, and set the icon and label for each.

Tip: You can add up to five time zones, including your current time zone and up to four configurable time zones.

[Other View Options](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#other-view-options)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

You can set it in the "···" - "View Options" in the upper right corner of the calendar view.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/37cd6ae9c3ee6ca04781d7055bebcecd.png)

*   Click "Show Details" to display detailed properties of tasks in the calendar, such as time and list.
*   Click "Show Completed" to display completed tasks, habits, and subscribed calendar events in the calendar.
*   Click "Show Check Items" to display check items set in tasks in the calendar.
*   Click "Show All Repeat Cycles" to display repeated tasks on the calendar according to their repeat cycle.
*   Click "Show Habit" to display habits in the task bar of the calendar.
*   Click "Show Focus Records" to display focus records in the calendar.

You can click on the "..." in the upper right corner of the calendar view and go to "View Options" to make adjustments.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/eb301a8db38257999b8e81db2147c6fc.png)

*   Click "Show Completed" to display completed tasks, habits, and subscribed calendar events on the calendar.
*   Click "Show Check Item" to display check items set in tasks on the calendar.
*   Click "Show Future Cycles" to display repeated tasks on the calendar according to their repeat cycle.
*   Click "Show Habit" to display habits in the task bar of the calendar.
*   Click "Show Focus Records" to display focus records on the calendar.

[Batch Operations in Desktop Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#batch-operations-in-desktop-calendar)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can now select multiple tasks at once in the calendar view to perform batch actions and improve scheduling efficiency.

How to use:

Hold down Ctrl (Windows) or Command (Mac) and click, or use your mouse to drag and select multiple tasks.

Then, drag them to reschedule or right-click for more options.

> Currently available on Windows and Web.
> 
> Drag-and-drop is not yet supported on macOS.

[Postpone Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782085826445312#postpone-tasks)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A new Postpone feature is now available, allowing you to select multiple tasks and delay their scheduled time with just one click — perfect for adjusting disrupted plans with ease.

How to use: In the task list or calendar view, select multiple tasks, then click the Postpone button to shift their scheduled times forward in bulk.

Whether it's a sudden meeting, traffic delay, or unexpected change in plans, this feature helps you respond quickly and keep your task list organized.

> Currently available on Windows and Web.
> 
> Drag-and-drop is not yet supported on macOS.

Agenda View - Stringing Tasks by Time

How to Maintain Focus?
======================

[White Noise](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704#white-noise)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

White noise usually refers to real sounds from nature or our daily life, such as rain, wind, flowing water, bird chirping, and people's conversations in cafes.

Scientific research has shown that these sounds can effectively help us relax and clear our minds, thereby improving our focus and work efficiency.

To help you stay more concentrated in every Pomodoro, TickTick provides various white noise options to create a comfortable and concentrated working environment for you.

Mobile

Desktop

After starting focus, click the "Sound" icon in the upper right corner and enter "White Noise" to choose your favorite white noise.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

Enter the focus page, click the "Sound" icon in the upper right corner to choose different white noise.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

> Not yet available on the Web version.

[Full-Screen](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704#full-screen)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After starting focus on the focus page, click the screen to enter the "Simple Digital" style.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

Swipe left to switch to the "Page Flip Clock" style.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

Continuously swipe left to the "Pixel Clock" style.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

How to enable Full-Screen Mode on the desktop app?

After starting focus, click on the three dots icon in the upper right corner and select "Full-Screen Mode".

How to Automatically Enter Full-Screen Mode?

Navigate to the upper right corner "..." on the focus page, then select "Focus Settings." Enable "Auto access to Full-Screen Mode" to activate this feature.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

How to Pause, Associate Tasks, and Perform Other Actions in Full-Screen Mode?

Simply tap the screen to choose the desired action.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

[Screen Always On](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704#screen-always-on)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Currently, only the mobile app supports it. Once you enter focus mode, you can enable the Screen Always On mode by clicking on the "sun" icon located at the top-right corner of the screen.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

[Floating Window](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704#floating-window)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the Focus page, tap the “…” icon in the top-right corner and select “Open Floating Window” to keep the Pomodoro timer visible while using other apps.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

> Currently available on mobile only.

[Flip Start](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704#flip-start)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Currently, this feature is only available on mobile apps. You can switch on "Flip Start" by clicking on the settings icon located in the top-right corner of the focus page.

When "Flip Start" is enabled, the timer will only run when the mobile device is facing downward. The focus session will automatically pause when you pick up your device.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

[Strict Mode](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704#strict-mode)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Can't control the urge to pick up your phone and unintentionally enter entertainment mode.

On the Focus page, tap the “…” icon in the top-right corner → Focus Settings → enable Strict Mode to help reduce how often you pick up your phone.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

You can also add some learning apps to Allowlist, so they can be used even in Strict Mode.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

> This feature is only applicable to "Pomodoro" and is not available in "Stopwatch" mode. In addition, iOS needs to be upgraded to iOS 16 or above to support it.

[iOS 16 Live Activity](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704#ios-16-live-activity)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iPhone users can update to 16.1 and click on the Settings icon in the upper right corner of the Focus page to enable "Live Activity" and experience seeing the focus status on the lock screen.

In addition, you can set the color and style according to your preferences.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

What should I do if I still can't see "Live Activity" even after enabling it in settings?

If you cannot see the Live Activity, you can open the Live Activity button in the System Settings > TickTick.

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

What should I do if I want to use other features while in Focus mode?

Click the "∨" in the upper left corner of the Focus page, and the Focus page will be minimized to the bottom.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

Why is Pomo-ending notification missing on macOS and how to enable it?

If you find yourself not receiving Pomo-ending notifications on your macOS device, it may be due to a specific system setting. The macOS version of our Pomodoro timer uses the Mac's own system notification.

Please go to System Settings - Notifications - TickTick - check if you've enabled "Play sound for notifications".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781994591944704)

How to Start Focus?

Timer

How to Start Focus?
===================

[Enable the Pomodoro](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#enable-the-pomodoro)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Go to **Settings** > **Tab Bar**, find **Pomodoro**, and tap the **plus icon** to enable it. Once enabled, you will see the Pomodoro feature in the bottom navigation bar.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/bae26d7f6d8ae41fe8a69ddd3fc975c6.png)

Click your profile avatar, go to **Settings** > **Features**, find **Pomodoro**, and toggle the switch to enable it. Once enabled, you will see the Pomodoro feature in the side navigation bar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

[Start Focus on the Focus Tab](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#start-focus-on-the-focus-tab)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Before you start focusing, you can choose a timing mode:

*   **Pomodoro**: A countdown timer with 25 minutes of focus followed by a 5-minute break. This helps you stay focused while allowing for proper rest.
    
*   **Stopwatch**: Tracks focus time in a count-up format. Ideal for those who prefer uninterrupted, immersive sessions.
    

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/cf4cc11d368b7aadac5f01857d6d2eb5.png)

If you want to have an data analysis of your task focus time, you can also click on "Focus" above the time to select it with your task.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5f111ebd919bc09f85a16b71426f09b6.png)

Then, tap the Start button at the bottom to begin your focus.

When you activate the Focus feature, you can directly click on the Focus button in the sidebar to enter the page and click "Start" to quickly enter the focus state.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

[Start Focus on the Task tab](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#start-focus-on-the-task-tab)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Start Focus on the Task List View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#start-focus-on-the-task-list-view)

Mobile

Desktop

1.  Task Swipe Actions

Please go to "Settings" > "General" > "Swipe Actions", and then select "Start Focus". This way, you can start focusing directly in the task list by swping.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/0afcf0c1528e7dd1db0ca756f2346fec.png)

2.  Task Context Menu

If you are an iOS user, you can also enable the "Task Context Menu" in "Settings" >"General". This way, you can quickly start focusing by long-pressing on a task.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ba58ea4a10be50ddb576d0359036e80f.png)

On the task list page, right-click on the task name, click "Start Focus", and then select Pomo/Stopwatch to start the focus.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

### [Start Focus on the Task Detail](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#start-focus-on-the-task-detail)

Mobile

Desktop

Click on the task to enter the task detail, then click on "..." on the top-right corner and select "Start Focus" to enter the focus mode.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

In the task details page, click on "..." on the top-right corner, select "Start Focus", then choose Pomo/Stopwatch to start focus.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

### [Start Focus on Reminder Pop-up](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#start-focus-on-reminder-pop-up)

You can quickly start focus by clicking "Focus" in the task reminder pop-up.

[Sync Across Devices](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#sync-across-devices)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TickTick supports sync across multiple devices for the Pomodoro Focus feature.

When you start a focus session on one device, it will automatically sync to all your other devices. Similarly, when you pause or finish a focus session on one device, it will be paused or finished on all other devices as well.

Mobile

Desktop

How to Use? Click the "..." in the top right corner of the Focus page, and then toggle on "Sync Across Devices" in the "Focus Settings."

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/87d79daa1311a8026b1874bf023301a3.png)

How to Use? Click the "..." on the Focus page, then select "Focus Settings," and choose to enable "Sync Across Devices."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

[Tips for Focus](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#tips-for-focus)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Adjusting Time during Focus](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#adjusting-time-during-focus)

Mobile

Desktop

In the focus page, click the time area to display the plus and minus signs. You can click "+" or "-" to adjust the time according to your needs.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

You can move your mouse to the time area on the focus page and click the "+" and "-" buttons on both sides of the time to adjust the focus time.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

### [Focus Note](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#focus-note)

Mobile

Desktop

Clicking on the "Add Focus Note" button located at the bottom of the focus page allows you to jot down any thoughts or ideas that come to mind during your focus session, enabling you to easily capture your ideas without interrupting your concentration.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ffba3d357b7f9044758f49485997ec77.png)

Clicking on the "Focus Note" area located in the bottom-right corner of the focus page enables you to quickly record any thoughts or ideas that come to mind.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

### [Edit or Add Focus Duration After a Session](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#edit-or-add-focus-duration-after-a-session)

Mobile

Desktop

After a focus timer ends, if you're still working on the task, tap Extra Time below the timer number to add the additional time to your focus record.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

If you finish earlier but forget to stop the timer, you can tap the timer number or go to **⋯** > **Edit Focus Duration** on the Focus Completion page to manually adjust the time for more accurate records.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

After a focus timer ends, if you continue working on the task, click Add Extra Time below the timer to include the additional duration in your focus record.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

If you finish earlier but forget to stop the timer, click the timer number or go to **⋯** > **Edit Focus Duration** on the Focus Completion page to manually adjust the time for more accurate records.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

How to enable the Focus tab?

Mobile

Desktop

Web

You may go to "Settings" > "Tab Bar" > "Pomodoro".

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/bae26d7f6d8ae41fe8a69ddd3fc975c6.png)

You may go to "Avatar" > "Settings" > "Functions" > "Focus".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

Click on the profile picture - Settings - Features - Enable "Pomodoro".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

If you begin a focus session on the desktop version, will your mobile device also enter into focus mode?

TickTick supports sync across multiple devices for the Pomodoro Focus feature.

You can click on the "···" in the upper right corner of the Pomodoro interface, then go to "Focus Settings" and enable "Sync Across Devices".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782010496745472)

Add Tasks
=========

Create the things you want to do or need to do as tasks one by one and assign them to TickTick to reduce the pressure of remembering everything in your brain.

[Quick task addition](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#quick-task-addition)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Click the "+" icon that is visible everywhere, enter the task, and click the icon to easily create the task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

You can also set the "date", "priority", "tag" for the task, and move the task to the "list".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

You can customize the order of the bottom toolbar when adding tasks. Just click on the "..." and select "Settings" to quickly configure your frequently used features.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

Enter the content in the "task addition bar" at the top of the task list page, and press the Enter key to create it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

When adding a task, you can also press the shortcut 'Shift + Enter' to quickly add a task description. After entering the description, press 'Command + Enter' to create the task successfully.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

Click the dropdown option on the right side of the input box to quickly set the priority, add attachments, or select from templates. You can also click 'Input Box Settings' to switch the input box style.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

Regular lists and Smart lists

Lists are a common way to organize tasks.

*   Regular lists: Lists created by you.
    
*   Smart lists: Lists that intelligently filter and display tasks based on certain conditions, such as All, Today, Tomorrow, and Next 7 Days.
    
    ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)
    

[Smart Recognition](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#smart-recognition)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TickTick supports recognizing dates and times in tasks. You only need to add dates and time in the task content, and we will automatically set the reminder time for you, greatly simplifying the operation steps.

For example, input "Meeting at 9 tomorrow"

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

When you don't need to recognize the time, simply press the "Delete" key on the keyboard or click on the "recognized time" to cancel recognition.

How to turn off Smart Recognition?

Open the app - "Settings" - "General" - "Smart Recognition" - "Smart Date Parsing" to turn off smart recognition.

[Task Default](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#task-default)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Task defaults refer to the pre-filled properties automatically applied when creating a new task. You can preset attributes such as the **date, list, and priority** for new tasks.

How to configure? **Go to Settings → General → Task Default.**

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

[Voice Adding Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#voice-adding-tasks)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When it's inconvenient to type, try voice input.

### [Long Press Mode](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#long-press-mode)

Long press the "+" button to start voice input. When you see the prompt "Speaking now" on the screen, speak to create a task, and release to complete the voice input.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

> *   When new users use the voice input function for the first time, holding down the "+" may trigger a system permission request. Select "Allow" to proceed.
> *   When using voice input, content that includes special information such as time will be intelligently recognized as the deadline and reminder time for a task. For example: "Meeting at 10 AM tomorrow morning."
> *   iOS users can experience the real-time transcription feature, but this is not supported on Android for now.

### [Recording Mode](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#recording-mode)

1.  Long press the “+” button and drag left/right to switch to recording mode.
    
2.  Once in recording mode, you can release the button and continue typing without holding the plus button.
    
3.  After finishing input, click the stop button to end the recording and save the text content.
    

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/4cd8192315d8aa74c1d582e59475f15d.png)

> *   The recording duration limit is 30 minutes. Once the limit is reached, it will automatically save.
> *   To save both the recording and the text, you need to upgrade to a Pro membership.
> *   iOS requires iOS 17 or later to use, and some Android models do not support recording mode.

[Adding Tasks with Widgets](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#adding-tasks-with-widgets)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TickTick also supports adding tasks through "widgets". You can click on the "+" on the widget to directly enter the task adding interface and quickly add tasks.

Android

iOS

Windows

Find the "+" button on the widget and click on it to enter the task adding interface where you can directly type in the task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

How to add a TickTick widget?

On the home screen, press and hold for about 2 seconds on a blank space, then click on "Add Widget" that appears at the bottom of the screen. In the new window, find "TickTick" and select the desired widget. Click "Add Widget" to add it successfully.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

On the widget, find the "+" sign and click it to quickly open the app's "Task Add Bar" and enter the task you want to create.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

How to add a TickTick widget?

On the home screen, press and hold for about 2 seconds to enter screen editing mode. Click on the " +" sign in the upper left corner and search for "TickTick". Click on the desired widget to add it successfully.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

Click on the input box to enter the task title, and press enter to create it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

How to add a TickTick widget?

Right-click on the TickTick icon in the system tray in the lower right corner of the screen, and select the widget you want to add.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

[Global Shortcut Keys for Desktop](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#global-shortcut-keys-for-desktop)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TickTick provides Windows and Mac users with a "global add" shortcut (Shift + Alt + A). Whether you're replying to work messages or browsing courses, simply press the shortcut key to bring up the "task add bar" with just one click.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

[More ways to add tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#more-ways-to-add-tasks)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Add tasks via email](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#add-tasks-via-email)

Do you use email for collaboration in your work? If you don't have time to deal with an email, you can turn it into a task to ensure that you don't forget about it.

To create a task via email, log in to the web version of [**TickTick**](https://ticktick.com/)
, click "Avatar" > "Settings" > "Integrations & Import", and find "Add tasks via email."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

*   The first one: [todo@mail.ticktick.com](mailto:todo@mail.ticktick.com)
    
*   The second one: your personalized email link (each person's personalized email link is different)

What is the difference between these two email addresses?

*   The first one: [todo@mail.ticktick.com](mailto:todo@mail.ticktick.com)
    . You need to send an email from your registered email address with TickTick to this email address to save the email as a task.
*   The second one: your personalized email link. When you send an email from "any email account" to the second email address, it will be saved as a task in TickTick.

Therefore, if you only have one commonly used work email and this email is also your TickTick account email, it is recommended that you save the first email address to your contacts. If you use multiple email accounts at the same time, it is recommended that you save the second email address to your contacts.

In the future, when you come across emails that you don't have time to deal with immediately, you can forward them to this email address, and they will be saved to TickTick.

### [Adding Tasks with iOS Siri](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#adding-tasks-with-ios-siri)

TickTick users on iOS can enable the "Siri" feature in the app to directly add tasks using Siri.

Open the app - "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - find "Siri" and select to enable it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

After enabling "Add Tasks via Siri", you can tell Siri:

*   Add "Go to library tomorrow" to TickTick.
*   After opening TickTick, you can see the task you just added.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

You can use simpler sentence structures by enabling "Auto-import from Reminders" Then you can tell Siri, "Remind me to go to library tomorrow."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

*   Once enabled, TickTick will automatically import tasks from the "Reminders" default list every time it is opened.

> To avoid tasks being reminded in both applications at the same time, the original task in "Reminders" will be deleted after each import.

### [Adding a Single Task to the Clipboard](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#adding-a-single-task-to-the-clipboard)

If the content you copied contains special information such as time, you can quickly add it as a task using TickTick's "Clipboard Add Task" feature.

*   Enable "Recognize information in clipboard" in "Settings" - "General" - "Task Quick Add". After enabling the option, if the content in the clipboard contains "time information," the app will prompt "you may want to add a task" when opened, and clicking "add" will create the task successfully.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

> If there is no content in the clipboard or no identifiable information in the content, no prompt will be given.

### [Copy and add multiple tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704#copy-and-add-multiple-tasks)

Copy multiple lines of text and the app will prompt "Batch Add Tasks" when opened. Select "OK" to create multiple tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782422935240704)

Set Up Recurring Tasks
======================

Writing daily reports, weekly reports, changing contact lenses, paying rent, deducting insurance fees... There are always recurring tasks that we need to remember.

Let's hand them all over to TickTick, set them as recurring tasks, and relieve our brains of the burden. 😎

[How to set Repeat?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752#how-to-set-repeat%3F)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

First, collect all the recurring events and create them one by one in TickTick. After creating a task, click "Date & Repeat" on the task details page and select "Repeat" to choose the recurrence option you need.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

> TickTick provides "Every day/week/month/year/custom" repeat options to meet your various needs.

With so many recurrence options, which one to choose? It can be simply divided into 2 categories:

*   Common recurrence (🌈Daily Trivia)
*   Custom repetition (😄 As you wish)

[Daily, Weekly, Monthly, Yearly](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752#daily%2C-weekly%2C-monthly%2C-yearly)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Daily (Dog walking, Jogging)
*   Weekly (Weekly report, Grocery shopping)
*   Monthly (Credit card bill payment)
*   Yearly (Family, Friends' birthdays 🎂)

For example, if you need to repay your credit card bill on the 20th of every month, click "Date & Repeat" and select the repayment date "20" on the calendar - set "Repeat" to "Monthly".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

How to Remove Repeat?

Open the task edit page, tap the date field to enter the settings page, locate the repeat option and tap the ✖ icon next to it to clear the repeat settings.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

[Custom Repeat](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752#custom-repeat)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If the common repeat cycles do not meet your needs, you can also use "Custom Repeat" to set the repeat cycle as you wish.

Custom Repeat includes three types of repeats: By Due Dates, By Completion Date, and By Specific Dates.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

### [By Due Dates](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752#by-due-dates)

> Due date repeat refers to the repetition that will remind you at the setting time.

For example: Wendy plans to arrange next week's work every Friday at 13:00.

*   After setting the due date repeat at 13:00 every Friday, TickTick will send a reminder at 13:00 every Friday.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

### [By Completion Dates](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752#by-completion-dates)

> Completion repeat refers to the next reminder time calculated based on the time the previous task was completed, and the next reminder time will change with the completion time.

For example: Wendy plans to exercise once every three days.

*   When the first exercise is on Tuesday, the second reminder will be on Friday (every three days).
*   However, if Wendy is delayed on Friday and can only complete the task on Saturday, the next reminder will be on Tuesday (three days later).

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

### [By Specific Dates](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752#by-specific-dates)

> Custom date repeat refers to the ability to set the repetition time of a task freely, which can be selected for one day or multiple days.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

[FAQs](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752#faqs)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

How to end the repetition?

Common recurring tasks are repeated indefinitely. You can automatically end the task's repetition by setting "Repeat Ends On" or "Repeat Ends After xx times"

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

*   Repeat Ends On: Set a repeating task to end on a specific "date", and the task will not repeat after that date.
    
*   Repeat Ends After xx times: Set a repeating task to end after a certain "count" of repetitions, and the task will not repeat after reaching that count.
    

What is the difference between "Repeat Ends On" and "Repeat Ends After xx times"?

Assuming you originally set a task to repeat on the 1st of every month, but the task was delayed and not completed until the 3rd:

*   With "Repeat Ends On", the next task reminder will still be on the 1st.
*   With "Repeat Ends After xx times", the next task reminder will be on the 3rd.

How can I modify a single cycle of a recurring task?

On the calendar view page, you can modify the date and time of the recurring task, then select "Only this Recurrence" in the pop-up window.

How can I display all future repeat cycles?

In the calendar view's "View Options", enable "Show All Repeat Cycles".

Multilevel Tasks

📆 Calendar

Effective Reminder Feature
==========================

When you set a "reminder" for your task, you will be reminded on time according to the reminder time you set, which helps you efficiently complete various tasks.

[How to set a reminder](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872#how-to-set-a-reminder)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Option 1: When creating a task, click the calendar icon below the title and select "Set Reminder."
    
*   Option 2: Enter the task details page, click "Date & Reminder" above the task title, and select "Reminder."
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)

You can also set "multiple reminders" for the task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)

How to set a custom reminder time?

When setting a reminder, select Custom to freely choose your preferred reminder time.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)

How to set the same reminder for a task?

You can modify the "task default reminder" and select the commonly used reminder as the default reminder in "Settings" - "General" - "Task Default" - "Default Reminder."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)

*   You can also set "default date", "default priority", "default list", and more for tasks.

[Reminder Pop-up](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872#reminder-pop-up)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After setting a reminder time for a task, TickTick will remind you to complete the task on time.

A "reminder pop-up" will appear to remind you to handle the task. You can choose "Dismiss", "Start Focus", "Done", or "Snooze" based on your actual situation.

In addition to receiving reminders within the app, you can also receive reminder pop-ups outside the app and when the screen is locked.

Why didn't I receive a reminder?

You can enable notification permissions in TickTick's "Settings" - "Sounds & Notifications".

Why didn't the task remind me on time?

Due to Android system restrictions, some phones need to enable "Alert Mode" in "Settings" - "Sounds & Notifications" - "Advanced Settings".

[Email Notifications](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872#email-notifications)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can log in to our web version: [ticktick.com](http://ticktick.com/)
 - click on your Avatar - Settings - Reminders & Notifications, and enable Email Notifications.

[Task reminders for more scenarios](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872#task-reminders-for-more-scenarios)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Location Reminder](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872#location-reminder)

Do you have tasks that require you to be in a specific location to complete, such as "go to the print shop to copy the company's brochure," but in reality, you forget about it completely when passing by the print shop?

The "Location Reminder" feature can help you.

*   Create a task such as "Go to the print shop to copy the company's brochure," enter the task details page, click on the top right corner "..." - "Location", and enter the print shop location.
    
*   After setting it up successfully, when you arrive at the print shop location, TickTick will automatically remind you.
    
    ![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)
    

> The "Location Reminder" feature is currently only available on iOS and Android applications.

### [End Time Reminder](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872#end-time-reminder)

When you have a meeting or event scheduled, how can you easily know when it's about to end and avoid running over?

After setting the task's duration, choose "Reminder," and check the "At the end" option. Once set, you'll get a reminder at the task's end time.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)

[How to set Reminder Ringtone](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872#how-to-set-reminder-ringtone)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After setting the reminder time for the task, you can select your favorite ringtone in "Settings" - "Sounds & Notifications" - "Reminder Ringtone".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)

If you want to set "different reminder ringtones for tasks with different priorities": when the time comes, you can distinguish the priority of the task through the ringtone without having to open your phone. You can enable "Priority Reminder Ringtone".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)

Google Calendar
===============

If you're using Google Calendar, you can choose "Subscribe from Google Calendar" or "Integration with Google Calendar."

**Subscribe from Google Calendar**

When you want to be able to manage all your things in TickTick, you can try "Subscribe from Google Calendar" to display Google Calendar events in TickTick.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781593733922816)

> You can add, modify, and delete calendar events in TickTick, and these actions are also synced to Google Calendar.

**Integration with Google Calendar**

When you want to see TickTick tasks in Google Calendar, you can try "Integration with Google Calendar" and these tasks will be displayed in Google Calendar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781593733922816)

> You can add, modify, and delete calendar events in Google Calendar, and these actions are also synced to TickTick.

Tip: Integration with Google Calendar requires an upgrade to "Android& iOS v7200, Windows & Mac & Web v5500".

[Subscribe from Google Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781593733922816#subscribe-from-google-calendar)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Go to "Settings"-> "Import & Integration"-> "Calendar" -> "Google", select "Subscribe from Google Calendar", and proceed with Google Calendar account login authorization.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/7d105826ca3dcbc4e9fa7b5ce619c63c.png)

After successful authorization, you can see the subscribed calendar in the page. Additionally, you can also view all calendar events in this calendar account under the "Subscribed Calendars" section in the sidebar.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/18dc63e785767a4068372cecc1c115da.png)

> These calendar events will also be intelligently displayed in the "Today", "Next 7 Days" smart lists, and calendar view.

You can also click the "+" button in the subscribed calendar list to add events. Once added successfully, they will be synchronized with your Google Calendar as well.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/489a7afd9986fc55490e2f43448f0c52.png)

> Operations like adding, modifying, or deleting events will be synchronized bidirectionally with Google Calendar.

Click on your Avatar -> "Settings" -> "Integrations & Import" -> "Google", select "Subscribe from Google Calendar", and proceed with Google Calendar account login authorization.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3d4daf4933f2650c9f2ebb7e9694b331.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/7ff1cd1135bfd60d5729a359238d3bfb.png)

After successful authorization, you can see the subscribed calendar account in the page.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/91551f7ca09f22d9e776c18186cc0f5a.png)

Additionally, you can also view all calendar events in this calendar account under the "Subscribed Calendars" section in the sidebar. ![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/11dd4e5dbf8ae314f2315055bd2634c4.png)

You can also click on the "input box" in the subscribed calendar list to add events. Once added successfully, they will be synchronized with your Google Calendar as well.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/b1c6225ad38960a67b42d0079dce4913.png)

> Operations like adding, modifying, or deleting events will be synchronized bidirectionally with Google Calendar.

[Integration with Google Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781593733922816#integration-with-google-calendar)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This feature requires an upgrade to "Android& iOS v7200, Windows & Mac & Web v5500."

Mobile

Desktop

Navigate to "Settings"-> "Import & Integration"-> "Calendar" -> "Google", select "Integration with Google Calendar", and proceed with Google Calendar account login authorization.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/7d105826ca3dcbc4e9fa7b5ce619c63c.png)

After successful authorization, on the "Integration with Google" page, you can set the integration options:

**1\. Choose the List and Calendar to Integrate**

Click on " Choose List" and "Choose Calendars" to choose the lists (from TickTick) and calendars (from Google Calendar) you want to synchronize bidirectionally.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/cfae697ef194ca55d9dd5c7eb30439e6.png)

*   Tasks with time attributes in the selected list will be synchronized as calendar events in the integrated Google Calendar.
*   Adding calendar events in the integrated Google Calendar will also be synchronized as tasks in the selected list.

**2\. Set Task Default Attributes**

To manage calendar events added from Google Calendar effectively, we provide "Default Tags" for you to customize the tags assigned to calendar events synced into TickTick.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/91836a09900256f50407f4c8b6116c41.png)

When you choose "All" list, you can also set a "Default List" to customize where Google Calendar events sync to in TickTick.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/a85393a8ea8655bc906969b547ffa88a.png)

**3\. Integrated**

Click "Integrate" to add the integration successfully. You will be able to see the integrated account on the page, and clicking on the account will allow you to view the details.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c8754f11c8e222250ce7a2e234e156f3.png)

**4\. Integration Effects**

After integration, the content of the integrated "list" and "calendar" will be synchronized bidirectionally.

*   List ➡️ Google Calendar: “All tasks with time attributes” in the list will be displayed as “calendar events” in Google Calendar.
    
*   List ⬅️ Google Calendar: Calendar events in Google Calendar will be synchronized as tasks in the list (existing/newly added calendar events with "Today or Future Time" set will also be synced as tasks in TickTick).
    

Any adjustments made to tasks in the lists will be synced to Google Calendar, and vice versa.

Click on your profile picture -> "Settings" -> "Integrations & Import" -> "Google", select "Integration with Google Calendar," and proceed with Google Calendar account login authorization.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3d4daf4933f2650c9f2ebb7e9694b331.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/7ff1cd1135bfd60d5729a359238d3bfb.png)

After successful authorization, on the "Integration with Google Calendar" page, you can set the integration options:

1.  **Select the Lists and Calendars to Integrate**

Click on "Select Lists" and "Select Calendars" to choose the lists (from TickTick) and calendars (from Google Calendar) you want to synchronize bidirectionally.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/8e7f3d650f798fff2d367a6acb557031.png)

*   Tasks with time attributes in the selected list will be synchronized as calendar events in the integrated Google Calendar.
    
*   Adding calendar events in the integrated Google Calendar will also be synchronized as tasks in the selected list.
    

2.  **Set Task Default Attributes**

To manage calendar events added from Google Calendar effectively, we provide "Default Tags" for you to customize the tags assigned to calendar events synced into TickTick.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/65baf9a288b0764fd365511d8a27374b.png)

When you choose "All" lists, you can also set a "Default List" to customize where Google Calendar events sync to in TickTick.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/7b9c5246b064ef3fa2cfe45073747d0d.png)

3.  **Integrated**

Click "Integrate" to add the integration successfully. You will see the integrated calendar on the calendar page and clicking on it will allow you to view the details.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/65fb3916ff4b143e3404914b88e6fc1e.png)

4.  **Integration Effects**

After integration, the content of the integrated "lists" and "calendars" will be synchronized bidirectionally.

*   Lists ➡️ Google Calendar: “All tasks with time attributes” in the lists will be displayed as “calendar events” in Google Calendar.
    
*   Lists ⬅️ Google Calendar: Calendar events in Google Calendar will be synchronized as tasks in the lists (existing/newly added calendar events with "Today or Future Time" set will also be synced as tasks in TickTick).
    

Any adjustments made to tasks in the lists will be synced to Google Calendar, and vice versa.

Please note that the following data content cannot be synchronized bidirectionally:

*   Working Location events created in Google Calendar
*   Out of Office events created in Google Calendar
*   Integrate previously created calendar events in Google Calendar with dates before today

5.  **Disintegration**

iOS

Android

Desktop

Navigate to "Settings" -> "Import & Integration" -> "Calendar", click on "Integrated Accounts" to go to the details page, click on the option you want to disintegrate, enter the "Edit Page", and click "Disintegration" at the bottom of the page to disintegrate.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/20bb52f1579933a7c422a2265988241e.png)

Navigate to the details page of the "Integration", click on the "..." in the upper right corner -> "Disintegration" to disintegrate.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/169f2a3b3cb10f65d77df36d988faece.png)

Navigate to "Settings" -> "Import & Integration" -> "Calendar", click on "Integrated Accounts" to go to the details page, click on the option you want to disintegrate, click "Disintegration" in the lower left corner to disintegrate.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/0a6cf3e81810164e985625256088cbdb.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/b4b25ebb9227f2d569a193e2b241bb74.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d94189f0d85012a1bf2e0585a2565372.png)

Please note that when you cancel the integrate, content previously synchronized in both directions will still appear in your Google Calendar and Lists. Here's how to remove them:

*   If you want to remove TickTick tasks that have been synced to Google Calendar, you can find the calendar events with the source labeled “TickTick” in Google Calendar and delete them one by one.
*   If you want to delete the Google Calendar events synchronized in the TickTick, you can find the tasks with the tag "GCal" (default tag) in the TickTick, click the tag, select and delete them in batches.

[FAQs](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781593733922816#faqs)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

What are the differences between subscribing from Google Calendar and integrating with Google Calendar?

1.  **Different Usage Scenarios:**

*   Subscribe from Google Calendar: Manage Google Calendar events centrally in TickTick and receive reminders.
*   Integrate with Google Calendar: Display tasks from TickTick in Google Calendar for centralized viewing.

2.  **Different Displayed Types after Synchronization in TickTick:**

*   Subscribe from Google Calendar: Synchronize as calendar events.
*   Integrate with Google Calendar: Synchronize as tasks.

3.  **Different Scope of Synchronization:**

*   Subscribe from Google Calendar: All calendars in the account can be subscribed.
*   Integrate with Google Calendar: Only one calendar can be integrated at a time.

Can multiple calendars be integrated within the integrated account?

Yes. Go to “Integrated Account Details” and click “Add Integration” to add another calendar account. You can connect up to 3 accounts, with up to 5 calendars under each account.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781593733922816)

How can I set task priorities and other attributes in Google?

You can enter shortcuts in the title of Google Calendar events. When the event is synchronized to TickTick, the shortcuts will be automatically recognized and the task attributes will be set accordingly.

1.  Priority: "Space!1" or "Space!High priority"
2.  Tags: "Space#Tag name"
3.  Add to List: "Space~List name" (can only be recognized successfully when integrating with TickTick's "All" list)

Is it possible to modify integrated lists and calendars?

To avoid synchronization issues, modification of integrated lists and calendars is temporarily not supported. You can cancel the integration and reintegrate it instead.

Can I integrate multiple Google Accounts?

You can integrate multiple accounts.

But please note that in order to avoid duplicate data synchronization, when an existing account is associated with the "All" list of TickTick, it will no longer be possible to associate a new account.

[CalDav Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781593733922816#caldav-calendar)

Enter the "Account", "Password", "Server Address", and "Name" of the third-party calendar that you need, and the synchronization will be completed.
