# Two-Step Verification

Two-Step Verification
=====================

TickTick supports Two-Step Verification, adding an extra layer of security to your account by requiring additional verification during login.

[Turn on Two-Step Verification](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7307588296744370176#turn-on-two-step-verification)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Web

Go to **Settings > Profile > Account Info** to enable **2-Step Verification**.

Tap to enable Two-Step Verification, complete the identity verification, and add your preferred method."

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/037715f94a24cf146d1ae3d1dc0eb3cf.png)

> Note that older app versions no longer support login. Please update to iOS V7.4.50, Android V7.4.5.0, Windows V6.1.30, macOS V6.1.20, Linux V6.0.20, or later versions.

You can choose **Email Verification Code** or **Authenticator App** for verification.Enter the code and tap 'Add' to complete the setup.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ae77ed96dee4a44def9a4ec83ade1a2d.png)

Go to your profile, then navigate to **Settings > Account to enable Two-Step Verification.**

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/498d11e5d6eb047104ef9e34fba853b4.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/44359c02f5e4354232278456110c8dcc.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/59a5c9cfcaedd0486ec6fed55c5ecd03.png)

You can choose **Email Verification Code** or **Authenticator App** for verification. Enter the code and click Add to complete the setup.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/7407520d1499dc7a6cfae3d828e0a6dc.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5b40929bc27f63796e137d632f1e6fe0.png)

How to Verify Using an Authenticator?

1.  Install an authenticator app on your mobile device (e.g., Google Authenticator or Microsoft Authenticator).
2.  Open the app and scan the QR code or enter the provided code to link your account.
3.  Enter the verification code displayed in the app to complete the verification.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/db802785bdca706c6e1be8e531b13858.png)

### [Email Verification](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7307588296744370176#email-verification)

1.  Select "Email Verification."
2.  Enter your email address and send the verification code.
3.  Enter the 6-digit code to complete the verification.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d89ce7bdecaa3736f470906eccd87d3b.png)

### [Authenticator App](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7307588296744370176#authenticator-app)

1.  Install an authenticator app on your mobile device (e.g., Google Authenticator or Microsoft Authenticator).
2.  Open the app and scan the QR code or enter the provided code to link your account.
3.  Enter the verification code displayed in the app to complete the verification.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/85d5f892e2bc1acf3fcc542b351056a7.png)

### [Backup Code](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7307588296744370176#backup-code)

Make sure to download and save your **Backup Code**. If you are unable to log in using other verification methods, you can use a backup code for quick access.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5268ad50123b595bab092343eecd16df.png)

[Using Two-Step Verification](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7307588296744370176#using-two-step-verification)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once Two-Step Verification is enabled, you will be required to verify your identity when performing the following actions:

*   Logging into your account
*   Linking an account
*   Changing linked account information
*   Deleting your account

[Turn off Two-Step Verification](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7307588296744370176#turn-off-two-step-verification)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Web

Go to **Account Info > Two-Step Verification**, Tap **Disable Two-Step Verification**, confirm by selecting **Disable**, and complete the verification to turn it off.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/633ec9ff8caafd5b935f3b3e806f1e5c.png)

Go to **Profile > Settings > Account > Two-Step Verification**, select **Disable** , and complete the verification to disable it.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/03760bbf73e49a2267e4f28a153f0f4d.png)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7307588296744370176#faq)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

How can I enable Two-Step Verification on Mac?

Currently, the Mac version does not support enabling Two-Step Verification directly. Please enable it via the Web version first.

How can I enable Two-Step Verification on PC?

Currently, the PC version does not support enabling Two-Step Verification directly. Please enable it via the Web version first.

Can’t receive the two-step verification code and can’t log in?

If you’re unable to receive the two-step verification code on your phone and don’t have any backup codes to log in, please send an **email to [support@ticktick.com](mailto:support@ticktick.com)
 using the email address linked to your TickTick account.**

Our support team will verify your information and assist you accordingly. To ensure the security of your account, we need to confirm that you are the legitimate account owner.

Please include the following information in your email:

*   Whether you have ever subscribed to **TickTick Premium**
*   If yes, please attach your **payment receipt** (for example, from **App Store, Google Play**, or **Stripe**) If your account is **not linked to an email**, please provide as much information as possible, such as:
*   Registered phone number
*   Account nickname or username
*   The device you last successfully logged in from
*   Premium payment proof (if applicable)

Once we verify your identity, we’ll help you recover access to your account or reset your verification method.

> ⚠️ To ensure your account’s security, please make sure the information you provide is accurate and verifiable. Otherwise, we may be unable to process your request.

---

# Updates in 2024

Updates in 2024
===============

[Fresh Look, Better Calendar✨ (Oct 31st)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#fresh-look%2C-better-calendar%E2%9C%A8-(oct-31st))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [New Color Themes for Desktop](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#new-color-themes-for-desktop)

As a tool you use every day, a visually pleasing interface can make your experience more enjoyable! Now, go to Settings > Appearance > Theme, and enjoy the new color themes!

### [Calendar Now Supports Checkboxes](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#calendar-now-supports-checkboxes)

Want to complete tasks more quickly in your calendar? Now, tap the "..." in the top-right corner of the calendar > "View Options," and switch the "Style" to Detailed. Tasks will show checkboxes, allowing you to easily mark them as done!

### [New Additional Time Zone for Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#new-additional-time-zone-for-calendar)

Need to manage cross-country work and travel schedules? Tap the "..." in the top-right corner of the calendar > "View Options," enable Additional Time Zone, and freely add the time zones you need.

This will make it easier to compare times across different time zones, helping you manage tasks more efficiently across regions!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

[🎉 Brand New Week View! Easily Organize Your Week 📅 (Oct 15)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#%F0%9F%8E%89-brand-new-week-view!-easily-organize-your-week-%F0%9F%93%85-(oct-15))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You're probably already familiar with the classic Week View layout, where all-day tasks appear at the top and time-specific tasks are shown on a timeline. This layout works great for those using time-blocking to better manage their day.

But what about light users who don't usually assign specific times to their tasks? Introducing the new grid layout in Week View! ✨

### [Exciting News! The All-New Grid Layout](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#exciting-news!-the-all-new-grid-layout)

The grid layout in Week View gives you a clear and organized view of your entire week in an 8-block format. It makes tracking and managing your weekly tasks a breeze—no need to remember every detail in your head!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

Compared to the classic timeline layout, the grid layout offers:

*   Better use of space, with no empty timeline slots—perfect for users who don't often set specific times for tasks.
    
*   Clearer task titles, making it easier to view on smaller screens.
    
*   More flexibility, allowing you to drag and drop tasks to different days, swipe through grids to view tasks, and do much more.
    

### [How to Switch to the Grid Layout in Week View?](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#how-to-switch-to-the-grid-layout-in-week-view%3F)

Just switch your calendar to Week View and tap the layout icon at the top to toggle to the new grid layout.

> Tip: The grid layout for Week View is available on mobile only. On desktop, you can use the multi-week view as an alternative.

[🍎 Now Adapted for iOS 18! Ready to Upgrade? (Sep 16th)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#%F0%9F%8D%8E-now-adapted-for-ios-18!-ready-to-upgrade%3F-(sep-16th))

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Control Center Controls](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#control-center-controls)

iOS 18 now allows third-party app controls to be added directly to the Control Center.

TickTick offers 8 controls for you to choose from! These controls let you quickly access specific app pages or start/stop focus, streamlining your workflow.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

How to add them?

Pull down the Control Center, tap the "+" icon in the top-left corner, then click "Add a Control." Search for "TickTick" to view and add its controls.

### [iOS 18 Tinted Mode Adapted](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#ios-18-tinted-mode-adapted)

TickTick's icon and controls are now fully adapted to iOS 18's Tinted Mode.

Bored with your current home screen? Now you can personalize it to fit your style!

### [watchOS 11 Adapted](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#watchos-11-adapted)

With the release of watchOS 11, TickTick now delivers a fresh experience on your Apple Watch!

*   Live Activities

Start live activities on iOS, and watchOS 11 will sync them seamlessly to display status updates in Smart Stacks, making multi-device management even more streamlined!

*   Interactive Controls

In Smart Stacks and on the watch face, you can quickly complete tasks by tapping the checkboxes on task and habit controls. Task completion has never been more convenient!

*   Double-Tap Action

When using TickTick on your watch, you can double-tap with your fingers to add or complete tasks, making operation faster!

⚠️ Please note: This feature is only available on devices that support double-tap functionality.

[✅ From Capture to Organization: Task Workflow Optimization (Aug 31st)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#%E2%9C%85-from-capture-to-organization%3A-task-workflow-optimization-(aug-31st))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Enhanced Task Addition Experience](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#enhanced-task-addition-experience)

The task addition toolbar is now customizable. You can place frequently used features at the forefront while moving less commonly used options into the "More" section.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

### [Improved Custom Recurrence Feature](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#improved-custom-recurrence-feature)

You can now select specific dates and set a recurring frequency of every \_\_ years, making yearly repetition more intuitive and convenient!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

(Not yet supported on PC & Mac.)

### [Optimized Section Deletion](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#optimized-section-deletion)

When deleting a section, you now have the option to either "Delete the Section and Tasks" or "Delete the Section and Move Tasks to," making it easier to preserve tasks from the deleted section.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

### [Enhanced Task Comments](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#enhanced-task-comments)

Task comments now support image attachments, adding more variety to your comments.

### [Improved Task Dragging in Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#improved-task-dragging-in-calendar)

You can now drag the edges of task blocks in the calendar on desktop to set them as multi-day tasks or adjust the time span across days, making task scheduling more convenient.

(Not yet supported on Mac.)

[⬆️ Desktop Version 6.0: Embrace a New Efficiency Level (Jul 2)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#%E2%AC%86%EF%B8%8F-desktop-version-6.0%3A-embrace-a-new-efficiency-level-(jul-2))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Task and Calendar in One View](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#task-and-calendar-in-one-view)

Now, tasks and calendar can be displayed in a single interface. You can view all tasks and scheduled events without switching tabs!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

Key Feature: Drag tasks to the calendar to easily arrange them. This helps you capture and organize tasks on one page, greatly enhancing efficiency!

### [Agenda View](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#agenda-view)

Loved the List Calendar View Timeline in the mobile version 7.0? Now, we have the Agenda View in Desktop Version 6.0!

All scheduled tasks can be displayed on a timeline, and you can easily scroll through all events with your mouse wheel!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

### [Enhanced Input Experience](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#enhanced-input-experience)

### More Efficient Task Addition

*   Add Description: While adding a task, press the shortcut "Shift + Enter" to quickly input a description, completing both task and description in one go!
    
*   New Input Box Style: The input box now supports style switching. The new style helps you set task dates, priorities, lists, and other attributes more quickly.
    

### Enhanced Editing Experience

*   Editing Menu: When editing text in task details, selecting the text will display the editing menu, reducing steps and allowing quicker formatting like bold and highlight!
    
*   Command Menu: Type "/" in the task details page to bring up the command menu. You can quickly set headings, bullet lists, and insert attachments or subtasks without using the mouse, enabling an immersive writing experience!
    

### [Upgraded Habit Module Experience](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#upgraded-habit-module-experience)

### New Visual Design

*   Habit Homepage: The habit homepage has a brand-new design, allowing you to choose between "list" or "card" styles.
    
*   Habit Check-In Styles: You can change the completed check-in style in the habit calendar to habit icons, making your interface more aesthetically pleasing.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

### Date Filter

*   Date Filter Function: If you have many habits, click the top date to filter and quickly check in the habits you need for the day.

[Major Updates! Sync tasks with Google events (May 28)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#major-updates!-sync-tasks-with-google-events-(may-28))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now you can Integrate Google Calendar in "Settings > Integrations & Import" to see your TickTick tasks in the Google Calendar.

After integrating, tasks added in TickTick will sync with Google Calendar, and any task changes will be reflected in both.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

Operation Guide: [Integration with Google Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781593733922816)

[Speed upgrade! View tasks faster💨 (Apr 22)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#speed-upgrade!-view-tasks-faster%F0%9F%92%A8-(apr-22))

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [New features for iOS：Live Activity](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#new-features-for-ios%EF%BC%9Alive-activity)

Important tasks are supported pinning to the lock screen for quick access!

How to use: Tap "More" in the task detail page or long-press the task in the task list page, then select "Add to live Activity".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

### [New features for PC：Mini Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#new-features-for-pc%EF%BC%9Amini-calendar)

How can you swiftly view tasks for a particular day within task lists? Just click on the Mini Calendar in the sidebar, and you can easily achieve it!

To enable: Head to Settings > More Settings > Mini Calendar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408)

Other optimizations

*   For Android tablet: Kanban is displayed in a multi-column format, enabling users to browse multiple groups simultaneously.
    
*   For PC summary feature: It now supports displaying "Calendar Events" and "Habits", and includes additional content like "Tags" and "Parent Tasks" to enhance the comprehensiveness of your summaries. Additionally, it offers "Summary Templates" to streamline your review process.
    
*   New command menu for Mac: Access the Command Menu with a simple key combination of "⌘+K", enabling seamless navigation to various major functional modules within the application by typing their names.
    

[Feature Update! Enhancements Across All Platforms ⬆️ (Mar 5)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#feature-update!-enhancements-across-all-platforms-%E2%AC%86%EF%B8%8F-(mar-5))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Tablet UI Enhancements](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#tablet-ui-enhancements)

Exciting news for our tablet users! We've implemented several upgrades to improve your experience:

*   The task detail page will now intelligently switch between split column or pop-up style depending on your usage scenario.
    
*   The navigation bar on Android tablets has been optimized to display on the left side from the bottom, providing easier access to more content.
    
*   Easily switch between different views on the calendar page for seamless scheduling.
    

### [Enhanced Apple Watch Experience](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#enhanced-apple-watch-experience)

We've introduced a significant update for Apple Watch users! The homepage layout has been optimized to make the header lighter and display more tasks. Additionally, we've introduced a new Focus module, enabling quick access to focus mode with a simple swipe to the left.

### [New Long-Press Actions for Calendar View](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#new-long-press-actions-for-calendar-view)

In Day / 3Days / Week view, you can now perform “Done”, “Delete”, “Duplicate” operations by simply long-pressing on a task, making it more convenient to manage your tasks.

### [Support for Moving Entire Sections](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#support-for-moving-entire-sections)

Tired of moving individual tasks within a section? Now, you can easily move the entire section by long-pressing on the section or clicking the “...” button on the right side. Streamline your task organization by moving entire sections to other lists effortlessly.

### [Customizable Reminder Notifications for Android](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7301088783166865408#customizable-reminder-notifications-for-android)

Want to customize your reminder notification bar by replacing the “Done” and “Snooze” buttons? Head to Settings > Sounds & Notifications > Notification & Status Bar to tailor the notification bar buttons to suit your preferences!

Currently available on Windows app only.

# ⏳ Countdown

⏳ Countdown
===========

In the fast-paced rhythm of life, there are always special days you don't want to forget—or rush through. TickTick's Countdown feature helps you thoughtfully record each important moment.

🎂 **Anniversaries** — Celebrate the moments that matter: falling in love, getting married, birthdays, the day you brought your pet home... Each year, these dates mark a time to cherish. TickTick will remind you right on time, so you can fully embrace these special occasions.

⏳ **Countdowns** — Count down to every moment you’re looking forward to: a trip, an exam, a performance, a goal achieved... Watching the days tick down fuels your motivation and builds a sense of joyful anticipation. TickTick helps you plan each step, making preparation smoother and more intentional.

📌 Perfect for:

*   Those who don't want to miss important dates
    
*   Those who love to plan ahead and prepare surprises
    
*   Those who need countdowns to stay motivated toward goals
    
*   Those who want to add more meaning and celebration to everyday life
    

These days may not always be the most urgent, but they are often the most heartwarming. Anniversaries help you honor the past; countdowns help you look forward to the future. One reminds you to treasure love, the other keeps you moving toward your dreams.

Start adding your important days now!

👉 [Add Countdowns](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408)

👉 [Customize Your Countdowns](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534550377070592)

👉 [Manage Your Countdowns](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534343065206784)

---

# Updates in 2023

Updates in 2023
===============

[Don't Miss Out! 💻 Experience New Windows Features (Dec 6)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#don't-miss-out!-%F0%9F%92%BB-experience-new-windows-features-(dec-6))

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Focus Mini Window](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#focus-mini-window)

Our all-new Mini Window feature unveils two trendy styles - "Circular" and "Minimalist." You can effortlessly slide them to the screen edges for a clutter-free experience, ensuring they won't obstruct your view anymore!

### [Independent Window](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#independent-window)

Have you ever dreamt of managing your lists and calendar side by side? Now, with TickTick's Independent Windows support, you can seamlessly make that dream a reality. Just right-click and choose "Open in a new window" to access this fantastic feature!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [Custom Fonts](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#custom-fonts)

Looking to elevate the visual appeal of your TickTick experience? Now, you can infuse your unique style by selecting your favorite font in "Settings" - "Appearance" - "Display".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

[💻 Desktop Version 5.0 is Live! (Nov 15)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#%F0%9F%92%BB-desktop-version-5.0-is-live!-(nov-15))

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Brand New Multi-Day & Multi-Week Views](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#brand-new-multi-day-%26-multi-week-views)

With version 5.0 comes a fresh multi-day view, allowing you to flexibly display schedules for 1 to 14 days according to your preferences, accommodating various short-term plans.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

The all-new multi-week view supports switching between schedules for 1 to 6 weeks. Opting for a 2-week or 3-week view can address the issue of grid display shortcomings when dealing with a higher volume of daily tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [Enhanced calendar view](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#enhanced-calendar-view)

Scroll up and down freely in the monthly view and swipe left or right in the weekly view for intuitive schedule browsing.

### [Enhanced List Addition Experience](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#enhanced-list-addition-experience)

Now, when adding a list, you can directly choose a view and preview the view style without the need to switch again within the list.

Other Optimizations

*   A fresh, cleaner, and lighter UI.
*   Redesigned reminder pop-up and setting interface for a lighter, user-friendly experience.

[Smooth New Experience! 📱 Mobile version 7.0 is officially launched (Nov 8)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#smooth-new-experience!-%F0%9F%93%B1-mobile-version-7.0-is-officially-launched-(nov-8))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After much anticipation, version 7.0 is finally here! Check out the highlights below:

### [Brand New Task Popup Style](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#brand-new-task-popup-style)

Considering that task details often contain minimal text, we boldly transformed the task details page into a task popup. This compresses the text area, creating a lighter visual experience.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

Additionally, the popup style enhances the single-handed operation experience—wherever your fingers can reach, the operation menu is right there.

### [Detail menu supports customization](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#detail-menu-supports-customization)

You can choose to put high-frequency operations on top and low-frequency operations away for a smoother and freer experience.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [The List Calendar View Timeline](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#the-list-calendar-view-timeline)

Enable "Show Timeline" in the top-right corner "..." of the List Calendar View, and your day's schedule will be visually connected in a timeline, making it intuitive and convenient for review.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [Month View Supports Vertical Scrolling](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#month-view-supports-vertical-scrolling)

Now, the calendar month view supports vertical scrolling to switch between months, providing more flexibility for viewing and scheduling tasks across different months.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [Redesigned reminder popups](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#redesigned-reminder-popups)

We've redesigned the reminder popups to make them more useful and harmonized. It also supports overlapping of multiple reminder popups, so you can quickly browse missed reminders.

### [Optimized Pomodoro Focus Experience](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#optimized-pomodoro-focus-experience)

Enable "Auto access to Full-Screen Mode" in "Focus Settings", and you will automatically enter Full-Screen focus mode 5 seconds after starting focus, reducing the tool's presence.

Moreover, in Full-Screen Mode, you can quickly perform actions by tapping the screen, making it even more convenient.

[For Apple Users: New Desktop & Watch Experience (Sep 28)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#for-apple-users%3A-new-desktop-%26-watch-experience-(sep-28))

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [macOS 14.0 Desktop Widgets](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#macos-14.0-desktop-widgets)

After upgrading to macOS 14.0, you can now place TickTick widgets directly on your desktop and interact with them.

### [watchOS 10 Smart Stacks](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#watchos-10-smart-stacks)

Following the watchOS 10 update, our Apple Watch widgets now support displaying on Smart Stacks. Simply scroll the Digital Crown to quickly check your tasks, habits, and more.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

[Adapted for iOS 17's New Features 🍎 (Sep 19)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#adapted-for-ios-17's-new-features-%F0%9F%8D%8E-(sep-19))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Interactive Home Screen Widgets](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#interactive-home-screen-widgets)

Your home screen widgets are evolving beyond mere information displays. With a simple tap on the widget, you can now complete tasks or check off your habits, making your actions both convenient and lightning-fast.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [StandBy](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#standby)

TickTick is now fully compatible with iOS 17's trendy StandBy mode. Personalize your widgets to effortlessly access your task lists and habits, enabling you to immerse yourself more deeply.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [iPad Lock Screen Widgets](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#ipad-lock-screen-widgets)

The beloved lock screen widgets from iOS 16 are now available on iPad's lock screen too! We now offer 10+ distinct styles of iPad lock screen widgets, including tasks, focus, habits, and more. So, go ahead, and equip your iPad for a more efficient lock screen experience!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

[Here it is! Focus Sync Across Devices👏 (Jul 24)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#here-it-is!-focus-sync-across-devices%F0%9F%91%8F-(jul-24))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hey there! 👋 The much-awaited Multi-Device Focus Sync is finally here!

When you start Focus on one device, it will sync and activate Focus mode on your other devices. Similarly, when you pause or end Focus on one device, it will also pause or end on the other devices.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

Pomodoro Focus with More Enhancements

*   Improved Focus White Noise: We've replaced it with higher-quality sounds. Also, we've added "Wooden Fish" white noise to help you achieve a deeper state of focus.

[New Widget 🎯 Track Weekly Progress for Individual Habits (Jul 4)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#new-widget-%F0%9F%8E%AF-track-weekly-progress-for-individual-habits-(jul-4))

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Introducing the new widget! Now, you can easily view the weekly progress of individual habits using this widget.

We offer two styles: 4×2 and 2×2, allowing you the freedom to choose based on your screen space.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

[🔥 Redesigned Kanban View (Jun 28)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#%F0%9F%94%A5-redesigned-kanban-view-(jun-28))

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Smart List, Inbox, Folder, and Tag Support Kanban View](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#smart-list%2C-inbox%2C-folder%2C-and-tag-support-kanban-view)

Great news! The use cases for Kanban View have become more comprehensive and diverse. 🎉

After the upgrade, not only regular lists, but also Smart Lists, Inbox, Folders, and Tags can use Kanban View to manage tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [Mobile Operations Upgrade](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#mobile-operations-upgrade)

A new section tab has been added to the top, making it easier and faster to view and switch between sections.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

Previously, we could drag tasks to the edge of the page to modify their sections. Now, you can also drag tasks directly into the top tab to modify the sections they belong to, making it more flexible and convenient.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

[Meeting Expectations: Focus Floating Window 🍅 (Jun 5)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#meeting-expectations%3A-focus-floating-window-%F0%9F%8D%85-(jun-5))

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here comes the Floating Window! Are you ready to increase productivity? Now, you can easily view your Pomodoro Timer progress from any page!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

Recent Detail Optimizations

*   Time Setting Support: You can choose between the 12-hour time format or 24-hour time format.
    
*   New Background Styles for iOS: When sharing task images, you can now select different background styles.
    
*   Notification Details Option for Windows: You can configure whether or not to display detailed content when receiving reminders.
    

[Sorting Major Upgrade! The Ultimate Task Manager for Mass Tasks ✅ (Apr 18)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#sorting-major-upgrade!-the-ultimate-task-manager-for-mass-tasks-%E2%9C%85-(apr-18))

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Previously, our sorting feature supported sorting by Date, Tags, Priority, and Custom order. However, as the number of tasks in the list increased, the existing sorting features seemed insufficient. To address this issue, we have upgraded it!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

Now, you can experience more than 20 different sorting scenarios combining "Group" and "Sort," helping you manage tasks more easily.

For example, in "Today" list, if we simply sort by Date, work and personal tasks will be mixed together. In this case, selecting to Group by List and Sort by Date allows for a categorized view of upcoming tasks, making it clear at a glance.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

Explore more ways to use it by clicking here 👉 [Manage Tasks with Group & Sort](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

[Optimization: Creating a More Efficient Efficiency Tool 💨 (Apr 1)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#optimization%3A-creating-a-more-efficient-efficiency-tool-%F0%9F%92%A8-(apr-1))

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We have made some adjustments and optimizations to make your use of TickTick more efficient. ✨

### [Directly Input Descriptions When Adding Tasks on Mobile](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#directly-input-descriptions-when-adding-tasks-on-mobile)

Now, you can directly input descriptions when adding tasks! Additionally, when the task is selected, clicking the input field again allows you to directly add images.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [Moving Tasks to Sections Directly on Mobile](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#moving-tasks-to-sections-directly-on-mobile)

Now, you can directly move tasks to the designated section of a specific list, eliminating the need to drag tasks again to modify their sections.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [Real-Time Search Support](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#real-time-search-support)

Previously, when searching for tasks, we needed three steps to reach the task page, which was inconvenient. With the optimization, when we enter the content we want to search for, the search results are displayed in real-time, allowing us to reach the task page more quickly.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

[Upgrade for Desktop Sticky Notes 🆙 (Feb 15)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#upgrade-for-desktop-sticky-notes-%F0%9F%86%99-(feb-15))

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Recently, we have made some optimizations and improvements to our Sticky Notes, making them better integrated into your desktop. We hope you love it! 🎊

Prefer dark mode but only have light-colored Sticky Notes? Now, you can use dark-colored Sticky Notes! Simply click the clothes icon in the Sticky Notes toolbar to switch to different background colors.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

In response to your strong demand, our Desktop Sticky Notes now support adjusting opacity! You can find the option to adjust opacity in "Settings" - "Sticky Notes" - "Opacity."

[New Timer Feature🔍 Streamline Focus on Fixed Tasks (Feb 8)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#new-timer-feature%F0%9F%94%8D-streamline-focus-on-fixed-tasks-(feb-8))

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

During our daily focus time, there are often a few tasks that occur frequently, such as reading or exercising. If you need to focus on tasks scheduled for the day, you have to repeatedly navigate between task lists or calendars.

To optimize this experience, simplify operations, and help you focus on important tasks, we have launched "Timer".👏

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

Now, you can add frequently focused tasks to Timer. When you need to focus, simply open the focus page and click on the corresponding item to quickly start!

Learn more by clicking here 👉 [Timer](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781980423585792)

[A Small Adjustment to Help Alleviate Anxiety 😎 (Jan 28)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#a-small-adjustment-to-help-alleviate-anxiety-%F0%9F%98%8E-(jan-28))

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While continuously bringing you new experiences, we are also responding to some minor adjustments: Now, you can enjoy the satisfaction of crossing off completed items one by one and free yourself from the overwhelming web of "unfinished" tasks, relieving anxiety.☀️

### [Completed Task Strikethrough Style](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#completed-task-strikethrough-style)

Feeling unfulfilled by just checking off completed tasks? Then start striking them off from now on!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [Hide Sidebar Count](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#hide-sidebar-count)

Feeling anxious with the increasing number of pending tasks? Hide the task count in the sidebar under the "Display" module and say goodbye to number anxiety!👋

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

[Focus Experience Upgrade 🔔 (Jan 10)](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#focus-experience-upgrade-%F0%9F%94%94-(jan-10))

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Another upgrade to the focus experience with two new additions for a more enhanced Pomodoro!🤩

### [New Focus Tab for Desktop](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#new-focus-tab-for-desktop)

We have added a "Focus" tab to the sidebar on the desktop. Now, you can quickly enter the focus state by clicking "Start" on the focus page!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

### [New Pixel Clock Style for Mobile](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080#new-pixel-clock-style-for-mobile)

Looking for more ways to enjoy Full-Screen mode? The adorable Pixel Clock style is here!

![](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7155128685119406080)

After clicking "Start" in the focus tab and entering Full-Screen mode, simply swipe left to switch to Pixel Clock Style.

Other Optimizations and Updates

*   Desktop Tab Sorting: Customize your preferred sorting by clicking and holding the corresponding feature icon to move it up or down.
*   Show Habits in the Timeline: After setting time reminders for habits, they will appear in the corresponding timeline on the calendar, helping you better view your schedule.

Add Countdowns
==============

Time slips by quietly. Have important anniversaries or moments of anticipation ever been forgotten in the midst of a busy life? Add Countdowns to make sure you never miss those meaningful days again.

[Enable the Countdown Feature](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#enable-the-countdown-feature)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Go to **Settings** > **Tab Bar**, find **Countdown**, and tap the **+** icon to turn it on. Once turned on, the Countdown tab will appear in your bottom navigation bar. (upgrade to v7.6.00 and above)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ee9cd188aa8df5959f9dda55c60f6ced.png)

Click your profile avatar, go to **Settings** > **Features**, find **Countdown**, and turn it on. Once turned on, you'll see the Countdown feature in the sidebar. (upgrade to v6.3.00 and above)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/bb5157d94ea29d89aca1dceceb829613.png)

[Add Important Dates](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#add-important-dates)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Open the Countdown tab from the Tab Bar, then tap the **+** icon in the bottom right corner to add a new countdown.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/37cea1faafd9b849b3055a2c4e462806.png)

Go to the Countdown tab in the sidebar, and click the **+** in the upper right corner to add a new countdown.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d558e430f460e0ff53dc0e63349f8fcf.png)

You can choose from four categories of important days to add:

*   **Holiday**: New Year's Day, Christmas, Thanksgiving, Halloween, etc.
    
*   **Birthday**: Birthdays of friends, family, or important people.
    
*   **Anniversary**: Special dates like wedding anniversaries, relationship anniversaries, work anniversaries, etc.
    
*   **Countdown**: Any significant date, such as exams, trips, performances, or goal completion dates. You can fully customize this.
    

### [Recommend](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#recommend)

Not sure which dates to add? Here are some commonly used countdowns and anniversaries to help you get started.

Simply tap the **Recommend** button next to the title field to browse and select from the suggestions.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/17b8f07a58de869a0a54d606410ac1ee.png)

### [Icons](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#icons)

Customize each countdown with a unique icon to make your special days stand out at a glance and add a touch of ceremony.

Mobile

Desktop

Click the icon at the top to set a custom icon for each of your countdowns. You can choose from a variety of recommended icons to make each countdown easy to recognize at a glance.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/789e31f82482615a82f969917c81a1af.png)

Or, you can also switch to emoji or text to customize your icon.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/45560431752cf13395404ab04fd474f4.png)

Click the icon button next to the title field to customize the icon. Choose from a wide range of default icons, or switch to emoji or text mode to match your personal style.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/87fac991ae781d75cc3f5eb2d1f82d64.png)

### [Date](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#date)

Setting an exact date is essential for an accurate countdown. You can track a past event or set a goal for the future:

*   Add an **Anniversary** like your "Work Anniversary" and input your start date to instantly see how many days you’ve been at your job.
    
*   Add a **Countdown** like "Payday" and input the upcoming payment date to track how many days remain.
    

Click the date to set a specific day. Once set, the system will automatically show how many days have passed or how many days remain.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/6b7212937568ecb76ddf125142946b5c.png)

> When adding a **Birthday**, you can choose to **Ignore Year** if you don’t know it or don’t need to track it.

[Never Miss Important Days](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#never-miss-important-days)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Reminder](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#reminder)

Worried about missing a big moment? Set a reminder for your event, and you’ll receive a notification at the time you choose.

Tap into the **Reminder** section to select multiple reminder times or customize how many days in advance and at what time you want to be notified.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/63aae23c6da75bfdd4e8d8ef45c68cc4.png)

For example:

*   Set a **Payday** reminder 3 days in advance to plan for payments, savings, or shopping.
    
*   Set a **Birthday** reminder 7 days ahead to have plenty of time to prepare a gift.
    

### [Repeat](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#repeat)

Some events repeat on a regular basis, such as birthdays, anniversaries, and paydays. You can set up a repeat rule so you don’t need to manually re-add the event.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c6e4d9db9d0dced0feaa5f49bab9444d.png)

> Birthdays and holidays are set to repeat annually by default and cannot be customized.

### [Type](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#type)

Selected the wrong type? Tap "Type" on the Add page to switch it. Your existing info won't be lost.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/2c7caea5e5ceb44917d749668a18e4f4.png)

### [Counting Mode](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#counting-mode)

Want to customize the counting mode for your anniversaries? For past dates with repetition (such as a yearly wedding anniversary), you can tap the **Counting Mode** button to select the display mode:

*   **Countdown**: Shows "XX days until XX" Example: "100 days until the wedding anniversary"

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/68056e7c632f6263afd857b4032afee7.png)

*   **Count Up**: Shows "It's been XX days since XX" Example: "It's been 100 days since the wedding"

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3e455523e87012a49cad6f9c722228a5.png)

Why don't I see the Counting Mode option?

The Counting Mode option will be hidden when a countdown anniversary is set to a future date (such as next year's exam) or is not set to repeat.

### [Day Calculation Mode](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#day-calculation-mode)

Prefer a specific way of counting days? For Anniversary-type countdowns, you'll see an option called Day Calculation Mode. You can choose whether the selected date should be counted as Day 1, allowing the countdown to match your preferred way of counting days.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408)

### [Show Age](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#show-age)

When you add a "Birthday" countdown, you'll see a "Show Age" toggle. Turn it on to display the exact age right on the anniversary—easy and convenient.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/6caabfc12e420a035424e94fce4c9acb.png)

### [Show in Smart List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#show-in-smart-list)

Want your important dates to integrate naturally into your daily planning? Countdowns can sync with your Smart Lists, helping you stay aware without interrupting your workflow.

Tap into **Show in Smart List** to set how you want the countdown to appear:

*   Show on the day
    
*   Show 3 days early
    
*   Show 7 days early
    
*   Always show
    
*   Do not show
    

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/4248c7f2d317c3d13622dc82c96f5536.png)

### [Show on Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#show-on-calendar)

In addition to the countdown list, your events can also appear on your calendar. Birthdays, anniversaries, project deadlines — all seamlessly integrated into your daily schedule.

Mobile

Desktop

On the Calendar page, tap **...** in the top right corner, open **View Options**, and enable **Show Countdown**. This way, your special days naturally blend into your everyday planning.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/64c1056ba53116718ddfd7b195cf0891.png)

Click **...** in the top right corner of the Calendar, open **View Options**, and enable **Show Countdown**. Now your countdowns will appear clearly amidst your busy schedule.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/f4d43601e1fc43efa3d4c575c91b7990.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/99ab08b680b8391862a410ff3fc41620.png)

### [View on Home Screen](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322524237753745408#view-on-home-screen)

Important days deserve to stay in sight. Add your countdowns to the home screen with a widget, so those special dates are always visible and gently remind you every day.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/917667f0eb9644a5d592ff97768835af.png)

[How to add widgets?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752#how-to-add-widgets%3F)

⏳ Countdown

Customize Your Countdowns
=========================

Each countdown captures a special moment. Design a unique visual style for your important days, making every day of waiting filled with warmth and anticipation.

[Set Style](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534550377070592#set-style)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Countdown events support customizable styles. You can choose a favorite look for each countdown, making it stand out beautifully in your list and adding a sense of ritual to every important day.

Mobile

Desktop

To customize your countdown's style, open it and tap the **Style** button at the bottom right corner.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/96ad642ffe2151388fecbe541a98585c.png)

Hover over a countdown card, click the **...** in the top right corner, and select **Style** to open the style settings.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/27a638f9d471e7957caaf00c0dce8f5f.png)

[Rich Styles](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534550377070592#rich-styles)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TickTick offers a rich selection of styles to match different moods and occasions. Whether you prefer something minimal and clean, warm and cozy, fun and playful, or bold and vibrant, you'll find a style that fits just right.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ecf1b063127aa62a14d1cfee56acb887.png)

[Custom Color](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534550377070592#custom-color)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After choosing a style, you can further personalize it by selecting a custom color scheme. Adding your own color touch makes each countdown feel even more personal and instantly recognizable at a glance.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/bac9267e44415d86693a54fb31a2b8b4.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/a7758dade8f7f1b1bae5e088df8d9153.png)

[Edit Image](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534550377070592#edit-image)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you select an image style, you can also upload your own background image, giving each countdown a unique story and emotional touch.

Mobile

Desktop

After choosing an image style, switch to the **Image** tab to either select a provided image or upload your own, making each countdown more vivid and personal.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5048a1f7b674ce65b53424f26dd6b63b.png)

In the style editing window, click **Edit Image** to upload a new background, making your countdowns even more vivid and meaningful.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/be171be34369110ac39e49c4d2b7b46d.png)

After setting styles for your countdowns, your page will feel more colorful, personal, and lively.

[Switch Between Days, Weeks & Years](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534550377070592#switch-between-days%2C-weeks-%26-years)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you see "Married for 2,000 days," you might also want to know how many years or weeks that is.

Mobile

Desktop

Open a countdown and tap the number of days in the details page. You can quickly switch between days, years, and weeks to get a clearer sense of how time has passed.

Click the number of days on the countdown card to quickly switch between days, years, and weeks. Using different units helps you get a clearer sense of how time passes.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/aa6fc8fb5c36b75aeb3fb7c92135c111.png)

[Add Notes](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534550377070592#add-notes)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Want to record a small story about that day, or leave a reminder for yourself? On the countdown details page, tap the note icon in the bottom-left corner to add a note for that day.

When writing a note, tap Insert Time in the bottom-left corner to quickly insert the current time. You can also choose whether to Show on Details Page, so important information is visible at a glance.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534550377070592)

[⏳ Timeline View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780375439605760)

[💻 Cross-Platform Support](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780388337090560)

[🌮️ Widgets](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780404896202752)

[📝 Desktop Sticky Notes](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780431722971136)

[⌨️ Desktop Shortcuts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776)

How to Share a List
===================

[Shared List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520#shared-list)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Only regular lists that you create yourself can be shared. Smart lists such as Today, Tomorrow, and Next 7 Days, as well as the Inbox, do not support sharing or collaboration.** Before sharing, create a new regular list specifically for collaboration.

Next, go to the list details page, tap the **…** menu in the top-right corner → select **Share**/**Collaborate** → tap **Invite Member** to invite others to join the shared list.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520)

[Invite New Members](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520#invite-new-members)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two ways to invite new members:

*   Contact invitation: Enter the contact's email address and press enter to send an invitation. An email account that has not registered with TickTick can activate sharing by clicking the link in the email. You can also choose one or more contacts from Recent Invites displayed to invite.
    
*   Link invitation: Click to create a sharing link and copy it to send to others.
    

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520)

[Accept Invitations](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520#accept-invitations)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After receiving an invitation, the invitee can enter the Notifications center to view it. By selecting "Accept," they can join the Collaborate feature.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781706355179520)

🤝 Collaboration

Manage Your Countdowns
======================

Keep every countdown organized and clear, so you’ll always have a perfect view of your upcoming moments.

[Show Group](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534343065206784#show-group)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you add more and more countdowns, managing and browsing them can get tricky. To make it easier, tap the "..." icon in the top right corner of the countdown homepage to enable **Show Group**. Once enabled, all your dates will be automatically grouped by type: Countdown, Anniversary, Birthday, and Holiday.

Mobile

Desktop

You can switch between groups by tapping the group names at the top or by swiping left and right, making management more efficient and organized.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/7d83a2826b39c92940c0559737a44a08.png)

As you add more countdowns, managing and browsing them can become challenging.

To improve this, click the "..." icon in the top right corner of the countdown homepage to enable **Show Group**. Once enabled, all dates will be automatically grouped by type: Countdown, Anniversary, Birthday, and Holiday.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e3fef9688f52bde456373b683b5a566f.png)

You can switch between groups by clicking the group names in the top left corner, making management more efficient and organized.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/fb8311915c06bf6a1748d1a8bca833fd.png)

[Edit](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534343065206784#edit)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

Want to change the name of a countdown? Entered the wrong date? Need to adjust the type or counting mode? No worries — you can easily edit anytime to keep your information accurate and up-to-date.

Mobile

Desktop

Open the countdown anniversary page, tap the "..." in the top right corner, then select **Edit**. You can quickly update the icon, name, date, reminder, repeat, type, counting mode and more.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/6b7d6af7253eb53643e71ddb8569ba67.png)

Right-click or click the "..." in the top right corner of the countdown anniversary card, then select **Edit**. You can modify the icon, name, date, repeat, type, counting mode, reminders, and more for flexible adjustments.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5bd8e14bf31d697ee04f92cbf228374a.png)

[Pin](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534343065206784#pin)

------------------------------------------------------------------

Project deadlines, exam dates, wedding countdowns... Want your most important countdowns always at the top of your list?

Mobile

Desktop

Tap on the countdown, then tap the **...** in the top right and select **Pin** to keep the countdown at the top of your list for easy access.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ac0fd9b94d8adfd2a9a0dbe8dbe1c5ec.png)

Hover over the countdown card, then click the **Pin** button at the top right to keep it at the top of the list for easy access.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/1b161f001d7a663d02b189630f9f612d.png)

[Archive](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534343065206784#archive)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------

Finished a countdown but want to keep the memory? You can archive it — preserving your important moments without cluttering your main list.

Mobile

Desktop

On the countdown detail page, tap the **...** in the top right, then select **Archive** to move it to the **Archived** section, keeping your main list tidy.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/63a0edb064c32e495fad406c83adc4f0.png)

Right-click or click the **...** in the top right corner of the countdown card and select **Archive** to move it to the **Archived** section, keeping your main list tidy.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5bd8e14bf31d697ee04f92cbf228374a.png)

How to view archived countdowns?

Mobile

Desktop

To view archived countdowns, go to the Countdown page, tap the **...** in the top right corner, and select **Archived** to view them.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d3beb0e322f6af9f343ba627ad44178e.png)

Click **Countdown** at the top left corner of the page and switch to **Archived** to view all your archived memories.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/bfc8f33a72c2dadddb467fbd54f6fddc.png)

How to unarchive a countdown?

Mobile

Desktop

To unarchive a countdown, go to the **Archived** page, select the relevant countdown, tap the **...** in the top right corner, and tap **Restore**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/371268f23a74243fd68ffb326654c6b5.png)

To unarchive a countdown, hover over the archived countdown you wish to restore, click the **...** in the top right corner, and select **Restore**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/f6f62222008c566e922bd10a5d4ffaa4.png)

[Delete](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534343065206784#delete)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

Canceled countdowns or no longer needed countdowns? You can delete them permanently to keep your list clean and focused.

Mobile

Desktop

On the countdown detail page, tap the **...** in the top right, then select **Delete** to free up space in your countdown list.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/6b56dbac9897d374ea3334026b9ad23f.png)

Right-click or click the **...** in the top right corner of the countdown card, select **Delete,** and free up space in your countdown list.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5bd8e14bf31d697ee04f92cbf228374a.png)

[FAQs](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7322534343065206784#faqs)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

Can I swipe on countdowns?

Yes! In the countdown list, swipe left on a countdown to quickly pin, archive, or delete it.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/a3f24136e3669ffdae50d54551d3839a.png)

Can I pin multiple countdowns at once?

Currently, only one countdown can be pinned, and the rest will be sorted by time.

Can I recover a deleted countdown?

Deletions are irreversible. Proceed with caution. If you wish to keep the data, it’s recommended to use the **Archive** feature instead.

Does Countdowns support swipe gestures?

You can swipe countdowns in list view to quickly pin, archive, or delete them for more efficient management.

However, after enabling **Show Group**, swipe actions are no longer available.

Customize Your Countdowns

🤝 Collaboration

Badges
======

Badges are awarded for a particular achievement and give you something to show for your time with TickTick.

The number of hours you have paid for, the number of times you have recommended TickTick to your friends, the number of hours you have used TickTick, the tasks you have completed, the habits you have developed and the number of hours you have focused on can all be automatically redeemed for badges.

There are several types of badges available:

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488)

[VIP](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488#vip)

------------------------------------------------------------------

You will receive a badge of the corresponding level when you have recharged your membership for a total of 1, 12, 24, 36, 48 and 60 months.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488)

[Perseverance](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488#perseverance)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you use the TickTick for a total of 3, 7, 21, 50, 200 or 1000 days, you will receive a medal of the corresponding level. Each day you open the TickTick, you will be considered to have used Use.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488)

[Get Things Done](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488#get-things-done)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can earn a badge of the corresponding level by completing a total of 5, 10, 50, 200, 1000, and 5000 tasks. There is a daily cap of 50 badges, over the cap will not be counted in the badge count.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488)

[Mindfulness](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488#mindfulness)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Accumulated concentration time of 25, 100, 500, 2000, 10,000, 50,000 minutes, you will receive a badge of the corresponding level. Both Pomo and Stoptime are counted as valid hours.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488)

[Warm Heart](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488#warm-heart)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With a total of 1, 5, 20, 100, 500 and 1000 successful invitations, you will receive a badge of the corresponding level. A successful invitation is counted when a friend signs up for TickTick.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488)

[Self-Discipline](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488#self-discipline)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Accumulate 3, 7, 21, 100, 500 and 2000 check-ins and you will receive medals at the appropriate level. There is a limit of 10 check-ins per day and any medals above this limit will not be counted.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082279841969471488)

🏆 Achievements

Achievements and Statistics
===========================

Sometimes, it is not enough to know that you have completed a few more tasks this week than last week.

You can't judge whether the efficiency has improved based on only two numbers.

[Achievement Value](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082302534169133056#achievement-value)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Achievement values are directly related to the completion of tasks and task delays. It can scientifically and intuitively feedback whether the efficiency is improved or not, and to a certain extent, it motivates you to plan your daily tasks reasonably and complete them on time.

The more you complete, the higher the achievement value. With the increase of the achievement value and the corresponding improvement of the achievement level, you can also get corresponding rewards for your efforts.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082302534169133056)

TickTick has simplified achievement levels to 12 tiers. Only actions directly related to achieving goals will affect your achievement score, making it more challenging to increase. However, this also means that those who put in the effort will find it easier to stand out from the rest.

[Achievement Value Changes](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082302534169133056#achievement-value-changes)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you achieve your goals, you'll earn corresponding achievement points, such as for adding or completing tasks.

If tasks are left unprocessed or expire, you may lose some achievement points.

Completing tasks on time will give you additional boosts. Achievement points are updated daily at 00:00, not in real time.

To ensure that your achievement points reflect your personal actions, TickTick prevents others' actions from affecting your score in shared lists.

If a task you assigned to someone else is delayed, your achievement points won't decrease.

Similarly, tasks added or completed by others in a shared list won't increase your achievement points.

[Task Completion Trend & Completion Rate](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082302534169133056#task-completion-trend-%26-completion-rate)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can intuitively see the trend of the number of tasks completed this day/this week/this month.

In order to help you track efficiency changes, completion rate statistics can help you understand the achievement of your goals.

The ratio of the tasks you actually completed today/this week/this month to the tasks you originally scheduled at the corresponding time is your completion rate.

The TickTick hopes to help you make a summary of this week with a relatively accurate number, instead of looking at how many completed and expired tasks are in "Today" without any pain.

You can clearly see that the completion rate last week is 80%, and the completion rate this week is 90%, so as to urge yourself to plan carefully and complete it on time.
