Integrate Notion
================

TickTick now supports two-way sync with Notion, making task management simpler and more efficient.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

**Effortless Viewing, Efficient Reminders**

Easily sync your Notion database with TickTick to view tasks in lists or calendars and set reminders—never miss a critical deadline again.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

**Flexible Editing, Automatic Updates**

Any changes made in TickTick will automatically sync to Notion, keeping your tasks up to date and boosting management efficiency.

[Add Integration](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#add-integration)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Go to **Settings → Import & Integration → Notion**, and tap **Add Integration**.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Click on your profile picture, go to **Settings**, find **Integrations & Import → Notion**, and click **Add Integration**.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

[Login and Authorization](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#login-and-authorization)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Log in to your Notion account and click **Next** to authorize TickTick's access. You can choose your preferred connection method.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Log in to your Notion account and click **Next** to authorize TickTick's access. You can choose your preferred connection method.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

*   Method 1: Choose **Use a template provided by the developer** to create a new Notion database, with properties automatically linked for easier synchronization.
    
*   Method 2: Choose **Select pages to share with TickTick** to select an existing Notion database. This method offers more flexibility in customizing how properties are synchronized between Notion and TickTick.
    

[Method 1: Use a Template Provided by the Developer](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#method-1%3A-use-a-template-provided-by-the-developer)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Step 1: Choose a List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#step-1%3A-choose-a-list)

Mobile

Desktop

Choose Method 1 **Use a template provided by the developer.** In the **Choose List Page,** select the list you want to link with Notion, then tap **Integrate** to establish the connection.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Choose Method 1 **Use a template provided by the developer.** In the **Choose List Page,** select the list you want to link with Notion, then click **Integrate** to establish the connection.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

### [Step 2: Integration Successful](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#step-2%3A-integration-successful)

Mobile

Desktop

Once Integrated, a new template page provided by TickTick will appear in the private group of your Notion workspace. The content in this list will sync bidirectionally with the database:

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Once Integrated, a new template page provided by TickTick will appear in the private group of your Notion workspace. The content in this list will sync bidirectionally with the database:

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

*   When you create a **New Page** in the database, TickTick will automatically add tasks.
    
*   The **Checkbox, Name, Date, and Description** properties in the database will correspond to the task fields. (You can later modify how these properties are mapped on the detail page of the integrated database in TickTick.)
    
*   Note: Deleting the **Checkbox, Name, Date, or Description** properties from the database will affect synchronization.
    

[Method 2: Select pages to share with TickTick](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#method-2%3A-select-pages-to-share-with-ticktick)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Step 1: Select Pages to Share](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#step-1%3A-select-pages-to-share)

Mobile

Desktop

Choose Method 2 **Select pages to share with TickTick** and select the pages you want to grant TickTick access to.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Choose Method 2 **Select pages to share with TickTick** and select the pages you want to grant TickTick access to.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Please Note:

*   TickTick can only integrate to the pages you’ve allowed access to.
*   For each new integration, in addition to selecting the pages you want to integrate, make sure to also check any pages already integrated. Otherwise, the previously integrated databases won’t sync due to lack of access.

### [Step 2: Select Content to Sync](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#step-2%3A-select-content-to-sync)

Mobile

Desktop

After authorization, you’ll be redirected to TickTick, where the **Integrated content page** will appear.

On the Integrated Content Page, tap **Choose List** and **Choose Database** to choose the list and database you want to integrate. Then, tap **Next** to proceed to the **Integrated properties page**.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

After authorization, you will see the **Integrated content** page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

On the Integrated Content Page, tap **Choose List** and **Choose Database** to choose the list and database you want to integrate.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Then, click **Next** to proceed to the **Integrated properties** page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

FAQ

1.  **Why are some lists missing on the "Choose List" page?**

Only lists owned by you can be Chooseed for integration.

2.  **Why are some databases missing on the "Integrated Database" page?**

Due to Notion's restrictions, only authorized databases will appear on the "Integrated Database" page.

If you've added new databases in Notion after authorization, you will need to reauthorize them to display. You can reauthorize through one of the following two methods:

**① In Notion**

Go to the database details page, tap the **“more"** in the top right, find **Connections**, and tap the **TickTick** authorization page to reauthorize.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

**② In TickTick**

Mobile

Desktop

Go to **Settings → Import & Integration → Notion**, tap **Add Workspace**, and reauthorize to allow TickTick to access the new pages.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Go to **Settings → Integrations & Import → Notion**, and reauthorize to allow TickTick to access the new pages.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

3.  **There is no content on the database selection page?**

When there is no database in the page you authorized, there may be no content on the database selection page. You can go to Notion to add a database. How to add: [https://www.notion.com/help/intro-to-databases#create-a-database](https://www.notion.com/help/intro-to-databases#create-a-database)

### [Step 3: Select Integrate Properties](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#step-3%3A-select-integrate-properties)

Mobile

Desktop

On the **Integrate properties page**, you can skip configuration and simply tap **Integrate** to complete the integration.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

On the **Integrate properties page**, you can skip configuration and simply click **Integrate** to complete the integration.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

After Successful Integration:

*   The 200 most recently edited items in the database will sync as incomplete tasks in TickTick, and 200 incomplete tasks in TickTick will sync to Notion.
*   New tasks, task name changes, and task deletions will sync in both directions. Other actions will not sync.
*   Tasks synced to TickTick will display the following properties from the Notion database on the task details page: Text, Number, Select, Multi Select, Status, Date, Person, Checkbox (up to 4 data points will be shown). This sync is one-way for viewing only, and editing is not supported.

For more two-way sync options, you can enable Task Date, Task Description, and Task Status settings. Once integrated, these options will sync in both directions as per your configuration.

### [Task Date](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#task-date)

Tap the **Task Date** option, and a pop-up will display all the **Date** type properties you’ve added in your database. Select the property you want to display as the task date in TickTick.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

After integrate, the **Date** property in your database will correspond to the task date in TickTick.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

### [Task Description](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#task-description)

Tap the **Task Description** option, and a pop-up will display all the **Text** type properties you’ve added in your database. Select the property you want to display as the task description in TickTick.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

After integrate, the Record property in your database will correspond to the task description in TickTick.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

### [Task Status](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#task-status)

Tap the **Task Status** option, and a pop-up will display all the **Status, Checkbox**, and **Select** properties you’ve added in your database. Select the property you want to display as the task status in TickTick.

**① Select the Checkbox Property**

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Choose the option named "Checkbox" (this is the checkbox property added in Notion). The status of this property will correspond to the task status in TickTick, as shown in the image below:

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

*   Tasks with an unchecked checkbox in the database will appear as "Incomplete" tasks in TickTick.
*   Tasks with a checked checkbox in the database will appear as "Completed" tasks in TickTick.
*   Marking tasks as "Completed" in TickTick will also update the checkbox status in the Notion database.

**② Select the Single Select or Status Property**

Choose the option named "Status" (this is the status property added in Notion). Since this option includes multiple statuses, you can select which statuses will sync as "Incomplete" and "Completed" tasks in TickTick.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

After selecting the Incomplete option, you'll see the "Incomplete Default" setting below it. This allows you to define how "Incomplete Tasks" in TickTick are marked in Notion. The same applies to the Completed option.

**Note:** Any unselected options will default to syncing as "Incomplete Tasks" in TickTick.

How to Add a Notion Database Property？

In the Notion database details page, tap **More** in the top-**right corner → Properties → New property.**

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

[Integration Results](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#integration-results)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Sync Results](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#sync-results)

Once Integrate, TickTick and Notion will sync based on the properties you’ve set. The initial sync covers the 200 most recently edited items, including incomplete tasks from TickTick syncing to Notion.

Subsequent actions, such as adding, editing, or deleting tasks, will also sync automatically to ensure your most recent updates are reflected in both platforms.

### [View Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#view-tasks)

You can view the database content in the Integrate list within TickTick and visually track tasks using the calendar view.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Tap on a task to view its details, where you'll see a "**Notion**" card displaying key information. Tap the "**Go to View**" button to quickly navigate to the Notion app.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

*   The card displays properties from the database, including **Text, Number, Select, Multi-Select, Status, Date, Person**, and **Checkbox**. To ensure functionality of other actions on the task details page, a maximum of 4 properties are shown. The displayed properties and their order follow the data transmitted from Notion. Viewing is supported, but editing is not.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/51f8b8088ce7729b04f86be3ea2481b6.png)

*   If the above properties have no content, they will not appear on the card.
    
*   Properties configured on the **Integrated properties** (such as Task Date, Task Description, or Task Status) will not be displayed on the card, as they are already mapped to their respective fields.
    

### [Edit Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#edit-tasks)

In the Integrate list within TickTick, changes to the task name and properties configured on the **Integrated properties** will automatically sync to the Notion database.

[Remove](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120#remove)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1\. Remove Workspace**

Mobile

Desktop

Go to **Settings → Import & Integration→ Notion**, tap **TickTick**, and on the details page, tap Remove at the bottom to successfully remove the workspace.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Go to **Settings → Integrations & Import**, click to enter the **Integrated** Notion workspace, then click the "..." in the top-right corner and select **Remove** to successfully remove the workspace.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

*   After Remove, all content will stop syncing bidirectionally, but previously synced content will remain intact.

**2\. Remove Database**

Mobile

Desktop

Go to **Settings → Import & Integration → Notion**, tap on **TickTick**, select the database you want to remove, tap **More** in the top-right corner and choose **Remove** to complete the process.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Go to **Settings → Integrations & Import**, click to enter the **Integrated** Notion workspace, then select the database you want to remove.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

In the top-right corner, click the "···" and choose **Remove** to complete the process.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

*   After remove, all content will stop syncing bidirectionally, but previously synced content will remain unchanged.

1\. How to Add a Database?

Mobile

Desktop

Open a new or existing Notion page, click "+", find the database, and select the desired database view. This will add the database to your page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

Open a new or existing Notion page, type “/,” then type “database,” and select the appropriate database view to add it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7263009660070789120)

2\. What are Database Properties?

Database properties help you manage the content within the database, such as due dates, text, and more.

[https://www.notion.com/help/database-properties](https://www.notion.com/help/database-properties)

3\. Can I integrate multiple Notion workspaces?

Yes, you can integrate up to 3 workspaces.

4\. Can I integrate databases from multiple Notion workspaces?

Yes, you can integrate up to 5 databases.

Suggested Tasks
===============

When you have a long list of tasks but don't know where to start, try Suggested Tasks. It categorizes your tasks based on their creation time, modification frequency, due date, and other factors — helping you quickly decide what to start today.

[Find Suggested Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616#find-suggested-tasks)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

In the **Today** Smart List, tap the 💡 button in the upper-right corner and choose **Suggested Tasks** to view your suggestions.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616)

In the **Today** Smart List, click the **Suggested Tasks** button in the top-right corner to view your suggestions.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616)

[View Suggested Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616#view-suggested-tasks)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Based on your task data — such as when they were added, how many times their due dates have been changed, and their due dates — there are four sections in Suggested Tasks.

### [Recently Added](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616#recently-added)

Worried about forgetting tasks you just added but haven't scheduled yet? In **Recently Added** section, you can view tasks created **Just now**, **Today**, or **Yesterday** that don't have a scheduled time.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616)

Quickly review these new items and schedule those that need to be handled soon in Today.

### [Postponed Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616#postponed-tasks)

Do you have tasks that you've postponed again and again without completing? In **Postponed Tasks**, tasks are sorted by how many times their dates have been changed — from highest to lowest.

Tap **Postponed Tasks** to view tasks postponed **Over 5 times**, **Over 3 times**, or **Over 2 times**, and prioritize those that have been delayed too many times.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616)

### [Long Overdue](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616#long-overdue)

Some tasks were created long ago but never completed? In **Long Overdue**, you can view tasks that have been created for **Over 7 days**, **Over 14 days**, or **Over 30 days**.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616)

Browse these long-pending items and move the ones you still want to pursue to Today.

### [Upcoming](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616#upcoming)

Already finished today's tasks and still have time left? In **Upcoming**, you can view tasks that are due **Tomorrow** or **In 2 days**.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616)

Choose some of them to handle ahead of time and keep your workflow more relaxed and predictable.

[Add to Today](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616#add-to-today)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From the Suggested Tasks list, pick the tasks you'd like to work on today. Click the **+** button beside them to quickly **Add to Today**, without manually copying or editing.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7401564165023727616#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. Do Suggested Tasks include all my tasks? What's the scope?

Suggested Tasks filters out any recurring tasks, tasks already scheduled for today, and completed tasks, then recommends from the remaining ones based on several criteria.

Constant Reminder

Use Siri & URL Scheme with TickTick
===================================

You can add some common operations to Siri as voice commands, and in the future, you can automatically execute them by simply speaking to Siri. Doesn't that sound cool?

If you're used to checking your tasks every morning, you can add "View 'Today'" to Siri shortcuts and record a voice command (such as "What am I doing today?").

Then, whenever you say "What am I doing today?" to Siri, Siri will help you automatically open the TickTick smart list "Today".

[Create Tasks with Siri](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781515422072832#create-tasks-with-siri)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enable "Add tasks via Siri" in "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - "Siri" to create tasks with Siri.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781515422072832)

[Siri & Shortcuts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781515422072832#siri-%26-shortcuts)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add common operations to Siri as voice commands. After setting up, you only need to give a voice command to Siri, and Siri will automatically execute it for you.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781515422072832)

[URL Scheme](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781515422072832#url-scheme)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to the above shortcut commands, you are free to use the URL Scheme we provide to set up your own.

The current TickTick URL Scheme can execute commands such as

*   Add task: add a task called "buy eggs"
*   Show smart list: Show "Today" smart list
*   Search for a task: search for a task containing the word 'meeting'

These instructions will be communicated via a specific link in the format of

> ticktick://v1/command?parameter1=value1&parameter2=value2&...

Opening these links will start the ticktick list and execute the commands. Where:

*   command indicates the type of command, currently the tick list supports "add task", "show" and "search" commands
*   parameter means parameter, e.g. to add a task, parameters include "task title", "start time", "task content", etc.
*   value indicates a specific value, for example the parameter "task title" has the specific value "buy eggs".

For example, if you wanted to display a "Today" smart list, the link would look like the following

> ticktick://v1/show?smartlist=today

Next, you will learn how to use the three commands in detail.

Next, you will learn how to use the three commands in detail.

### [Add Task Command](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781515422072832#add-task-command)

The "Add Task" command supports the x-call-back convention, which means that when you open the TickTick application with the "Add Task" command and successfully add a task, you can return to the application that initiated the command.

There are currently three callbacks supported by the TickTick: x-success, x-error, x-cancel.

Therefore, the specific link format for the "Add Task" command is as follows:

> ticktick://x-callback-url/v1/add\_task parameter1=value1&parameter2=value2&...&x-success={{scheme of next app}}

**The "Add Task" command includes the following parameters:**

*   title: title of the task (required)
*   startDate: start time
    *   format (with time zone): 2018-05-07T18:00:00.000+0000
    *   format (without time zone): 2018-05-07T18:00:00.000 (note: without time zone, it will be parsed according to the current time zone of the device)
*   endDate: end time Format (with time zone): 2018-05-07T01:20:00.000+0000 format (without time zone): 2018-05-07T01:20:00.000 (note: without time zone, it will be parsed according to the current time zone of the device)
*   allDay: whether it is an all-day task
    *   true if it is an all-day task; false if it is not an all-day task
    *   required if startDate or endDate has a value
*   priority: priority
    *   no priority=0; low priority=1; medium priority=3; high priority=5
    *   default=0
*   content: content of the task
*   list: The name of the list to which it belongs
    *   default=inbox
*   subtasks: check items

Example: Add the task "Buy eggs"

> ticktick://x-callback-url/v1/add\_task?title=buy%20some%20eggs&x-success={{scheme of next app}}

Example: Add the task "Buy eggs tomorrow at 6pm" to the "Shopping" list

> ticktick://x-callback-url/v1/add\_task?title=buy%20some%20eggs&startDate=2018-05-08T18:00:00.000+0000&allDay=false&list=shopping&x- success={{scheme of next app}}

After adding a task successfully, if the callback is x-success, the ticktick will return the following parameters for the next x-callback-url directive call:

*   title: the title of the task
*   taskID: the unique identifier of the task

### [Show Command](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781515422072832#show-command)

The specific link format for the "Show" directive is as follows:

> ticktick://v1/show?parameter=value

**The "Show" command includes the following parameters:**

*   smartlist: smartlist name (required)
    *   all=all
    *   today=today
    *   tomorrow=tomorrow
    *   last\_7\_days=next\_7\_days
    *   Assign to me = assign\_to\_me

Example: Showing a "today" smart list

> ticktick://v1/show?smartlist=today

### [Search Command](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781515422072832#search-command)

The specific link format for the "Search" command is as follows:

> ticktick://v1/search?parameter=value

**The "Search" instruction includes the following parameters:**

*   keyword: keyword (required)

Example: Search for all tasks containing the keyword "shopping"

> ticktick://v1/search?keyword=shopping

[⌨️ Desktop Shortcuts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780449171275776)

[🖱️ Desktop Interaction Tips](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7351523697951244288)

[📔 Notes and Summary](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055780476358754304)

[🕐 Smart Recognition](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7081924556310446080)

[🔜 Shortcuts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

Import Apple Health Data
========================

TickTick now supports importing **Apple Health data**, allowing you to view relevant health information in the calendar view to better manage your time and health.

> Health data syncing is available only on iOS (iOS 16 or later), you must update the app to v7.5.20 or later.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/4e362728bf9f8b5be82617a232bdb9bb.png)

[Import Health Data](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7309856263616069632#import-health-data)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to **Settings**, select **Import & Integration**, tap **Apple Health Data**, and elect the health data you want to sync to TickTick.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d235a9d2b55ae66dffe589429320d423.png)

[Display Health Data](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7309856263616069632#display-health-data)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once authorized, your health data will appear in the **Calendar view**.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/4e362728bf9f8b5be82617a232bdb9bb.png)

Tap a session to view detailed health information.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/2a5372b96b3300d4b3952fdbe127e3b6.png)

[Sync Focus Time to Apple Health](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7309856263616069632#sync-focus-time-to-apple-health)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When the Focus Time feature is enabled, your focus sessions in TickTick will sync to the Mindfulness section of Apple Health.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/8f5ecc40dc217412e28ab4d1e5e811e4.png)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7309856263616069632#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

Why can't I see the synced data on my computer?

Currently, health data is available only on iOS and does not support multi-device syncing.

Why isn’t Apple Health data showing up?

1.  Ensure that TickTick has been granted access in Apple System Settings > Privacy & Security > Health.
2.  Reauthorize access: Go to Apple System Settings > Health > Data Access & Devices, remove TickTick’s access, and then reauthorize it.

Does TickTick support syncing all health data?

Currently, only data from the last six months to the most recent records is automatically synced.

Can I customize how health data is displayed?

No, the display format cannot be customized. The data is synced and displayed according to Apple Health records by default.

TickTick MCP

Data Backup and Import
======================

[Backup & Import](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781405648748544#backup-%26-import)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the web version, click the avatar in the top left corner, then go to **Settings > Account > Backup & Import**.

Here, you can:

*   Generate backups of your TickTick data
*   Import existing backups
*   Import tasks from other applications

> Web version: [www.ticktick.com](http://www.ticktick.com/)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781405648748544)

[Import from Other Applications](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781405648748544#import-from-other-applications)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to import tasks from other applications into TickTick, you can click on the top left corner Avatar - "Settings" - "Integrations & Import", select the corresponding application and upload the backup file to TickTick.

iOS

Android

Web

In "Settings" - "Import & Intergration", you can directly import Reminders, Todoist, and Microsoft To Do. Importing more third-party apps needs to be done on the web end.

In "Settings" - "Import & Intergration", you can directly import Todoist, Microsoft To Do, [Any.do](http://any.do/)
, etc. Importing more third-party apps needs to be done on the web end.

You can choose the corresponding app (Todoist, Microsoft Todo, Wunderlist, OmniFocus, Toodledo, iCal, etc.) to upload backup files to TickTick.

Calendar Subscriptions
======================

The calendar has become an indispensable part of our lives, effectively helping us plan our time, organize tasks, and provide timely reminders of important upcoming events.

By subscribing to and integrating third-party calendars to display in TickTick, you can easily achieve automatic updates and synchronization of calendar events, significantly improving the efficiency of time management and scheduling.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781614550253568)

*   [Local Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209482814528421888)
    
*   [Google Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781593733922816)
    , [iCloud Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209479055807086592)
    
*   [Outlook Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209436222337318912)
    , [Exchange Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387581639753728)
    
*   [CalDav Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209388126463066112)
     , [URL Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)
    

Additionally, we also support subscribing to TickTick in other applications.→ [Subscribe to TickTick in Third-Party Calendars](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781574649839616)

Sign Up and Log In
==================

[Sign Up and Log In](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781436309110784#sign-up-and-log-in)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When registering with an email, simply click on the email verification link to complete the registration process.

[Bind Email](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781436309110784#bind-email)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Click "Settings" - "Avatar" - "Nickname" - "Email" to modify your email.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781436309110784)

You may go to our Web app - click on the avatar in the upper left corner - "Settings" - "Account"-"Change Email".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781436309110784)

[FAQs](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781436309110784#faqs)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

What should I do if I forget my password?

If you forget your login password, click "Forgot Password" below the login box on the login page to reset your password.

Enter your registered email on the webpage, click "Reset Password", and then check your email for the reset password link or your phone for the verification code. Follow the prompts to reset your password.

How do I sign out?

Mobile

Desktop

Click "Settings", scroll down to the bottom, and click "Sign out".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781436309110784)

Click the avatar in the upper left corner - "Sign out".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781436309110784)

How to manage login devices?

You can manage your login devices in the "Login Devices" section under "Account" on the web page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781436309110784)

🎨 Appearance
=============

Personal themes and designs not only enhance the user experience but also make opening the app more enjoyable!

Let’s explore how to easily set themes and customize the appearance, making your app stand out!

[How to Set Themes?](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7254750337695744000#how-to-set-themes%3F)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Currently, TickTick supports color themes, seasonal series, city series, photography series, and custom themes.

Mobile

Desktop

Simply go to 'Settings' > 'Appearance' to switch to your favorite theme under 'Theme.'

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d776c1c254b8e870b3ac87cd8f11234a.png)

When you choose 'Custom,' you can select any image on your device as the custom theme background. After selecting an image, you can adjust the Theme Color, Background Text, Opacity, Blurred, and Card Opacity for a more cohesive visual.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ff3d18b1031c48384c7d586761a28edf.png)

If you want the app to automatically switch to dark mode at night, enable 'Auto-Night Mode.'

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5bdd0f4515f54bfdaa7f25cd143b1606.png)

Just click your profile picture, go to 'Settings' > 'Appearance,' and switch to your preferred theme.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/9b9e9fd085366dcbc02a441aba0c26ff.png)

When you choose 'Custom Theme,' you can also select an image for the background.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/74b236d56235a494ca5675661b76ff68.png)

After choosing an image, click 'Options' in the bottom left to customize the Theme Color, Brightness, Blurred, and Opacity for a harmonious look.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/cc8b0ab4061d1467b4d2643477b7af3d.png)

To follow the system and automatically switch to dark mode at night, enable 'Auto switch dark theme according to system appearance.'

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e76d6fe578870b0746339071c197f86d.png)

[How to Set the App Icon?](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7254750337695744000#how-to-set-the-app-icon%3F)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

TickTick offers ten app icons for you to choose from. Go to 'Settings' > 'Appearance' > 'App Icons' to select your favorite icon, adding a personal touch to your TickTick experience.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d9275ebc74f1c2f6b3c2ab9fa8208897.png)

TickTick offers ten app icons for you to choose from. Just click your profile picture, go to 'Settings' > 'Appearance' > 'App Icons,' and select your favorite icon to personalize your TickTick experience.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/4d77caab75b587303ad10fa88e04a9d8.png)

[How to Adjust Font Size and More?](https://help.ticktick.com/external/articles/7254750337695744000#how-to-adjust-font-size-and-more%3F)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

In 'Settings' > 'Appearance' > 'Display,' you can set the font size, choose whether to hide the task count in the sidebar, and completed task style.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/094a53128200b88e3604048b3a1d5a4b.png)

Click your profile picture and go to 'Settings' > 'Appearance' > 'Display' to adjust the font size, choose whether to hide the task count in the sidebar, and set the style for completed tasks.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5b4fe11df6e44d6e6830345035ccb332.png)

Hiding the sidebar task count can help alleviate anxiety about unfinished tasks. If you still want to know the number of incomplete tasks but prefer not to see the note count, you can just enable “Hide Note.”

Setting completed tasks to a strikethrough style can enhance the sense of accomplishment after completing tasks.

Overall, you can choose these display settings according to your preferences.

How to Customize Font?

Currently, TickTick's font follows the system and does not support custom fonts.

How Teams Can Collaborate
=========================

[Assign Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#assign-tasks)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After the shared list is created, any member can assign tasks within it and assign them to specific performers. The assigned member of the task will receive notification reminders in the "Notification Center".

### [Assign Existing Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#assign-existing-tasks)

You can enter the task details page and click on the "Assign" icon in the upper right corner to assign the task.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

You can also assign tasks in bulk on the task list page. Click on the "..." icon in the upper right corner, "Select," and select multiple tasks. Then click on the "..." icon in the lower right corner and choose "Assign to" to assign the tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

### [Assign tasks when creating them](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#assign-tasks-when-creating-them)

Open the task input field and enter the task. Click on the "Assign" icon. Type "@" and select the assignee.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

### [Comment Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#comment-tasks)

After receiving an assigned task, you can use the comment function to add notes or communicate your ideas with other team members.

Enter the task details page, click the "..." button in the upper right corner, select "Comment", enter your comment, and click "done" to add a comment.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

You can leave a message or @ someone in the comment. After a successful comment, the user you commented on or @ will receive a reminder in the "Notifications" center.

[Collaboration Notification](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#collaboration-notification)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Notifications Center](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#notifications-center)

To get real-time updates on changes to shared lists, you can choose to enable notification permissions for the list. When there are changes to tasks, click the notification button in the left sidebar to view message notifications.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

### [Notifications](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#notifications)

TickTick supports setting notification permissions for shared lists.

Mobile

Desktop

Swipe left or long-press the list, select **Edit** → **Notifications**, and enable permissions such as "Complete a task/Undo", "Add a task/note", or "Delete/Move a task/note" for the current list.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

You can set notification permissions for a single shared list by clicking the **Share button** next to the list title (or right-clicking the shared list in the sidebar and selecting **Share** → **Notifications**). Then, enable permissions such as Complete a task/Undo, Add a task/note, and Delete/Move a task/note for the current list.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

### [Reminders](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#reminders)

Mobile

Desktop

Swipe left or long-press the list, select **Edit** → **Notifications** → **Reminder**, and choose to receive reminders for All Tasks, All Tasks (except assigned to others), Tasks Assigned to Me, or No Reminders.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

Right-click the shared list, select **Edit**, find **Reminder**, and choose to receive reminders for All Tasks, All Tasks (except assigned to others), Tasks Assigned to Me, or No Reminders.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

### [Show in Smart List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#show-in-smart-list)

Mobile

Desktop

Swipe left or long-press the list, select **Edit**, and find **Show in Smart List**. Then choose which tasks to display in smart lists such as All, Today, Tomorrow, and Next 7 Days. You can select All Tasks, All Tasks (except assigned to others), Tasks Assigned to Me, or Do Not Show.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

Right-click the shared list, select **Edit**, and find **Show in Smart List**. Then choose which tasks to display in smart lists such as All, Today, Tomorrow, and Next 7 Days. You can select All Tasks, All Tasks (except assigned to others), Tasks Assigned to Me, or Do Not Show.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

[Managing Member Permissions](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#managing-member-permissions)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In a shared list, you can also set editing permissions for list members. Click on the "Members" icon next to the list title to view all members of the list. Click on the "Edit" button next to a member to set their editing permissions. You can set permissions for members to edit, comment, or have read-only access to the list.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

[FAQs](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584#faqs)

--------------------------------------------------------------------

How to view task activities?

Mobile

Desktop

You can find the responsible person for each step of the task in the task activities, and also check all changes made to the task from creation to completion.

*   To view the task activities, go to the task details page, click the "..." button in the right corner, and select "Task Activities".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

How to view List Activities (Web only)?

If you are the project leader, you may need to know the progress of all members and things in the project. In this case, the list activities can meet your needs, as you can see who did what.

On the desktop version, click the “···” in the top right corner of the list and select “List Activities”.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781688281923584)

Do all members need to have a premium account to share a list with multiple people?

No, only the owner of the list needs to have a premium account. The list can be shared with up to 29 members, but non-premium members cannot use premium features.

If I share a list with someone, will all the content in my account be shared with them?

No. Only the content within the shared list will be visible to others. Everything else in your account will remain private.

How to Share a List

# Agenda View - Stringing Tasks by Time

Agenda View - Stringing Tasks by Time
=====================================

TickTick's desktop version 6.0 offers a Agenda View, where all your scheduled tasks are displayed in a linear timeline. You can easily scroll through them using your mouse wheel.

In the Agenda View, you can simultaneously see past completed tasks, current progress, and future plans. This helps you track your daily timeline, adjust plans promptly, and enhance planning and scheduling.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ce9c7e67552f241c7d9f33ce72809e6d.png)

### [How to enable Agenda View?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7213444784319365120#how-to-enable-agenda-view%3F)

Click the view switch option in the top right corner and select 'Agenda View.'

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3637d4e1ea43e7df387d183c1cc46cf1.png)

List View - View Tasks by Day

Calendar View Options

Show Tasks with Calendar
========================

Want to view your task list while scheduling your calendar? Try the Split View feature, which lets you display tasks and calendar side by side. This helps you quickly turn your to-dos into plans, making task management more efficient and organized.

This feature is especially useful in scenarios like:

*   You have many tasks without specific times that need to be quickly scheduled into your calendar;
    
*   You want to keep the context of your task list visible while planning, making it easier to review and adjust.
    

[How to Enable Split View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7358389904469917696#how-to-enable-split-view)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can enable Split View in the following ways:

*   **Right-click the task icon**, then select **Show with Calendar**:

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7358389904469917696)

The calendar will appear on the right side of your task list. This mode is ideal when you want to schedule tasks while keeping the list as your main reference.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7358389904469917696)

For example, if you have your Work task list open with many tasks, showing the calendar side by side lets you consider each task’s priority or urgency as you schedule time.

*   **Right-click the calendar icon**, then select **Show with Task**:

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7358389904469917696)

The task list will appear on the right side of your calendar. This mode suits those who prefer to view their schedule first, then pick tasks to fill available time slots.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7358389904469917696)

For example, when viewing today’s calendar and noticing free time in the morning, you can drag tasks from the adjacent list into the calendar to fill those slots—making sure your day is balanced and productive.

How to close Split View?

Simply right-click the task or calendar module icon and choose **Close Split View** to return to the single module display.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7358389904469917696)

[Drag and Drop Scheduling for Greater Efficiency](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7358389904469917696#drag-and-drop-scheduling-for-greater-efficiency)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With tasks and calendar displayed side by side, you can:

1.  Drag tasks from your list into the calendar.

Quickly assign dates or specific times to tasks without opening each task’s details—just drag and drop.

2.  Drag tasks from the calendar back into the task list area.

Tasks will be moved from their original list to the currently viewed list, while retaining their existing time settings.

3.  Drag tasks onto a list or tag.

Tasks will be reassigned to the target list or automatically tagged accordingly.

4.  Drag tasks onto a smart list.

Tasks will automatically receive the time conditions associated with that smart list, such as “Today” or “This Week.”

Combine your task lists and calendar for easier scheduling and clearer planning!

Calendar View Options

FAQ - Calendar
==============

How to add task on the calendar view?

Mobile

Desktop

*   Click on the "+" sign in the bottom right hand corner to add a task or long press on the all day task bar to add a task.
*   In a view with a timeline, long press on a place in the timeline to add a task at the corresponding point in time.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e13e7726eeaa586a30368f315ceb045c.png)

*   Tasks can be added by clicking on the date grid of the calendar view.
*   In a calendar view with a timeline, click on a place on the timeline to add a task at the corresponding point in time.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/de4ff4f670b452eade2f49b27d9aebbe.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/b2f6cf802e364f55cb3da5a691103f2b.png)

How to arrange tasks on the calendar view?

Mobile

Desktop

*   Swipe left on the right-hand screen edge, or click on "..." - "Arrange Tasks" in the top right-hand corner of the calendar view and drag and drop them into the calendar.
*   Simply drag and drop the tasks in the task bar throughout the day to the corresponding time points on the timeline.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/cb23ee357bb44570a9abb34f660eeaf7.png)

> Habits can't be dragged.

*   Click on the "..." in the top right corner of the calendar - "Arrange tasks"
*   Simply drag and drop the tasks from the all-day task bar to the corresponding time points on the timeline.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c5b72c19b546a58abeb3e9f9f4edba43.png)

How to change the color of the task blocks in calendar?

Mobile

Desktop

Click on the "..." button on the top right of the calendar view, then click on "View Options" > "Color" > "Color By", you can choose the color of the task blocks according to the list, priority or tag.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/51766c2fcae5052bfeb3df20fa2c61d2.png)

Click on the "..." in the top right corner of the calendar view - "View Options"- "Color", and click on the List option.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c49c1d043746b7916b7ed9fa28c05549.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ffc7f8c9608d580228adcfabad58ca33.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c7da6dd9be7556749b047027a64b3721.png)

Why do my tasks not have colors on the calendar view?

The colour that tasks are displayed on the calendar view is determined by the list they belong to. Please remember to set different colours for different lists when creating/managing lists.

How can I adjust the time period hidden in the timeline?

Mobile

Desktop

After expanding the hidden time period, just long press and drag the button up and down.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7063851189372190720)

After expanding the hidden time period, long press and drag the button up and down.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/9c82f11fdc08dde209328ded4941d8c3.png)

How can I quickly adjust the duration of tasks?

Mobile

Desktop

Long press the task block until two dots come out from the top and bottom of the task block, drag and drop to adjust the task duration.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/1977cca0a1ac6db644e460bc6e98a649.png)

Place the mouse on the edge of the task block, and drag and drop to adjust the task duration after the up and down arrow icons appear.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7063851189372190720)

How to enable the Mini Calendar?

This feature is exclusive to the Web & Windows version. First, click on the Avatar - "Settings" - "More" to enable "Mini Calendar", then click on the small arrow at the bottom of the sidebar to show it.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/2c3674f73ab5c12789090576d80ad1af.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/23d718bcbc167df575e9ca44899d9959.png)

How to display Alternate Calendar?

Options include the Korean Lunar, Hebrew, Hijri, Indian, Persian Calendar and Chinese Lunar calendars.

You can enable these in 'Settings' - 'Date & Time'.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7063851189372190720)

How do I change the start day of week in the calendar?

Mobile

Desktop

Click on "Settings" - "Date & Time" - "Week Start on".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7063851189372190720)

Click on your Avatar - "Settings" - "Date & Time" - "Start Week on".

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c7da91c46b8df7f6b4c8bfac9327ebbd.png)

Why can't I see subtasks and recurring tasks on the calendar view?

Click the "..." icon on the top right corner of the calendar view, and check if the corresponding option is enabled.

Can't I see the full calendar in the calendar list view?

In the list view, press and hold your finger on the first row of calendars and pull down to expand a small panorama of calendars.

What else can I do in the timeline on the desktop?

*   You can adjust the timeline scale by using the two-finger zoom on your laptop touchpad.
*   Hold Ctrl/Command and slide the mouse wheel to adjust the timeline scale.
*   "Timeline" supports hiding time periods.

> Click on a hidden time period to expand it, and click on any of the expanded hidden time periods to hide them. After expanding the hidden time period, long press and drag the button up and down to adjust it.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/9c82f11fdc08dde209328ded4941d8c3.png)

Show Tasks with Calendar

Task Details and Editing
========================

[Common Features](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#common-features)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Date and Duration](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#date-and-duration)

Mobile

Desktop

To set a date for a task, go to the task details page and click on "**Date & Reminder**". In the date selection box, switch to "**Duration**" to set a time period task by selecting "**Start Time**" and "**End Time**".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

Right-click a task and choose Date to set it as Today, Tomorrow, Next Week, or a custom date.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

Or, click **Due Date** in the task detail area to set a date and time.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

To add a duration, switch to **Duration** in the date picker, then select a start and end time. You can:

*   Set a duration within a single day, e.g., 9:00–12:00.
    
*   Set a duration across multiple days: click All Day to extend the task over one or more days.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

For more information on how to set reminders and repeats, we have prepared more detailed content for you:

👉 [How to Set Reminders for Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782395743567872)

👉 [How to Set Repeats for Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782206349770752)

### [Move to List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#move-to-list)

Mobile

Desktop

When you have a lot of tasks and want to organize them by work, life, and study, click on "**List**" at the top of the details page to quickly move tasks to other lists. You can also enter the list name to quickly search for it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

Right-click a task and choose **Move to**, or click the **List** field at the bottom of the task detail area to quickly move a task to another list. You can also type a list name to search.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Priority](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#priority)

TickTick provides four priorities for tasks: High, Medium, Low, and None. You can set priorities for tasks based on their importance. Prioritize completing "High Priority Tasks" every day to keep your tasks organized.

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Body (Style and Markdown)](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#body-(style-and-markdown))

Mobile

Desktop

If you have more detailed content to record, you can do so on the detail page.

You can also style text, including "title", "bold", "highlight", "italic", "underline", and other text formats. You can even use Markdown syntax to set input styles.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

When you need to note down key points of a task or make temporary notes on a current event, you can record them in the task details.

Select the text, and you can format it with 'Heading,' 'Bold,' 'Highlight,' 'Italic,' 'Underline,' and other text styles.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

By typing '/', you can quickly set paragraph styles like headings and bullet lists, or insert attachments and add subtasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Tags](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#tags)

Mobile

Desktop

Adding tags to tasks can help us manage them more conveniently. Click the icon in the lower left corner to directly select existing tags or create new ones.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

Right-click a task, or click ... in the bottom-right of the task detail area → Tags. You can choose existing tags or create a new one.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Check Items](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#check-items)

TickTick supports switching between "task text content" and "check items".

Mobile

Desktop

Click the toggle button located just above the right side of the keyboard to switch. In check items mode, a new check item can be created by pressing return.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

Click the toggle button at the top right of the task detail area to switch between description and check items modes.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

Edit and manage check items:

*   Select a check item to edit directly;
*   Click the "Delete" button on the right side of the check item to delete the entire check item;
*   Long press the "≡" on the right side of the check item to drag and sort the check item;
*   When editing the check item, click the clock button above the keyboard to set a reminder time for it.

### [Attachment](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#attachment)

When taking notes, writing logs, or organizing information, we often need to insert images to assist with recording. Currently, TickTick supports inserting images, recordings, files, videos, etc., making note-taking even more smooth and efficient.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

> *   Premium users can upload up to 99 attachments per day, with a limit of 20 attachments per task, and a maximum size of 20M per attachment.
> *   Free users can upload up to 1 attachment per day, with a maximum size of 10M per attachment.

[More Features](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#more-features)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Pin](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#pin)

Too Many High-Priority Tasks, How to Quickly Find the Most Important One?

You can "Pin" important tasks to always display at the top of the list, so you can see at a glance what needs to be done.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

You can share your tasks/notes as text, images, and schedule with friends and colleagues.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Won't Do](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#won't-do)

When handling tasks, there are always some things that you don't want to do, but you don't want to delete them either. What should you do if you want to be able to see them later when you review? You can choose to "Won't Do" this task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

All abandoned tasks can be viewed and managed in the "Won't Do" list in the sidebar, and can also be displayed in the "Completed & Won't Do" section in the task list.

To deal with uncertain situations, abandoned tasks can also be marked as "Restart", and it's okay if there are temporary changes in plans.

### [Comments](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#comments)

In a shared list, we can comment on tasks for team collaboration. In your own exclusive list, you can also use comments as notes.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Copy Link](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#copy-link)

Copy and paste the link of a task to another task, and click the link to jump to the task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Create Duplicate](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#create-duplicate)

If you want to copy a task and make modifications based on the original, you can directly click "Duplicate".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Save as Template](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#save-as-template)

New feature document release, offline event venue setup, promotion video production and distribution...

There are many routine tasks that recur regularly in our daily work. We should consciously summarize these experiences and precipitate them into personal methodology, establish our own rules and order, and directly follow the previous methods when encountering similar things again.

Enter the task details page, click the "..." in the upper right corner - "Save as Template", use the template function to save the regular workflow, and provide reference for future actions.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Task Activities](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#task-activities)

Accidentally deleted the hard-edited text? Not sure who modified the task during collaborative work? In such cases, you can view the history information in "Task Activities".

To view the historical modification information of a task, enter the task details page and click on the "..." button in the upper right corner, then select "Task Activities".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Convert to Note/Task](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#convert-to-note%2Ftask)

Sometimes, you may find that a task is more like a note. Don't worry, TickTick supports converting tasks and notes to each other.

To convert a task to a note, enter the task details page and click on the "..." button in the upper right corner, then select "Convert to Note".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [Start Focus](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#start-focus)

In the "Focus" tab, you can quickly focus on a task without switching to the Pomodoro page.

To start focusing on a task, enter the task details page and click on the "..." button in the upper right corner, then select "Start Focus". Choose a duration in the focus window and click "Start".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

### [How to Edit the Details Page Action Menu?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720#how-to-edit-the-details-page-action-menu%3F)

On the task details page or in the popup, click on the top right corner "..." - "More." Locate the "Edit" option in the bottom left corner to customize the task details action menu.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

Click "-" to unpin, click "+" to pin. Long-press the drag icon on the right and drag it up or down to rearrange the order of various actions.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782408586526720)

Constant Reminder
=================

For important tasks like meetings, exams, or ticket bookings, you don’t want to risk missing them. Constant Reminder keeps notifying you until you take action, ensuring you never overlook critical events.

[How to Enable](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7374017550633402368#how-to-enable)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iOS

Android

Set a reminder time for a task, then turn on Constant Reminder switch.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c49ad0810851bb7cefea0ac2b5a7675f.png)

**Reminder types (iOS 26 and later)**

On devices running iOS 26 or later, you can choose how persistent reminders are delivered:

*   **Alarm Reminder**: Uses the system alarm to deliver persistent alerts
    
*   **Notification Reminde**r: Uses system notifications to deliver persistent alerts
    

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/03ae256f984ef6d072b1e73c47116dd2.png)

**Required permissions**

To use Alarm reminders, TickTick must be granted system alarm permission. If this permission is not granted, alarm-based reminders will not be available.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3d39f17f8dbd7c412069b6c4fd511834.png)

Set a reminder time for a task, then turn on Constant Reminder switch.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/09821fd905a71a00d556ea1f041e42ae.png)

[What to Expect](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7374017550633402368#what-to-expect)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iOS

Android

**System Alarm Reminder (iOS 26)**

When the reminder time arrives, you’ll receive a system-level alarm that continues until you take action.

*   Full-Screen Alert: Displays in full screen on your lock screen.
    
*   Bypasses Silent Mode / Do Not Disturb: The alarm will still ring and vibrate even if your device is in Silent Mode, DND, or Sleep Focus.
    
*   Works Regardless of App Status: The alarm will go off on time even if TickTick is closed or removed from the background.
    

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/00cdfbcac2cb0f34e6ebe66bc8f95f61.png)

*   Snooze: Tap Snooze to temporarily pause the alarm. You can adjust the snooze duration in app settings.
    
*   Close: Tap Close the alarm.
    
*   Power/Volume Buttons: Pressing the power or volume button will automatically snooze the alarm for 9 minutes, just like the native iOS alarm.
    

**Snooze Reminder**

After you set a Snooze Reminder, a Live Activity countdown will appear on your screen. When the countdown ends, you’ll receive another reminder.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/4cc7bf33ef23b1983b03d1012f19db25.png)

> Live Activity Requirements: iOS 16 or later. Make sure the Live Activities permission is enabled: Go to iOS Settings > App > TickTick > Live Activities and allow access.

Why am I not receiving Alarm Reminders?

If you didn’t get an alarm reminder, check the following:

1.  System Version: Make sure your iPhone is updated to iOS 26 or later, since this feature is only supported on iOS 26+.
    
2.  Permission Settings: Confirm that Alarm permission is enabled for TickTick. Go to iOS Settings > Apps > TickTick > Alarm to allow access.
    

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/fd383c2956a84587bd36e11de0f02770.png)

Will Constant Reminders always ring after granting Alarm permissions?

Yes, they will always ring and vibrate. This is a system-level alarm that bypasses Silent Mode / Do Not Disturb, ensuring 100% reliable alerts.

What happens if multiple tasks are due at the same time?

Due to iOS limitations, only one task can appear on the full-screen alarm interface at a time. However, all other task notifications will still be delivered to the Notification Center, so you won’t miss any reminders.

Is the old Constant Reminder still available?

Yes. If you haven’t granted Alarm permissions, TickTick will automatically fall back to the old notification-based reminder system.

**App Notification Reminders (iOS 18 and below)**

If Alarm permissions are not enabled or your device runs below iOS 26, TickTick will use the classic notification reminder method instead.

*   You’ll receive two notifications within one minute, repeating until you take action.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/02394a13636d5c09a9528fe9e4c43c5d.png)

When the reminder time arrives, you’ll receive an app notification alert. The alert will cycle 30 seconds on, 30 seconds off for a total of 5 minutes, and will continue until you take action.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/8757a21b3a6b41706fda8fbf5c523766.png)

Effective Reminder Feature

Suggested Tasks

Desktop

In "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - "Calendar" - "CalDav", enter the "Server Address", "Account", and "Password" of the third-party calendar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209388126463066112)

In "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - "Calendar"- "CalDav".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209388126463066112)

Enter the calendar "Account", "Password", "Server Address", and "Name" that need to be subscribed to, and synchronization can be completed.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209388126463066112)

# Exchange Calendar

Exchange Calendar
=================

If you want to display calendar events from Exchange in TickTick, you can easily achieve this by subscribing to Exchange.

[Adding a Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387581639753728#adding-a-calendar)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Go to "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - "Calendar", select "Exchange", enter your account and password, and after successful authorization, the subscription will be successful.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387581639753728)

Click on your avatar - "Settings" - "Integrations & Import", select "Exchange Calendar", enter your account and password, and after successful authorization, the subscription will be successful.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387581639753728)

Outlook Calendar

CalDav

# Focus Statistics

Focus Statistics
================

For athletes and professional gamers, reviewing and analyzing their performance is almost as important as eating three meals a day. Without tracking and recording events, you will never know where you went wrong and will never be able to improve effectively.

Therefore, while constantly updating your Pomo Records, don't forget to regularly evaluate your historical completion status and consider whether you can do better next time.

In TickTick's Focus Statistics, you can see your daily focus time periods and distribution, making it easy for you to check time distribution and review in a timely manner.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

[Focus Trend Chart](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400#focus-trend-chart)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can view the focus trend by year, month, and week.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

[Focus Timeline](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400#focus-timeline)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The distribution and length of daily focus periods are clear at a glance.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

[Most Focused Time](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400#most-focused-time)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Monthly statistics of your most focused time.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

[Year Grids](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400#year-grids)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

An overview of your focus situation over the year, with the color depth representing the length of your focus time each day.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

[View Statistics](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400#view-statistics)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

On the focus page, click on the statistics icon in the upper left corner to enter the the Focus Statistics page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

On the Focus Statistics page, you can view and manage your focus records.

*   Add Record

Find the focus record and click the + icon on the right to add a record. You can also go to the Focus Record page and click the + icon in the bottom-left corner to add a record.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

*   Filter Records

On the Focus Record page, you can filter records by tapping the options at the top for Date, Duration, or Linked Status.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

*   Delete Record

To delete a record, open the record and tap Delete Record at the bottom.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

*   Bulk Select & Delete All

On the Focus Record page, tap the … menu in the top-right corner to choose Select or Delete All for quick large-scale management.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

*   View Time Spent

At the top of the Details area, you can switch between Day, Week, Month, or a Custom time range to view corresponding focus data. On the right side of the focus ranking, you can view the focus time distribution by List, Tag, or Task, helping you better understand where your time is being spent.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

On the Focus page, you can view some focus statistics on the right side.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/310a99a1f8f110e5b279bbc7ac095a1d.png)

To view more Focus statistics, you can click on the avatar - "Statistics" and switch to the "Focus" tab. There, you can see statistics for the number of Pomos and Focus Duration, both on a daily and weekly basis.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

How to add focus records?

Mobile

Desktop

*   On the Pomodoro page, tap the … menu in the top-right corner and select Add Record to quickly add one.
    
*   You can also go to the Focus Statistics page, find Focus Record, and tap the + icon on the right to add a record.
    
*   Additionally, on the Focus Record page, tap the + icon in the bottom-left corner to add a new record.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

Click on the Focus page, and you can add a focus record by clicking the "+" on the right of the Focus Record.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

How to delete a focus record?

Mobile

Desktop

In "Focus Statistics", enter "Focus Record", enter the record to be deleted, click "Delete Record" in the lower right corner to delete it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

To delete a focus record, click on the corresponding focus task in the Focus Record page to enter the details page, and then click on the delete button in the lower right corner.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781966800486400)

How to display focus records in the calendar?

In the "Calendar" tab, select "View Options" and click to enable "Show Focus Records" to synchronize your focus time blocks in the calendar view.
