Timer
=====

Perhaps you have also made this discovery?

During daily focus, there are usually several commonly used tasks, such as:

👨🏻‍💻For professions: work, language learning, reading

🙇🏻‍♀️For students: homework, vocabulary memorization, general courses

"**Timer**" can help you to concentrate on things more effectively and simplify operations.

[How to Use Timer](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781980423585792#how-to-use-timer)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add things that you need to focus on frequently in your daily life to Timer, such as language learning and exercise.

When you need to focus, open the focus page and click on the corresponding item to quickly start the Timer.

### [Adding Timer](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781980423585792#adding-timer)

Mobile

Desktop

Enter the Focus page, click on the "..." sign in the upper right corner, and add Timer.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/273158c222ace207ff95776b646f5fbe.png)

This way, when you need to focus, press the start button to quickly enter focus mode.

> By clicking on the screen, you can enter Full-Screen and swipe right to experience different styles.

Of course, you can also set a task or habit as a timer.

Here's how to enable it: When adding a timer, click the "Select" button and select the task or habit.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781980423585792)

Enter the Focus page, click on the "+" sign in the upper right corner↗️, and add Timer.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/6b218daf850f869a3465e82bcc1e42de.png)

This way, when you need to focus, press the start button▶️ to quickly enter focus mode.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/e85696da212c185188fbf49bb45468f3.png)

Of course, you can also set a task or habit as a timer.

Here's how to enable it: When adding a timer, click the "Select" button and select the task or habit.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/392f67344380be7e366fc9389e1a970e.png)

### [Choose Different Timer Modes](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781980423585792#choose-different-timer-modes)

You can also create different timer for different focus scenarios.

For example, taking a 45-minute public course, or recording a 10-minute bedtime meditation.

Just select the Pomo Timer mode and the corresponding duration when adding.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/fee4dffd1b801509afff3708a1612fa9.png)

> Each Pomodoro session ends exactly on time when you complete the task, which helps you save time on repetitive operations

Alternatively, if you want to start an immersive reading session without a time limit, you can choose the **Stopwatch** timer mode.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/01e1573a7d7b45d32aefc8626f3fcbce.png)

### [View Focus Data](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781980423585792#view-focus-data)

In addition to starting focus with one click, you can also view weekly, monthly, and yearly statistics on the details page.

> If you need to add a focus record retroactively, you can also click "+ Add Record" directly on this page to add it.

How to view the distribution of focus time for all tasks?

You can access the Focus Statistics page by clicking on the statistics icon in the top left corner of the focus page.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ffba583200ff5c626489c3c3051b31e7.png)

On the Focus Statistics page, click "By Task" to clearly see the pie chart of the time you spent.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/55cc3f12440ff0c8227839bbc3312c0c.png)

### [Return to the Focus Page](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781980423585792#return-to-the-focus-page)

To focus on temporary tasks, click on the "Focus Bar" at the bottom to open the original Focus page.

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781980423585792#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

How to bind tasks or habits as Timers?

You can select the tasks or habits when adding a timer by clicking the "Select" button in the editing bar.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/2dcd8409ad49363279f271660aafe1f8.png)

Your previous Focused Days and Total Focus will also be counted in timers.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/142746588133393ce1a23532a41dc5f8.png)

How Do I Edit, Archive, or Delete a Timer?

Mobile

Desktop

Want to make changes to a Timer? Open it, tap the ⋯ icon in the top-right corner, and choose to edit, archive, or delete it.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/47d68bee2ebce3aa66063b11d6c62475.png)

Need to update or remove a Timer? Right-click it to edit, add record, archive, or delete it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781980423585792)

TickTick MCP
============

[What Is MCP?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#what-is-mcp%3F)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

MCP (Model Context Protocol) is an open protocol that allows MCP-compatible AI clients, such as Claude, ChatGPT, Cursor, and VS Code, to interact directly with external services. Simply put, MCP allows AI to perform actions directly within your apps.

By connecting to TickTick MCP, your AI assistant can read, create, and manage your tasks directly, becoming your personal task manager. You do not need to switch between apps — you can manage your tasks right from the AI chat interface.

For example, you can say to your AI assistant:

*   What tasks do I have today?
    
*   Create a task for me: Prepare meeting materials tomorrow at 3:00 PM, high priority.
    
*   Mark "Buy milk" as completed.
    

The AI will automatically call the appropriate TickTick MCP tools to complete the action.

[Connect to TickTick MCP](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#connect-to-ticktick-mcp)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TickTick MCP supports the Streamable HTTP transport protocol and uses OAuth for dynamic authentication and authorization.

You can connect using the following URL:

    https://mcp.ticktick.com
    

You can connect the TickTick MCP to different AI tools. Below are configuration instructions for common AI clients.

### [Claude Desktop](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#claude-desktop)

> Available on Pro, Max, Team, and Enterprise plans.

1.  Open Claude Desktop and navigate to **Customize** > **Connectors**.
    
2.  Click "+" and select **Add Connector**.
    
3.  Enter the MCP server URL: `https://mcp.ticktick.com`.
    
4.  Click Connect after saving, then follow the on-screen prompts to complete OAuth sign-in and authorization.
    

### [ChatGPT](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#chatgpt)

> Available in beta to Pro, Plus, Business, Enterprise and Education accounts on the web.

1.  Open ChatGPT and go to **Settings** > **Apps** > **Advanced Settings**.
    
2.  Turn on **Developer Mode**.
    
3.  Click **Create App**.
    
4.  Enter the MCP server URL: `https://mcp.ticktick.com`
    
5.  Save the configuration and follow the prompts to complete OAuth sign-in and authorization.
    

### [Claude Code](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#claude-code)

1.  Run the following command in your terminal:

    claude mcp add --transport http ticktick https://mcp.ticktick.com/
    

2.  In your Claude Code session, run `/mcp` and follow the prompts to complete the OAuth authorization flow.

### [Cursor](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#cursor)

1.  Open Cursor and go to **Cursor Settings**.
    
2.  In the left sidebar, select **Tools & MCP**, then click **Add Custom MCP**.
    
3.  Edit the `.cursor/mcp.json` file and add the following content:
    

    {
      "mcpServers": {
        "ticktick": {
          "url": "https://mcp.ticktick.com"
        }
      }
    }
    

4.  Save the configuration, then reopen **Tools & MCP**.
    
5.  Find TickTick in the installed MCP services list, click **Connect**, and complete OAuth sign-in and authorization in your browser.
    

### [VS Code](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#vs-code)

1.  Create or edit the `.vscode/mcp.json` file in your workspace and add the following content:

    {
     "servers": {
        "ticktick": {
          "type": "http",
          "url": "https://mcp.ticktick.com"
        }
      }
    }
    

2.  You can also open the Command Palette (Ctrl+Shift+P / Cmd+Shift+P), run **Add Server**, choose **HTTP (HTTP or Server-Sent Events)**, enter the MCP server URL `https://mcp.ticktick.com` and an ID, then choose whether to apply it to the workspace or globally.
    
3.  Save the configuration and follow the prompts to complete OAuth sign-in and authorization in your browser.
    

[Available Tools](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#available-tools)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you make task-related requests in an AI conversation, the AI will automatically call the tools provided by TickTick MCP to complete the operation. These tools act like a set of capabilities that allow the AI to query tasks, create tasks, or update task statuses.

> 💡 In most cases, you do not need to remember these tool names. Just describe what you want in natural language, and the AI will choose the appropriate tool automatically.

The following tools are provided by TickTick MCP:

### [Task Queries](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#task-queries)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904)

### [List Queries](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#list-queries)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904)

### [Task Management](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#task-management)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904)

[How to Use](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#how-to-use)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the connection is complete, you can simply use natural language to make requests in your AI conversation. The AI will automatically call TickTick MCP capabilities based on your instructions to query, create, or update tasks.

Below are some example prompts to help you understand how you can interact with the AI.

### [Task Review and Search](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#task-review-and-search)

For example:

> "What tasks do I have today?"

> "List all my high-priority tasks for this week."

> "What tasks did I complete last week?"

> "What unfinished tasks are left in my exam prep list?"

The AI will return the relevant task information based on your request, making it easier to review your plans or reflect on your progress.

### [Task Creation and Management](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#task-creation-and-management)

For example:

> "Create a task: Finish the presentation deck, today at 3 PM, high priority."

> "Buy some plants today, visit the park this weekend to see flowers, and celebrate my friend's birthday next Tuesday. Add all of these to my Life list."

> "Complete the tasks 'Buy milk' and 'Buy daily essentials' in my Personal list."

> "Move 'Go camping' to my Outdoor Activities list."

The AI will automatically understand the task content, extract the relevant details, and perform the corresponding actions—such as creating tasks, updating task status, or organizing tasks into lists.

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7438129581631995904#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

Can I connect if my client does not support Streamable HTTP?

At the moment, TickTick MCP only supports the Streamable HTTP protocol and does not support SSE. If your client only supports SSE, it cannot connect directly for now.

What if the action does not work as expected?

There may be several reasons:

*   The AI model may have misunderstood your request.
*   The wrong tool may have been selected.
*   The parameters passed to the tool may be incorrect.

You can try the following:

*   Use a more specific description, such as the project name, exact date, or priority.
*   Break a complex request into multiple steps, for example: first ask the AI to find the task, then confirm and perform the action.

Does TickTick MCP support all TickTick features?

Not yet. At present, TickTick MCP mainly supports basic task and project operations. Other modules and advanced features are not supported yet.

Do I need to sign in again every time I restart the AI client?

No. OAuth authorization supports automatic token refresh, so under normal circumstances, you do not need to sign in again. You only need to reauthorize if the token has expired after a long period of inactivity or if you manually revoke access.

Integrate Spark
===============

[Connect TickTick to Spark](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082670095834546176#connect-ticktick-to-spark)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iOS

macOS

**Method 1：**

1.  Open an email and tap More on the toolbar at the bottom - “Add Service”.
    
2.  Select “TickTick” and follow the onscreen instructions to log in.
    

**Method 2：**

1.  Tap the menu icon at the top left.
2.  Open “Settings” - “Services”.
3.  Tap “Add Service” and select “TickTick”.
4.  Follow the onscreen instructions to log in.

> Connected Services don't sync between devices. If you want to use TickTick with Spark on several devices, please add this service separately to each of them.

**Method 1：**

1.  Open an email and click More on the toolbar at the top - “Add Service”.
2.  Select “TickTick” and click “Connect”.
3.  Follow the onscreen instructions to log in.

**Method 2：**

1.  Click “Spark” at the top left of your screen.
2.  Select “Settings”.
3.  Go to the Services tab.
4.  Choose “TickTick” and click “Connect”.
5.  Follow the onscreen instructions to log in.

> Connected Services don't sync between devices. If you want to use TickTick with Spark on several devices, please add this service separately to each of them.

[Turn an email into a task](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082670095834546176#turn-an-email-into-a-task)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iOS

macOS

1.  Open the email needed.
2.  Tap “More” on the toolbar at the bottom and select “TickTick”.
3.  By default, the Subject of the email is offered as a future card’s title. Tap at the title to change it.
4.  Choose export options: Link (creates a secure web link to the whole thread) or Email (exports the email text to your TickTick task).
5.  Set a Due date.
6.  Click “Save” at the top right.

With Spark for Teams, you can streamline your team communication and project management with private chat and email export. All of your [private team discussions](https://support.readdle.com/spark/integrations/ticktick)
 will happen in Spark where you can agree on tasks and then export them to TickTick to track progress on their completion.

1.  Open the email needed.
2.  Click “More” on the toolbar at the top and select “TickTick”.
3.  By default, the Subject of the email is offered as the card’s title. Click on the title to change it.
4.  Choose export options: Link (creates a secure web link to the whole thread) or Email (exports the email text to your TickTick task).
5.  Set a Due date.
6.  Tap Save at the top right.

With Spark for Teams, you can streamline your team communication and project management with private chat and email export. All of your private team discussions will happen in Spark where you can agree on tasks and then export them to TickTick to track progress on their completion.

[Remove a connected service](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082670095834546176#remove-a-connected-service)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iOS

macOS

1.  Tap the menu icon at the top left.
2.  Open “Settings” - “Services” - “TickTick”.
3.  Tap Remove Account.

1.  Click “Spark” at the top left of your screen.
2.  Select “Settings” - “Services”.
3.  Under Connected Services, click “TickTick”.
4.  Select “Log Out” at the bottom right.

Time Zone
=========

TickTick provides a 'Time Zone' feature to assist frequent travelers to cope with time zone changes.

[Turn on Time Zone](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082251620645339136#turn-on-time-zone)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Tap on 'Settings' - 'Date & Time' -turn on the 'Time Zone' switch.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082251620645339136)

Once switched on, you can select "Fixed Time Zone" or " Floating Time" when setting the time for a task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082251620645339136)

Click on "Avatar" - "Settings" - "Date & Time" - to turn on the "Time Zone" switch. Once switched on, you can select "Fixed Time Zone" or "Floating Time" when setting the time for a task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082251620645339136)

[Fixed Time Zone](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082251620645339136#fixed-time-zone)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Selecting 'Fixed Time Zone' means that the time of the task will change depending on the time zone you are in.

*   Example 1:If you are flying from the US to London, then a 9am US time assignment will be displayed as 2pm London time.

When the time of an event is based on a certain time zone (e.g. grabbing a Festival train ticket at 9am US time), then you can use Fixed Time Zone to automatically calculate the corresponding local time, even if you are abroad.

In addition, Fixed Time Zone is not only useful for personal situations abroad, but also for collaboration across time zones:

*   Example 2: A colleague in London informs you of a meeting at 10am London time, all you need to do is add a task: select 'Fixed Time Zone' - select London time - and set the task time to 10am. The task will then automatically calculate to remind you of the meeting at 18:00 BST.

[Floating Time](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082251620645339136#floating-time)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Selecting 'Floating Time' means that the time of the task will remain the same regardless of the time zone you are in.

*   Example: You are used to doing your morning run at 7am every day, simply set the task time to 7am and select 'Floating Time'.

This way, whether you are in Los Angeles for business or Barcelona for pleasure, TickTick will remind you to get up early and exercise at 7am local time.

Suggested Tasks

[Floating Time](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7082251620645339136#floating-time)

Subscribing to TickTick in Third-Party Calendars
================================================

TickTick supports generating "URL links" that allow you to sync TickTick calendar with other calendars such as Google and Outlook.

Login to TickTick on desktop, go to “Avatar > Settings > Integrations & Import”, then find “Others > Subscribe to TickTick.”

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d451247fdb8bdb313663939d6f8668af.png)

Click on "Enable the URL", select the list you want to subscribe to, generate the corresponding URL link, and enter the link in other applications to complete the subscription.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5d446ccb495766f6ab6d2d9a36d07834.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c3c0ffa8d447df161462692606c20f42.png)

URL

URL
===

You can subscribe to third-party application content into TickTick through a URL link, allowing you to view these events and receive reminders in TickTick.

[Adding a Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072#adding-a-calendar)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Go to "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - "Calendar", select "URL", and enter the URL link of the third-party calendar to successfully subscribe.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

Click on your "Avatar" - "Settings" - "Integrations & Import", select "URL", and enter the URL link of the third-party calendar to successfully subscribe.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

[Getting Todoist List Link](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072#getting-todoist-list-link)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Right-click on the project you want to subscribe to, select "Project calendar feed", copy the project link, and paste it into the URL calendar input box in TickTick to successfully subscribe.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

[Getting Google Calendar Link](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072#getting-google-calendar-link)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Right-click on the calendar you want to subscribe to, select "Settings and sharing", find "Get shareable link", copy the link, and paste it into the URL calendar input box in TickTick to successfully subscribe.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

[常见问题](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072#%E5%B8%B8%E8%A7%81%E9%97%AE%E9%A2%98)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How to unsubscribe from a calendar?

Mobile

Web

macOS

Windows

On the edit page of the subscribed calendar, click "Unsubscribe" to unsubscribe from the calendar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

Click on "Settings" - "Integrations and Import", then click on "Edit" next to the calendar you want to unsubscribe from, and click "Unsubscribe".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

Select the calendar you want to unsubscribe from in the "Calendars" sidebar, and click "-" to unsubscribe.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

Click on the profile picture - Settings - Calendar Subscription - click on "Edit" next to the calendar you want to unsubscribe from, and click "Unsubscribe".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209387325833347072)

CalDav

Outlook Calendar
================

If you want to display calendar events from Outlook in TickTick, you can easily do so by subscribing to your Outlook calendar.

[Add Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209436222337318912#add-calendar)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Go to "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - “Calendar”, select Outlook, and grant authorization. Once the authorization is successful, the subscription will be completed.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/30775a2fa9c791a184b2e54f5b28ad73.png)

Click on your avatar - "Settings" - "Integration & Import", select Outlook, and grant authorization. Once the authorization is successful, the subscription will be completed.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/65f533beca7674889b126e61a9bcaa62.png)

[View Calendar Events](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209436222337318912#view-calendar-events)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the subscription is successful, you can view calendar events in the "Subscribed Calendars" section of the sidebar.

iCloud Calendar

Exchange Calendar

Local Calendar
==============

If you want to display calendar events from your current device in TickTick, you can easily do so by subscribing to the local calendar.

[Add Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209482814528421888#add-calendar)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

macOS

In "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - "Local Calendars", toggle the switch to view local calendars in TickTick.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209482814528421888)

Click on your avatar, then select "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - "Local Calendar" . Toggle the switch to enable viewing of local calendars in the calendar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209482814528421888)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209482814528421888)

You can also customize the settings for local calendars to "Show", "Show only in calendar", or "Hide".

> Currently, setting local calendars is only available on Android, iOS, and Mac clients.

[Viewing Calendar Events](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209482814528421888#viewing-calendar-events)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After successfully subscribing, you can view calendar events in the sidebar under "Subscribed Calendars".

Calendar Subscriptions

Google Calendar

iCloud Calendar
===============

When you want to view your iCloud calendar in TickTick, you can easily do so by subscribing to your iCloud calendar.

[Add Calendar](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209479055807086592#add-calendar)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to "Settings" - "Import & Integration" - "Calendar", click on "iCloud", and add your iCloud account.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/3f370a9bebfa68971fa092e533acddde.png)

iCloud requires an app-specific password to connect your account.

[Generate an App-Specific Password](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209479055807086592#generate-an-app-specific-password)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iCloud requires generating an app-specific password to connect your account. Click on the "Generate an App-Specific Password" option and go to the Apple website. Log in with your Apple ID on the page, select to generate an app-specific password. Enter the obtained password into TickTick to complete adding your account.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c25040a880ebd431c1046cb4b012c2ef.png)

[Adding Calendar Events](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7209479055807086592#adding-calendar-events)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After successful subscription, you can view the calendar in TickTick under "Subscribed Calendars". Click on the "+" icon to add events. Once added successfully, they will also sync to your iCloud calendar.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/98e4d97470d0f565a68f93cc5aeb2b20.png)

Google Calendar

Outlook Calendar

Select Different Views
======================

TickTick provides three views for viewing tasks: List View, Kanban View, and Timeline View. You can choose the view that suits your needs.

To view all tasks in the list, use the List View 👉 [List View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

For presenting complex project assignments in a simple way and keeping track of every task, use the Kanban View 👉 [Kanban View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

For setting detailed plans for long-term tasks "from month to day," the Timeline View is a must-see 👉 [Timeline View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976)

Time Zone

List View

How to Manage Numerous Tasks
============================

TickTick offers a powerful way to manage tasks with 5 different levels, including "Folder" - "List" - "Section" - "Task" - "Subtask", which can help you manage a large number of tasks efficiently.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782309420597248)

*   [Folder](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782296019795968)
    : Folders are often used to manage lists. If you have a large number of similar lists, such as meetings, reports, and business trips, you can create a "Work" folder to organize them.
    
*   [List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608)
    : Lists can be used to categorize and organize tasks. You can create common lists based on your personal life and work schedule and put similar tasks in the same list. In addition, lists can be shared with others for collaboration.
    
*   [Section](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)
    : A small category within each project, such as "Department Meeting" or "Project Meeting."
    
*   [Task](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782436621254656)
    : The basic level of schedule management.
    
*   [Subtask](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)
    : A level lower than a task. Tasks can be divided into several subtasks to be completed one by one.
    

In addition, we also provide "Tags" and "Filters" to help you better manage your tasks.

Timeline View: A Game-Changer for Project Management

Manage Tasks with Folders

Did the content help you?

Payment and Upgrades
====================

How do I cancel my TickTick Premium?

To cancel your TickTick Premium subscription and stop it from auto-renewing, please follow the instructions based on the payment platform you used.

*   **Google Play & Stripe & PayPal**

If you subscribed via Google Play, Stripe, or PayPal, you can cancel your subscription on the **TickTick web app**:

1.  Click the **personal profile** at the top left and select **Settings**.
2.  Click on the **Premium Account** tab.
3.  Click the **Cancel Subscription** button and confirm by clicking **Yes, cancel**.
4.  Make sure you see the confirmation window indicating your subscription has been cancelled. If not, please repeat the steps.

Alternatively, you can cancel the subscription directly on the respective platform:

1.  Google Play: Visit your Google Play Store account and check if the TickTick subscription is set to auto-renew. If so, manually disable it to avoid future charges.
    
2.  PayPal: Log in to your PayPal account and manage your subscriptions here: [https://www.paypal.com/c2/cgi-bin/webscr?cmd=\_manage-paylist](https://www.paypal.com/c2/cgi-bin/webscr?cmd=_manage-paylist)
    

*   **Apple**

We can not cancel your App Store subscription due to Apple Restrictions. App Store subscriptions auto-renew by default, so it is suggested to cancel them manually. You can view your Apple ID in iTunes or the App Store and then select the “Subscriptions” option.

Why am I still being charged when I have cancelled my subscription?

You will need to check first if you have successfully cancelled your subscription in the unsubscribe method.

If you still have questions, please contact us under 'Help & Feedback'.

How do I request a refund?

**On Android / Web / Windows:** If you purchased TickTick premium subscription via Google Play, PayPal or Stripe, a refund is available within 14 days of payment. The refund cannot be issued if it is beyond 14 days. Please follow these specific steps:

Desktop:

1.  Click the **personal profile** at the top left and select **Settings**.
2.  Click on the **Premium Account** tab.
3.  Click the **Order History** to view orders that are valid for a refund and to submit your refund request. Once submitted, we will process your refund within 3 business days. You can check the status on the order history page or in the email you provided.

Mobile:

1.  Tap on **Settings** then select **your avatar**.
2.  Tap on **Premium Account** below your nickname.
3.  Scroll to the bottom of the page and tap on **Order History** to view orders that are valid for a refund and to submit your refund request. Once submitted, we will process your refund within 3 business days. You can check the status on the order history page or in the email you provided.

**On iOS / macOS:** If you purchased TickTick premium subscription via the App Store, please contact [Apple support](https://reportaproblem.apple.com/)
 to request a refund directly. Due to Apple limits, developers are not allowed to process a refund for payments on the App Store. For more information, please refer to [Request a refund for apps or content that you bought from Apple.](https://support.apple.com/en-us/HT204084)

**Note: Make sure you've cancelled the subscription from the platform where you purchased TickTick premium to ensure you will not be charged again.**

> Orders with invoices cannot be refunded.

How to issue an invoice？

Need an invoice for your TickTick Premium purchase? No problem!

*   **PayPal & Stripe**

If you subscribed to a TickTick Premium via PayPal or Stripe, please follow these specific steps:

Desktop:

1.  Click the **personal profile** at the top left and select **Settings**.
2.  Click on the **Premium Account** tab.
3.  Click the **Order History** to view all order records.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781420970541056)

4.  Update and confirm your billing information first in the **Billing Info** section before invoicing.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781420970541056)

5.  Find the exact invoice you require, and click **invoice**.
6.  **Download** or **print** the invoice PDF.

Mobile:

1.  Tap on **Settings** then select **your avatar**.
2.  Tap on **Premium Account** below your nickname.
3.  Scroll to the bottom of the page and tap on **Order History** to view all order records.
4.  Update and confirm your billing information first in the **Billing Info** section before invoicing.
5.  Find the exact invoice you require, and tap on **invoice**.
6.  The invoice PDF will download automatically.

*   **App Store & Google Play**

If you subscribed to a TickTick Premium via Google Play or App Store, please follow the instructions below to get an invoice.

[https://support.apple.com/en-us/HT204088](https://support.apple.com/en-us/HT204088)
 (App Store)

[https://support.google.com/store/answer/6160235](https://support.google.com/store/answer/6160235)
 (Google)

> Refunded orders do not support invoice issuance.

Will data be lost after the Premium Account expires?

We attach great importance to protecting your data security. After the Premium Account expires, your data will be fully retained. You can still use TickTick like a free account, but you cannot continue to enjoy the privileges corresponding to the Premium Account.

How do I buy and use a TickTick Gift Card?

**1\. Purchase channels**

Go to [TickTick](https://ticktick.com/home)
 and find the gift card at the bottom of the page and click on it to purchase.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055781420970541056)

**2\. What form will the gift card be sent to the recipient?**

The gift card will be sent to the recipient by email. Please ensure that you fill in the correct information for the recipient.

**3\. How do I redeem a Gift Card for a membership?**

The redemption code in the gift card email can be used to redeem a premium membership. You can redeem by:

*   In the mail: copy the redemption code - click on "Redeem in TickTick" - "Redeem" page - enter the redemption code;
*   Android: go to the 'Settings' page - 'Upgrade to Premium Account' - 'Redeem' at the bottom of the page - enter the redemption code;
*   Web: Click on "Personal Avatar" - "Settings" - "Redemption" - enter the redemption code. After successful redemption, the membership benefits will take effect immediately.

**4\. What should I do if the recipient does not receive the gift card in the mail?**

This situation may be caused by the email service provider blocking or filtering specific emails. You can check with the recipient to see if the gift card email has been filtered into "spam". If the recipient is still unable to find the gift card email through the above means, you can choose to resend a new copy.

Here are the steps to do this:

*   Go to the Gift Card purchase page - Click on the Purchase History page - Find the corresponding purchase history - Click on View to go to the purchase details;
*   Click on 'Resend' on the details page - change and confirm the recipient information again - resend.
*   After resending, a new gift card with the same redemption code will be emailed to the recipient. The redemption period for the gift card will remain 1 year from the date of purchase, not 1 year from the date of resending.

> If you do not see the "resend" portal, the gift card has already been redeemed by the recipient.

**5\. Can I request a refund for a gift card?**

Refunds are not available for gift cards. Please confirm the quantity and recipient information at the time of purchase.

Is there an Educational Offer for TickTick?

We have always believed that education can make a difference to individuals and to the world for good, and we want to help more students and staff manage their studies and lives, meet challenges and reach their goals.

To this end, we are offering a special Education Offer: current students and staff can get 25% off the TickTick Premium membership.

*   For step-by-step instructions and details, please click [Education offer](https://ticktick.com/education)
    .

Sign Up and Log In

TickTick Education Offer Application

Did the content help you?

Delete Account
==============

[What does deleting my account mean?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7136181511681736704#what-does-deleting-my-account-mean%3F)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Deleting your account means the cessation of our provision of products or services to you.

After the deletion, your personal information will be stored in our backup archives for 90 days after the account is deleted. For subscriptions and transaction records, we retain this information even after the account is deleted.

[How do I delete my account?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7136181511681736704#how-do-i-delete-my-account%3F)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you no longer wish to use TickTick and want to delete all your data records, you can delete your account.

Mobile

Desktop

Enter "Settings", tap "Avatar" - "Nickname" to enter the account information page, tap "Delete Account", and complete the operation guide to delete the account.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7136181511681736704)

Click on your Avatar - "Settings" - "Account" - "Manage Account" - "Delete Account" and complete the operation guide to delete your account.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7136181511681736704)

If you have multiple TickTick accounts and only want to keep one while merging data, you can first back up the data of the account you wish to cancel. Afterward, import the backed-up data into the account you intend to retain.

Data Backup and Import

Manage Tasks with Group & Sort
==============================

When there are more and more tasks in a list, managing them becomes a troublesome thing. Now, we can freely choose "Group" and "Sort" to manage tasks more easily.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

[What is grouping? What is sorting?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280#what-is-grouping%3F-what-is-sorting%3F)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Grouping can divide the tasks in the list into several categories, and sorting can sort the tasks in each category differently.

For example:

*   Want to find out important tasks in the near future? You can choose to group by time and sort by priority.
*   Want to see what's next in different groups? You can choose to group by custom and then sort by time.

[How to use Sections?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280#how-to-use-sections%3F)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Section allows for more detailed task categorization. For example, create a "Reading" list, and add "Novels", "History", "Workplace", etc. to differentiate book types.

Mobile

Desktop

To access the task list page, click the "..." in the upper right corner, then click "Manage Section" and "Add Section".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

Open a regular list, click ... in the top-right of the detail area → Add Section.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

In addition to custom sections, we also offer several smart sections:

*   List Section: When viewing smart lists or folders, you'll see an option to section by list. Selecting this option will section tasks by the list they belong to.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

*   Time Section: Selecting this option will section tasks by Today, Tomorrow, Next 7 days, Later, and Overdue.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

*   Priority Section: Selecting this option will section tasks by High priority, Medium priority, Low priority, and No priority.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

*   Tag Section: Selecting this option will section tasks by the tags you've added.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

*   Assignee Section: When sharing a list, you'll see an option to section by assignee. Selecting this option will section tasks by the person they're assigned to.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

Why can't I find the Manage Section feature?

Only regular lists support section management, and smart lists do not currently support it.

[How to use Group & Sort？](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280#how-to-use-group-%26-sort%EF%BC%9F)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Open the list and click the "..." in the upper right corner to select "Group & Sort" for settings.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

Open a list, then click the Sort button in the top-right corner to customize how tasks are grouped and sorted.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

If you want to view the deadlines of all tasks across lists in a folder or a Smart List, simply choose **Group by List** and **Sort by Date**.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

Or if you want to check the completion progress of each task in a target list, you can choose **group by Custom and sort by Priority**, so the tasks in the group will be sorted by high, medium, and low priority.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

If you use a shared list, you can also select **group by Assignee and sort by Date** to quickly view tasks assigned to you.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

[Kanban view supports Group & Sort](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280#kanban-view-supports-group-%26-sort)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to custom grouping, you can also directly select the corresponding grouping to achieve different grouped Kanban views.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

In daily work, selecting group by time can display your tasks for today, tomorrow, and the next 7 days in a Kanban view, making it easy for you to quickly check recent important tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

How to restore the default date sorting?

Mobile

Desktop

Click the button on the sorting page to restore the default order.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

Click "Restore default date order" on the sorting page to restore it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7056594711640801280)

![](data:image/svg+xml,%3csvg%20xmlns=%27http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%27%20version=%271.1%27%20width=%27210%27%20height=%2719%27/%3e)![](https://help.ticktick.com/res/article/sidebar-brand-tick.png?w=640&q=75)

Two-Step Verification
=====================

TickTick supports Two-Step Verification, adding an extra layer of security to your account by requiring additional verification during login.

[Turn on Two-Step Verification](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7307588296744370176#turn-on-two-step-verification)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Web

Go to **Settings > Profile > Account Info** to enable **2-Step Verification**.

Tap to enable Two-Step Verification, complete the identity verification, and add your preferred method."

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/037715f94a24cf146d1ae3d1dc0eb3cf.png)

> Note that older app versions no longer support login. Please update to iOS V7.4.50, Android V7.4.5.0, Windows V6.1.30, macOS V6.1.20, Linux V6.0.20, or later versions.

You can choose **Email Verification Code** or **Authenticator App** for verification.Enter the code and tap 'Add' to complete the setup.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/ae77ed96dee4a44def9a4ec83ade1a2d.png)

Go to your profile, then navigate to **Settings > Account to enable Two-Step Verification.**

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/498d11e5d6eb047104ef9e34fba853b4.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/44359c02f5e4354232278456110c8dcc.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/59a5c9cfcaedd0486ec6fed55c5ecd03.png)

You can choose **Email Verification Code** or **Authenticator App** for verification. Enter the code and click Add to complete the setup.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/7407520d1499dc7a6cfae3d828e0a6dc.png)

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5b40929bc27f63796e137d632f1e6fe0.png)

How to Verify Using an Authenticator?

1.  Install an authenticator app on your mobile device (e.g., Google Authenticator or Microsoft Authenticator).
2.  Open the app and scan the QR code or enter the provided code to link your account.
3.  Enter the verification code displayed in the app to complete the verification.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/db802785bdca706c6e1be8e531b13858.png)

### [Email Verification](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7307588296744370176#email-verification)

1.  Select "Email Verification."
2.  Enter your email address and send the verification code.
3.  Enter the 6-digit code to complete the verification.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/d89ce7bdecaa3736f470906eccd87d3b.png)

### [Authenticator App](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7307588296744370176#authenticator-app)

1.  Install an authenticator app on your mobile device (e.g., Google Authenticator or Microsoft Authenticator).
2.  Open the app and scan the QR code or enter the provided code to link your account.
3.  Enter the verification code displayed in the app to complete the verification.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/85d5f892e2bc1acf3fcc542b351056a7.png)

### [Backup Code](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7307588296744370176#backup-code)

Make sure to download and save your **Backup Code**. If you are unable to log in using other verification methods, you can use a backup code for quick access.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/5268ad50123b595bab092343eecd16df.png)

[Using Two-Step Verification](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7307588296744370176#using-two-step-verification)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once Two-Step Verification is enabled, you will be required to verify your identity when performing the following actions:

*   Logging into your account
*   Linking an account
*   Changing linked account information
*   Deleting your account

[Turn off Two-Step Verification](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7307588296744370176#turn-off-two-step-verification)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Web

Go to **Account Info > Two-Step Verification**, Tap **Disable Two-Step Verification**, confirm by selecting **Disable**, and complete the verification to turn it off.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/633ec9ff8caafd5b935f3b3e806f1e5c.png)

Go to **Profile > Settings > Account > Two-Step Verification**, select **Disable** , and complete the verification to disable it.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/03760bbf73e49a2267e4f28a153f0f4d.png)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7307588296744370176#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

How can I enable Two-Step Verification on Mac?

Currently, the Mac version does not support enabling Two-Step Verification directly. Please enable it via the Web version first.

How can I enable Two-Step Verification on PC?

Currently, the PC version does not support enabling Two-Step Verification directly. Please enable it via the Web version first.

Can’t receive the two-step verification code and can’t log in?

If you’re unable to receive the two-step verification code on your phone and don’t have any backup codes to log in, please send an **email to [support@ticktick.com](mailto:support@ticktick.com)
 using the email address linked to your TickTick account.**

Our support team will verify your information and assist you accordingly. To ensure the security of your account, we need to confirm that you are the legitimate account owner.

Please include the following information in your email:

*   Whether you have ever subscribed to **TickTick Premium**
*   If yes, please attach your **payment receipt** (for example, from **App Store, Google Play**, or **Stripe**) If your account is **not linked to an email**, please provide as much information as possible, such as:
*   Registered phone number
*   Account nickname or username
*   The device you last successfully logged in from
*   Premium payment proof (if applicable)

Once we verify your identity, we’ll help you recover access to your account or reset your verification method.

> ⚠️ To ensure your account’s security, please make sure the information you provide is accurate and verifiable. Otherwise, we may be unable to process your request.

Delete Account

[🔜 Shortcuts](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7270720248427315200)

List View
=========

### [List View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176#list-view)

The List View presents tasks in a vertical list format, allowing you to quickly browse through the to-do items in the list by scrolling up and down.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

### [Group & Sort](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176#group-%26-sort)

Currently, on the task list page, TickTick provides you with multiple sorting methods, so you can choose different sorting methods according to your own needs.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

### [Drag and Drop Sorting](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176#drag-and-drop-sorting)

You can also manually drag and drop tasks to make the sorting more flexible.

Hold the task and freely choose where to place it. Multiple operations, done with just one "finger".

Mobile

Desktop

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

[Drag to Create Subtasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176#drag-to-create-subtasks)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to supporting drag and drop to adjust task order, TickTick also allows you to use drag and drop to convert "tasks" ➡️ "subtasks".

Long press a task and drag it to the bottom right of another task to convert it to a subtask.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

[Pin](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176#pin)

------------------------------------------------------------------

TickTick also provides a thoughtful "Pin" function, where you can "Pin" important information to always display at the top of the list, so you can easily keep track of it.

Tap the “…” button in the upper-right corner of the task details page, or long-press a task, then select Pin.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

[Swipe Actions](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176#swipe-actions)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the task list page, you can quickly operate a single task by swiping it.

Swipe the task to the left to see three options appear on the right side of the task. They respectively represent "Move Task", "Delete Task", and "Modify Date". Click on the corresponding option as needed to operate.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

Swipe to the right for "Done" and "Pin" respectively.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

You can also customize the swipe actions in "Settings" - "General" - "Swipe Actions" according to your own preferences to set a more convenient swiping method.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

[Batch Editing Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176#batch-editing-tasks)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iOS

Android

Desktop

On the task list page, click the "..." icon in the upper right corner - "Select" - select multiple tasks, and then select the options below to edit the task as needed: edit the new date, edit the new list, delete, and even prioritize, share, and merge tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

Android users need to long press a task to switch to the batch selection interface, then select multiple tasks, and in the options in the lower right corner, they can edit the task's new date, edit its new list, delete it, and even perform operations such as setting priority, sharing, and merging tasks as needed.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

On the desktop, hold down Shift and select multiple tasks, or select the first and last tasks to perform batch operations.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782365863346176)

Timeline View: A Game-Changer for Project Management
====================================================

"Timeline view" is a lighter and more practical tool than Gantt chart. When you turn on "Timeline view" in the list, tasks will be displayed on a horizontal timeline.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976)

To select the timeline view, go to the view option in the three dots menu in the upper right corner of the list.

> Smart lists such as "Today", "Tomorrow", and "Next 7 Days" do not currently support Timeline View.

With "Timeline view", you can check the progress of each person's work in project management and adjust work plans in a timely manner.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976)

You can also plan and arrange work and life over a longer period of time.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976)

[Easily Create and Schedule Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#easily-create-and-schedule-tasks)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Add Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#add-tasks)

In the timeline view, adding tasks is very simple. You can click on a blank area to directly add a task. The task will automatically be given a time based on the date you clicked on. For example, a task added on April 2nd will automatically be set for April 2nd.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976)

### [Schedule Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#schedule-tasks)

Just like in the "Calendar View," the "Timeline View" can only display tasks with set times. Tasks without set times will be displayed in the "Schedule Tasks" section on the right. You can directly drag and drop tasks into the timeline and set their time.

[Efficient Task Viewing](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#efficient-task-viewing)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Scroll to View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#scroll-to-view)

You can view tasks for a week or a month in the timeline. Simply hold down the mouse to scroll and view.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976)

This horizontal and continuous task presentation is actually more in line with our daily reality. Compared to the calendar, in scenarios where tasks span across weeks and months, viewing and scheduling tasks in the timeline view will also provide a better user experience.

### [Switch Display Ratio](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#switch-display-ratio)

When the task time span is large, you can also adjust the display ratio by switching between day, week, and month.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976)

The significance of the display ratio switch is not only about "seeing more tasks within one screen," but also providing a " bird's-eye view." It helps us re-examine our time management within a broader time frame. Have we spent too much time on trivial matters but invested too little on important goals?

This is also the time management concept that we advocate, which is to focus on the present while also looking ahead.

[Responding to Changes More Confidently](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#responding-to-changes-more-confidently)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After making a plan, many people have probably encountered the situation of "the plan cannot keep up with changes":

*   The work that was originally estimated to take 2 days cannot be completed within the given time frame.
*   The insertion of new tasks at the last minute necessitates the adjustment of previously arranged task times.

As a result, some people think that making plans is useless: since plans will always change, they might as well not make them.

However, in reality, developing plans and adjusting them in a timely manner not only allows us to visualize our progress but is also a way to take the "first step" in psychology, combating procrastination and anxiety.

Therefore, the problem we face is not "whether to make plans" but "how to respond calmly and adjust quickly when plans change."

### [Drag to Modify Duration](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#drag-to-modify-duration)

In the timeline view, the length of a task represents its duration. If you want to adjust the duration of a task, simply move your mouse to the edge of the task and drag it. It only takes two steps to complete the adjustment.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976)

Previously, we had to complete several steps, including "select task → click time setting → select end time → select date → save" to modify the time.

### [Adjusting Time by Dragging](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#adjusting-time-by-dragging)

The position of a task represents its start and end times. When you need to adjust the task time, simply hold the task with your mouse and drag it to the corresponding position.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976)

After dragging, the start and end times of the task will be adjusted according to your release position, even to the corresponding time, which is very convenient.

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782331050622976#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

How to switch between List/Kanban/Timeline views?

To switch between the List, Kanban, and Timeline views, go to the list page and click on the "..." button in the upper right corner, then select "View".

How to display all recurring cycles in the Timeline view?

Currently, it is not supported to display all recurring cycles of a task in the Timeline view.

How to display task colors in the Timeline view?

Similar to the Calendar view, you can display task colors based on list, tag, and priority in the "View Options".

Does the mobile app support the Timeline view?

The Timeline view is now available on the mobile app. Please update to version V6.4 or above to use it.

Kanban View: Categorize and Manage Tasks
========================================

Kanban is a visual task management tool that allows you to gain more dimensions for task breakdown, intuitive information display, and concrete progress monitoring.

With Kanban, you can easily group and manage your tasks anywhere and anytime, whether it's for personal growth, project breakdown, information display, process tracking, or team collaboration.

*   Personal Growth (annual planning, career advancement, skill learning...)
*   Team Collaboration (recruitment management, office procurement, sales processes, marketing operations...)

💡 Want to go deeper? Check out our article: [What is Kanban? Learn Kanban and its Benefits](https://ticktick.com/resources/article/7309872500207255552/kanban-kanbanboard)

[Switching to Kanban View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#switching-to-kanban-view)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Kanban view is not a separate feature module; it is a display mode of your lists. Unlike other views, the Kanban view provides a clearer view of the items in each of your groups.

> Currently, you can switch to Kanban view within Smart Lists, Folders, and Tags.

How to Switch to Kanban View?

Mobile

Desktop

Go to the task list page of each list, tap the "..." icon in the top right corner, and select "View." Then choose "Kanban View."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

On the task list page of each list, click the "..." icon in the top right corner, select "Kanban View."

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

[Use Kanban View](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#use-kanban-view)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Manage Personal Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#manage-personal-tasks)

By selecting the Kanban view in the "Next 7 Days", you can quickly see what tasks you need to complete each day in the next seven days. This helps you have a clear understanding of how many tasks you have, what they are, and their completion status.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

You can also choose the sorting option of Date + Priority, which allows you to see clearly which tasks have higher priority each day.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

In the "Today" sorting option, selecting List + Date enables you to focus on arranging and tracking tasks in different categories throughout the day. During work hours, you can focus on the work list, and after work, you can pay attention to other lists.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

💡 If there are changes to your plans, you can simply drag and drop tasks to other columns, allowing you to adjust tasks flexibly.

### [Team Project Management](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#team-project-management)

You can also use the Kanban view to manage tasks for a specific phase or project. By using the Kanban view, we can have a clear understanding of the tasks that need to be completed in each stage.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

By selecting Assignee + Date in the sorting options, you can more clearly track the completion status of tasks assigned to different team members.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

[Creating Personal Kanban](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#creating-personal-kanban)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [Personal Kanban](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#personal-kanban)

You can create Kanban boards based on different time periods to visualize the tasks you need to execute.

> You can choose a yearly cycle or select shorter periods, such as a quarter, a month, a week, and so on.

For example, Annual plan:

*   Column 1: "Want-to-do" - Any ideas or things you need to do within this year can be written here.
*   Column 2: "Prepare-to-do" - Select a few ideas from the first column and place them here. It is recommended to keep it to three items or fewer.
*   Column 3: "Doing" - This column contains the tasks you are currently focusing on.
*   Column 4: "Done" - Once a task is finished, you can move it to this column.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/c4e798bea7bc5628a8b736087befe336.png)

Of course, you can also create different categories of sections based on your needs:

*   By theme: Work, Life, Entertainment...
*   By progress: Not Started, In Progress, Completed...

### [Editing sections](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#editing-sections)

Mobile

Desktop

In any list, tap the "..." icon in the top right corner, and select "Manage Section" to rename, create, and delete sections.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

Click the "..." icon in the top right corner of the "Section". You can rename, create, and delete sections from there.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

### [Drag and Sort](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#drag-and-sort)

Whether on desktop or mobile, you can freely drag and drop both sections and tasks to their desired positions.

💡On the mobile app, you can switch to the Sections tab by tapping on the top tab bar.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

### [Add Tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#add-tasks)

Mobile

Desktop

In the Section page, tap the "+" icon to add tasks to the corresponding section.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

Click the "+" icon in the top right corner of the "Section" to add tasks to a specific section.

![](https://pull.ticktick.app/hc/all/cedd1a6f3c6c20e4ebb991b724b139d8.png)

[Create Team Kanban](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#create-team-kanban)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TickTick's "Kanban View" can effectively help teams in the following ways:

*   Maintain team focus: Clear goals are marked on the Kanban board, allowing the team to concentrate and achieve them.
*   Increase work transparency: Team members can see the entire workflow, ensuring project direction and clear accountability.
*   Improve productivity: Task organizers can easily organize tasks and schedule them on the Kanban board.

You can freely create Kanban boards (sections) based on your team's situation and assign tasks to team members.

Flexible section sorting through drag and drop allows you to easily adapt to any changes in team work.

### [Assign Responsible Members](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#assign-responsible-members)

Once tasks are created, you can assign them by using the "Assign" feature, and team members will receive task assignment notifications.

*   Right-click on a task in the Kanban view and select "Assign to" to assign it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

### [Eliminate the Information Gap](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#eliminate-the-information-gap)

While conventional Kanban views are a passive way to display project progress, TickTick allows you and your team members to communicate through task comments, effectively addressing any information gaps among members.

*   When there is progress in a task, you can post updates in the comments section.
    
*   Click on a task, click on "Comments" in the popup window, and write your comment in the input box.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

Additionally, TickTick automatically generates "Task Activities" for each task created or edited, so you can view all the changes that have occurred during the task's progress at any time.

*   Click on a task, click on the "..." icon in the bottom right corner of the popup window, and select "Task Activities".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

[FAQ](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168#faq)

------------------------------------------------------------------

Does the Kanban view support width adjustment?

The desktop Kanban view supports width adjustment, and there are three sizes for you to choose: small, medium and large. Click "..." in the upper right corner of Kanban view, then go to "Display Settings" to adjust the width.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782353376903168)

Why can't I "Editing Sections"?

You need to change "Group" to "Customize" in "Sort" at the top right corner of the list before you can manage groups.

Manage Tasks with Folders
=========================

As the number of lists increases, you can use folders to organize your lists. For example, you can create a "Life" folder and put lists such as "Daily Life", "Shopping", and "Exercise" in it.

[Creating Folders](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782296019795968#creating-folders)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Option 1: Drag a list onto another list and release it. In the pop-up window, enter the name to create a folder.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782296019795968)

*   Option 2: Click "List Editing Page" - "Folder" - "Add Folder", enter the folder name, and click " Done" to create it successfully.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782296019795968)

[Ungrouping Folders](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782296019795968#ungrouping-folders)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On mobile devices, you can ungroup a folder by swiping left or holding it down. On desktop devices, you can ungroup a folder by right-clicking on it.

Manage Tasks with Lists
=======================

"List" is a commonly used way to organize tasks. Developing a "list mentality" can not only help us focus on important things, but also improve productivity and execution.

The key to list thinking is to be goal-oriented. You can create lists based on your goals, such as work, study, exercise, reading, etc., to improve your sense of control over life.

Currently, TickTick supports two types of lists: "Smart List" and "Regular List".

[Smart List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608#smart-list)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### [What is a Smart List?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608#what-is-a-smart-list%3F)

The "Smart List" feature helps you quickly identify what you need to do today and tomorrow. A smart list is a "list that filters and displays tasks based on certain conditions".

We have prepared five most efficient smart lists: "Today", "Tomorrow", "Next 7 Days", "Inbox", and "Assigned to Me".

*   In the "Today", "Tomorrow", and "Next 7 Days" smart lists, tasks with due dates of today, tomorrow, and the next 7 days will be displayed.
*   "Inbox" is a temporary task transfer station where all tasks that cannot be sorted temporarily can be placed. (Inbox cannot be hidden or deleted.)
*   "Assigned to Me" is a collection of tasks assigned to you from different shared lists. You can view your tasks in different shared lists in this list.

### [How to enable Smart Lists?](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608#how-to-enable-smart-lists%3F)

Mobile

Desktop

Click on the "Settings" icon to the right of "Add List" in the sidebar to open the "Smart List Management" page and set the smart lists you want to display.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608)

Click your avatar → Settings → Smart Lists to enable the ones you want.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608)

> We offer three display options: "Show", "Hide", and "Show if not empty", which you can set according to your actual needs.

[Regular Lists](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608#regular-lists)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to the smart lists we provide, you can also create your own lists. You can create different lists such as "Work", "Personal", and "Life" to categorize your tasks.

### [Creating a New List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608#creating-a-new-list)

Mobile

Desktop

Click on "Add" - "List" at the bottom of the sidebar to create a new list.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608)

Hover over Lists and click the + button on the right to create a new list.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608)

You can set the "name", "color", "folder", and "display/hide" of a list.

How to use Emoji as a list icon?

Different colored and styled Emojis can help customize your list in a more intuitive and personalized way. It can also make finding a specific list faster.

*   Option 1: On the list editing page, click the "icon" in front of the name, select the desired Emoji, and click "done" to create it successfully.
*   Option 2: Enter an Emoji at the beginning of the list name, and it will be automatically set as the list icon.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608)

### [Edit List](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608#edit-list)

Swipe a list in the sidebar to the left, and three options will appear: "Pin", "Edit", and "Delete". Click on the middle "Edit" icon to enter the list editing page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608)

[List Background](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608#list-background)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When switching between different lists, do you wish to easily tell apart your work, life, and personal lists? By setting different backgrounds, you can give each list its own unique visual identity.

Open the list you want to customize, tap the upper-right **…** → **Background** to set its background.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608)

You can choose from the following background styles:

*   **Follow App Theme**: Keep a simple and consistent interface.
    
*   **Color Background**: A solid color brings a cleaner visual style.
    
*   **Gradient Background**: Soft gradients create a richer visual experience.
    
*   **Image Background**: Choose an image to make your list more personalized.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782283059396608)

Do all lists support background customization?

Not all lists support this feature. The following lists currently do not support background customization: **Completed, Won't Do, and Trash**.

Manage Tasks with Folders
