Multilevel Tasks
================

Facing complex projects and don't know where to start? TickTick provides "subtasks" that allow you to add several related subtasks to a task, helping you simplify the overall goal and break it down into several clear and achievable small goals. This can greatly reduce the difficulty of execution.

[Create Subtasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248#create-subtasks)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

Option 1: Go to the task detail page, click on the "..." in the upper right corner, and select "Add Subtask".

You can click the "paper airplane" icon to complete the creation after entering the first subtask, or click the "return" key in the lower left corner of the keyboard to complete the creation of the current subtask, and continue to create the second subtask at the same level.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Option 2: Convert existing tasks into subtasks by dragging and dropping.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Option 3: To quickly create a "subtask" under a task, drag the "+" symbol to a slightly lower right position below the task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

> This function is not available in "Today", "Next 7 Days" and other smart lists, and can only be used in the "Inbox" and regular lists created by oneself.

Each subtask at every level has the same functions as a normal task. That is, subtasks can set time and duration, focus on them, write task details, recover deleted tasks in the "Trash", set tags and priorities, and assign them to others.

Option 4: Enter the subtask details page, click "..." in the upper right corner, and click "Add Subtask" to add subtasks to subtasks again, supporting up to five different levels of tasks.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

In the subtask details, you can click on the main task title above the subtask title to jump to the main task details.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Option 1: Click ... in the bottom-right of the task detail area → Add Subtask.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Option 2: Right-click a task → Add Subtask.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

After entering the first subtask, press Enter to create more subtasks at the same level.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Option 3: Hover over the task you want to convert, then drag the hamburger icon to the bottom-right of the target task to make it a subtask.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

### [Expand Subtasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248#expand-subtasks)

In the task list, you can click on the arrow icon on the right side of the main task to expand or collapse all subtasks under the task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

### [Link Parent Task](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248#link-parent-task)

Mobile

Desktop

Open a task to enter the task details page, click the "..." in the top right corner, and select "Link Parent Task." This way, you can set a task as a subtask of another task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Want to quickly organize multiple tasks under the same parent task? Go to the list details page, click the "..." in the top right corner and select "Select," or long-press a task to multi-select. Then, click the "..." in the bottom right corner and choose "Link to Parent Task" to quickly organize them.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Right-click a task, or click ... in the bottom-right of the task detail area → Link Parent Task. You can set one task as a subtask of another.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Want to quickly organize multiple tasks into the same parent task? Select multiple tasks and click Link Parent Task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

### [Unlink Parent Task](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248#unlink-parent-task)

Mobile

Desktop

Open the task detail page, click ... in the top-right → Link Parent Task, then click the ✖️ next to the linked task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

You can also drag to unlink a parent task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Right-click a task, or click ... in the bottom-right of the task detail area → Link Parent Task, then click the ✖️ next to the linked task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

Or, hover over the linked parent task and click Unlink.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

You can also drag to unlink a parent task.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248)

### [FAQs](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782219767349248#faqs)

Does multi-level task support unlimited splitting?

At present, we only allow up to 5 levels of nested tasks. If the limit is exceeded, you cannot continue to add.

What is the sorting rule for multi-level tasks?

The sorting of the list will not break the hierarchical structure of the tasks, but will only compare and sort tasks within the same level.

Will subtasks be displayed in the calendar view?

Sure, subtasks can also be freely dragged on the timeline.

Will subtasks and check items affect the completion progress of the parent task?

When both check items and subtasks exist or only one of them exists, only the completion of the check items will affect the task progress. After all check items are completed, the parent task will be automatically completed.

Filters - Choose What You Want to See

Set Up Recurring Tasks

# Manage Tasks with Tags

![](data:image/svg+xml,%3csvg%20xmlns=%27http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%27%20version=%271.1%27%20width=%27210%27%20height=%2719%27/%3e)![](https://help.ticktick.com/res/article/sidebar-brand-tick.png?w=640&q=75)

Ctrl K

Manage Tasks with Tags
======================

Adding "tags" to tasks can make task management more efficient. A task can have multiple tags, which are often associated with categories, status, or location.

Mobile

Desktop

*   Before use, confirm whether the "Tags" display has been enabled in the sidebar. Once enabled, tags will be displayed below the "Smart List".

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

If tags are not displayed in the sidebar, click the "Settings" button in the lower right corner of the sidebar to enter the list management page. Click "Tags" and select "Show" to enable.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

Before use, make sure Tags are enabled in the sidebar. Once enabled, tags will appear under lists.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

If tags are not visible, click your avatar → Settings → Smart Lists, then set Tags to Show.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

[Add tags to tasks](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216#add-tags-to-tasks)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

*   Option 1: When creating a task, click the "tags" icon below the task input field to select an existing tag or create a new one.
    
*   Option 2: Use "#" when creating a task to quickly create a tag.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

*   Option 1: Right-click a task, choose Tags to add an existing tag or create a new one.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

*   Option 2: When creating a task or editing its details, type # to quickly create a new tag or choose from existing tags.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

*   Option 3: Drag a task onto an existing tag to add it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

[Manage Tags](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216#manage-tags)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mobile

Desktop

When you swipe a tag in the sidebar to the left, three options will appear: "Pin", "Edit", and "Delete".

*   Clicking the "Edit" icon will take you to the "Tag Editing" page, where you can modify the tag's color and parent tag. After the operation, all tasks containing that tag will be updated accordingly.
    
*   Clicking the "Delete" icon will remove the tag from the sidebar and tasks, but the tasks will not be deleted.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

You can also click "List and Tag Management" - "Tags" at the bottom of the left sidebar to enter the corresponding tag editing page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

Right-click a tag to view options including Pin, Edit, and Delete. Select Edit to go to the tag editing page.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

### [Create Second-Level Tags](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216#create-second-level-tags)

The tag hierarchy supports creating "second-level tags." Drag a tag from the sidebar to below another tag to select a parent tag for the dragged tag.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

You can also swipe left on a tag, click "Edit," and select a parent tag for it.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

### [Tag Sorting](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216#tag-sorting)

TickTick supports users to customize the sorting of tags. By long-pressing a tag in the sidebar, you can drag and drop it to freely sort the list.

In addition, you can also group tasks by tags in the task list — tap “···” → “Group & Sort” — to quickly get an overview of your schedule.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782255804809216)

Manage Tasks with Group & Sort

Filters - Choose What You Want to See
=====================================

[Filter tasks with Filters](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782240994721792#filter-tasks-with-filters)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

First, create a task list based on your usage scenario, such as setting up a study plan or work tasks for next week. When creating tasks, try to add attributes such as "time", "tags", and "priority" to facilitate multi-dimensional filtering by filters.

### [Add Filter](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782240994721792#add-filter)

Mobile

Desktop

Option 1: Click "List Management" in the lower right corner of the sidebar and select "Add Filter".

Option 2: Click on "Add" - "Filter" at the bottom of the sidebar to create a new Filter.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782240994721792)

Make sure Filters are enabled in the sidebar. Once enabled, filters will appear under lists.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782240994721792)

If not visible, click your avatar → Settings → Smart Lists, then set Filters to Show.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782240994721792)

When setting the filtering conditions for the filter, there are two methods: Normal filtering and Advanced filtering.

### [Normal Filter](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782240994721792#normal-filter)

Filter by list name, tags, date, and other attributes, and you can also filter by content by keyword.

*   For example: By setting conditions, establish a filter for "read today", and then you can quickly find the corresponding task by selecting the filter.

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782240994721792)

### [Advanced Filter](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782240994721792#advanced-filter)

If you want to select multiple properties that are the same, we recommend using advanced filtering.

Advanced filtering allows for multi-statement queries using logical operators such as "OR" and "AND", as well as filtering conditions like lists, dates, priorities, and tags.

*   By setting the filtering conditions to "read today," you can quickly find tasks that meet the criteria through advanced filtering.
    
*   If you're unsure if your filtering conditions are reasonable, you can also click "Preview" to see the display effect, making it easier to modify quickly.
    

![](https://help.ticktick.com/articles/7055782240994721792)
